id='poem_sentence_0_1220403'>岳岳惟公，至德内充，择乎中庸，靡介靡通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220403_comment'></div>论议设施，孰复利疚，不为今妍，不袭往陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220403_comment'></div>惟活其心，以观物宜，用能泛应，不久其持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220403_comment'></div>惟下其心，由古于学，圣经沈酣，百氏扬搉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220403_comment'></div>气涵清夷，识洞缅邈，发为文章，丰润伟卓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220403_comment'></div>粤从妙龄，擢秀上第，旋中异科，声绝伦类，不卑小官，以淬以砺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220403_comment'></div>建炎之初，始为御史，造膝所陈，惟理是诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220403_comment'></div>宰相之官，讵以赏功，帝度其言，有嘉其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220403_comment'></div>爰自螭坳，代言西掖，新我王度，讨论润色，执宪中司，纪纲是饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220403_comment'></div>时方艰虞，民情屼岌，公居禁林，独擅手笔，诏令颁传，曲折烦悉，父老扶观，武夫感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220403_comment'></div>扈跸东巡，入赞枢机，海邦单外，忧勤百为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220403_comment'></div>既参大柄，正路爰启，贤哲汇征，号令风靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220403_comment'></div>出临会稽，实分忧顾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220403_comment'></div>易帅于闽，百废具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220403_comment'></div>公之为政，甚鄙钩距，不怒而威，莫予敢侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220403_comment'></div>兵民兴讹，变在漏刻，公独坚卧，已乃情得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220403_comment'></div>有猷入告，不远王室，去而扬之，曰后之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220403_comment'></div>帝曰遄归，予惟汝哲，悌政未孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220403_comment'></div>有若随会，晋盗奔驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220403_comment'></div>重来越绝，载欣载愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220403_comment'></div>我马未前，竹马在途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220403_comment'></div>建业留钥，控临长江，帝曰重臣，匪公谁双。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220403_comment'></div>公至劳民，顾色舒舒，将士钦然，骄矜内锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220403_comment'></div>帝方倚公，势如长城，淹忽讣闻，朝野震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220403_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220403_comment'></div>天不憖遗，丧此哲辅，山颓梁坏，不足以喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220403_comment'></div>公之居家，履行纯庞，孝友雍睦，刑于乡邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220403_comment'></div>公在朝廷，国有蓍龟，民所具瞻，士曰得师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220403_comment'></div>汲引后进，起仆振淹，笃若天性，不见所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220403_comment'></div>我实愚陋，公不鄙夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220403_comment'></div>厥初拜公，于霅之湄，有酒饮我，诗文是追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220403_comment'></div>凡我往来，无从见之，究所以然，公实谓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220403_comment'></div>乖暌会合，三纪于兹，逮公鼎贵，我困莫治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220403_comment'></div>避地飘流，拜公在所，公哀我穷，委曲见语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220403_comment'></div>时方须才，子不可去，他日丐归，或继以怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220403_comment'></div>公意必欲，寘我周行，蓬莱道山，儒士之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220403_comment'></div>滥巾实惭，公未厌斁，或挽或推，不遗馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220403_comment'></div>我独何人，得此殊遇，志穷术疏，报塞无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220403_comment'></div>谓德如公，固当期颐，公不百年，我心孔悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220403_comment'></div>永怆士神，十舍有溢，嗟我老癃，淹淹气息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220403_comment'></div>往拜勿躬，而愧心侧，缄辞遣奠，涕随感出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220403_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220403_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1220403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　居归安。秋，为范桐母朱氏作墓志铭。作品：宋故太孺人朱氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故太孺人朱氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220383")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220383'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220383'>太孺人朱氏，吴兴乌程人，故宣教郎同郡范君贲之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220383_comment'></div>朱，吴兴名族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220383_comment'></div>仕为秘书丞，未老而休官，以经术教授弟子，号乡先生讳临者，太孺人之大父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220383_comment'></div>以文章论议受知裕陵，为中书舍人讳服者，太孺人之世父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220383_comment'></div>太孺人之考讳形，与诸季皆以学问名于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220383_comment'></div>稍不偶，辄弃去，庐于先生墓之傍曰玲珑山，薙草植木，畦田圃桑，以业其家，以乐其身终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220383_comment'></div>太孺人自幼承家范，蹈壸则，惟俭惟勤，米盐靡密，布帛纺绩之类，习闻而熟见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220383_comment'></div>人或闻之能焉，人以是律范氏之家益勤弗懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220383_comment'></div>食不二羹胾，非有宾客外姻不御绮縠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220383_comment'></div>义所当为，惟恐居后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220383_comment'></div>宣教君二妹在室，太孺人始至，斥奁橐与之，为求良配，俾克成家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220383_comment'></div>已而宣教君登进士第，太孺人从之官，勉之奉公，不以家事丝发稍累其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220383_comment'></div>不幸宣教君早世，以其丧归，纲纪内外，小大秩秩，春秋之事无阙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220383_comment'></div>太孺人生一男二女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220383_comment'></div>初，长女议择配未决，太孺人曰：「吾异时尝一见沈秀才，其人当贵，议无以易此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220383_comment'></div>盖先枢密沈公与求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220383_comment'></div>未几，沈公游太学，取巍科，为名进士，旋遇真主，历三院御史、中执法、吏部尚书，遂参大政、知枢密院事，言听谏行，为时名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220383_comment'></div>于是乡党伟太孺人之识，以为奇男子不过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220383_comment'></div>男曰桐，太孺人励之以学，寒暑不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220383_comment'></div>尝曰：「吾自奉薄陋，有良士益友可以辅吾儿者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220383_comment'></div>日击鲜，躬调芼以进，不敢有所惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220383_comment'></div>桐嗜学，不得志于科举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220383_comment'></div>久之，沈氏甥固请以先公遗泽奏封太孺人，并桐补官，任右迪功郎、前监浙西安抚司回易库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220383_comment'></div>幼女适右文林郎严州桐庐县丞王棣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220383_comment'></div>孙男二，曰好德、好问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220383_comment'></div>孙女三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220383_comment'></div>太孺人以绍兴十五年六月十三日卒于正寝，享年七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220383_comment'></div>以其年九月十八日葬于乌程县澄静乡大正坞，祔宣教君之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220383_comment'></div>太孺人性明果，临终不乱，后事皆自处画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220383_comment'></div>桐奉治命惟谨，方当弃时，色忧惧如死灰，昼夜不解带者阅月，余每见而怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220383_comment'></div>既葬，以铭见属，且闵闵焉惧其母之懿不传也，余其忍辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220383_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1220383'>惟妇德，先俭勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220383_comment'></div>自厥初，袭清芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220383_comment'></div>律而家，裕乃身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220383_comment'></div>中岁嫠，茹苦辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220383_comment'></div>久弥励，志克振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220383_comment'></div>尚遗泽，溢后人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1220383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年闰11月16日</a>　居归安。除敷文阁待制指挥勿行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年闰12月17日</a>　居归安。落职依旧宫祠，上谢表。作品：谢落职依旧宫祠表。<div id='poem_1220256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢落职依旧宫祠表<span class='inlineComment2'>（除敷文阁待制，因除免语误。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年闰12月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220256")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220256'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220256'>人微恩重，罪大罚轻，祗服训辞，复增感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220256_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>伏念臣受才谫薄，赋性凡庸，更阅虽多，报称何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220256_comment'></div>矧年龄之颓暮，加疾疚之兢昏，比奏封章，恳辞误宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220256_comment'></div>荷再生之大赐，念几死以难酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220256_comment'></div>昧于叙陈，卒至乖谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220256_comment'></div>魄由天夺，戚乃自贻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220256_comment'></div>尚赖隆宽，特从末减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220256_comment'></div>复俾祠官之秩，仍沾廪稍之优，委曲保全，始终哀悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220256_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下乾坤覆载，父母生成，舜德洽于民心，尧言布于天下，兼容世类，一本至仁，遂令下愚，蒙此蕃贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220256_comment'></div>而臣视残骸之已病，知来日之无多，惟有衔恩，至于结草。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1220256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　春，至乌程卞山拜访叶梦得，有诗。作品：访石林叶少蕴观文二首。<div id='poem_529171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>访石林叶少蕴观文二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529171")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529171'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529171'>卿云覆其上，草木争鲜新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529171'>竹露先参差，晴曦破萧晨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529171'>万石纷拱揖，静默自主宾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529171'>似中有老仙，云霞焕精神。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529171'>朝暮林壑间，搜抉出怪珍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529171'>风攲青箬笠，雨垫乌角巾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529171'>山灵指相谓，个是夔龙身。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529171'>如何轻世累，萧散意许真。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529171'>了知衮衣贵，未若岩石亲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529171'>功名乃弃馀，道德受咨询。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529171'>我来追步趋，且复结胜因。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529171'>剧谈到羲轩，愧此真天人。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529171'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_529171_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529172?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529172'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529172'>夔龙在丘壑，神物发幽秘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529172'>森然万琼瑰，参错分位置。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529172'>踞地猛兽伏，拿空孤鸟厉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529172'>先后相长雄，突怒疑攫噬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529172'>各以奇自列，宁谓我独嗜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529172'>羊酪非不珍，莼羹有至味。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529172'>郑公信骨鲠，我但见妩媚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529172'>种竹被崖峦，恶木不得地。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529172'>荃兰偏九畹，秽草惨无类。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529172'>造化初何心，被物自殊志。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529172'>那知此岩傍，阅世等如寄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529172'>愿言赋丹青，远近同一视。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529172'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_529172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年9月22日</a>　居归安。梦中得诗。作品：和故人二首丁卯年九月二十二日梦中得之。<div id='poem_529304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和故人二首丁卯年九月二十二日梦中得之<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年9月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529304")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529304_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529304'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529304'>平生事业较粗疏，晚岁欣陪谢幼舆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529304'>林下商量好消息，不须嵇子绝交书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529304'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529304_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529305?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年9月22日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529305'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529305'>目前得已便休休，事业何曾有到头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529305'>客问函三<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作山）</span>孰为一，月明风静好清秋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529305'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_529305'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_529305_0'>⑴ 自注：此篇不记第二句，觉后足之。觉时已五鼓，梦中他语，皆谈妙理。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_529305_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年12月1日</a>　居归安。为钱悦《箕裘集》作序。作品：钱氏箕裘集序。<div id='poem_1220340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱氏箕裘集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年12月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220340")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220340'>右钱氏《箕裘集》，武肃王之六世孙名悦字稷臣者之所作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220340_comment'></div>武肃以兵拒巢贼，讨刘汉宏，诛董昌，尽有吴越之地，尊奉上国，四传至忠懿王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220340_comment'></div>武肃躬蹈忠孝，又以训子孙，而忠懿奉承惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220340_comment'></div>方太祖皇帝之下江南也，忠懿提兵取常润，已而来朝京师，太祖慰遣甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220340_comment'></div>太宗登极，卒以国入觐，而吴越之民几二百年不识兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220340_comment'></div>其阴德之茂在人膺肺间，至于今未忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220340_comment'></div>士大夫喜道其事而传闻异辞，或不审谛，故稷臣类其祖宗建立传序次第，以家世荣遇，人才瑰杰有闻于时者若干人，以为此集，将附之家谱，属余序其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220340_comment'></div>余尝观自昔门第之盛，席勋旧姻戚，世公世卿，宠遇赫奕，不为不多，故独以恩泽闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220340_comment'></div>而人才辈出，表仪搢绅如钱氏者，未见其比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220340_comment'></div>岂其世德所钟与他异欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220340_comment'></div>异时位孤棘、秉旄钺者，余盖识其一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220340_comment'></div>即之退然如窭人子，论道古今，考质疑义，以自乐于名教，其意岂肯与恩泽侯比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220340_comment'></div>其有挟册觅举，与寒士较得失，率攻苦食淡，淬励事业，使余爱叹之不已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220340_comment'></div>况前辈硕儒所谓一门三学士，三世四贤良，与其政绩行义，超诣卓越，余之所跂慕，愿见而不及者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220340_comment'></div>以是知人物门第，事不两全，钱氏既兼得之，又何多耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220340_comment'></div>如其不然，虽金张之盛，七叶珥貂，亦无取云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220340_comment'></div>稷臣在宗族中为最不遇者，客居异县，累然坐空卢，读古书，行古道，面有藜苋之色，是余寂寞之友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220340_comment'></div>绍兴十七年十一月辛卯，吴兴刘某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220340_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　居归安。为林仰父作墓志铭。作品：宋故左朝散郎通判安肃军林君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故左朝散郎通判安肃军林君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220387")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220387'>君讳某，字无惑，福州长溪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220387_comment'></div>曾祖仁珙，祖昱，父雄，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220387_comment'></div>父以君通朝籍，累赠承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220387_comment'></div>君自幼童知好学，刻意钻研，砺志寒暑饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220387_comment'></div>久之，自以闻见不伟，慨然出求师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220387_comment'></div>时太守蔡公襄大开学校，延四方豪英，而乡先生陈公烈起处士为学官，士类益集，君往从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220387_comment'></div>先生每日夜闻君诵书，策励群弟子必以君为言，且相器重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220387_comment'></div>元丰初为太学生，十年，声名日彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220387_comment'></div>司业朱公服览其艺文，以为有柳柳州气骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220387_comment'></div>又喜其庄重有常，处以职事，曰：「勉之，为馀子矜式」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220387_comment'></div>累试春官辄不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220387_comment'></div>至元祐六年始登进士第，授温州瑞安尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220387_comment'></div>未赴，相继丁内外艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220387_comment'></div>服除，调临江军司法参军，议法平允，为老吏所服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220387_comment'></div>再调邵武军司户参军，皆兼学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220387_comment'></div>移建州松溪令，政治不烦，悉出恺悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220387_comment'></div>岁旱，飞蝗被旁邑，独不入松溪境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220387_comment'></div>邑人德之，欲以闻部使者，君谢止之，曰：「使我得名，如他邑何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220387_comment'></div>终更，士民遮道，不得去者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220387_comment'></div>寻授泉州晋江丞，再授建州瓯宁令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220387_comment'></div>瓯宁负郭，当道路之冲，民剽悍健讼，最于一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220387_comment'></div>食且朝，造郡守使者，归听民讼，未竟，或当食，放匕箸出，迓客无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220387_comment'></div>君不自以为劳，事益精密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220387_comment'></div>夜秉烛省案牍，不一以诿吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220387_comment'></div>威信并行，盗为出境，囹圄屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220387_comment'></div>使者交荐之，御史中丞吴公执中以君治行闻于朝，不果召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220387_comment'></div>已而用荐改宣教郎、知湖州归安县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220387_comment'></div>君为归安甚暇，且教且治之，民不忍犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220387_comment'></div>岁潦民流，有圣旨赈济，君择地为茇舍区处之，适温凉燥湿之宜，视食饮淹速之节，所全活甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220387_comment'></div>使者上其事，减考功格三年，转奉议郎，再转承议郎、权宗子博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220387_comment'></div>以年高请补外，除通判安肃军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220387_comment'></div>待次京师，闻大将开边，君曰：「此胎祸也，吾不应及其难」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220387_comment'></div>亟买舟还乡，筑室于故园，与亲旧宾客举酒相乐，论者高之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220387_comment'></div>转朝奉郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220387_comment'></div>遇渊圣皇帝登极恩，迁朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220387_comment'></div>以某年某月某甲子终于新居，享年七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220387_comment'></div>以某年某月某甲子葬于长松比明宗佛寺之旁，盖君所自卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220387_comment'></div>娶同邑周氏，有贤行，先君十五年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220387_comment'></div>男二人，曰声、曰仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220387_comment'></div>三女，长适右迪功郎王旁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220387_comment'></div>次未嫁，与子声皆早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220387_comment'></div>幼适乡贡进士周直亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220387_comment'></div>孙一人，曰同仰，今为右修职郎、袁州宜春县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220387_comment'></div>君孝于亲，义于乡党，天姿粹然，金玉人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220387_comment'></div>钩贯经术，善属文，于词赋诗章尤工，后辈从君学者，皆有轨则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220387_comment'></div>有文集若干卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220387_comment'></div>其待人一本于诚，所治三邑，去皆见思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220387_comment'></div>尝语仰曰：「吾居官无以踰人，独小大之狱必以情，有不安者，蚤暮以思，未尝敢忘于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220387_comment'></div>吾老尚何求，以是遗汝耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220387_comment'></div>在归安时，余以邑子见君，君相遇甚厚，因获与仰游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220387_comment'></div>仰访余于里间，民吏惊曰：「是长官儿耶，我辈不之识也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220387_comment'></div>盖始出而从吾游，其审慎而畏谨每若此，使余心愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220387_comment'></div>仰嗜学能文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220387_comment'></div>仰父既葬君若干年，复见余于会稽，则论议益富，文益工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220387_comment'></div>其后以书抵余，求为君铭，所不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220387_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1220387'>正而朴，匪砻匪斫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220387_comment'></div>安且舒，惟仁是居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220387_comment'></div>狱政慈祥，有苾其芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220387_comment'></div>以遗其子，天其勿忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1220387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　居归安。与韩元吉交游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年8月2日</a>　居归安。叶梦得卒，有诗。作品：少保左丞叶公二首。<div id='poem_529361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529361?labeling=true' target='_blank'>少保左丞叶公挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529361")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529361'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529361'>四纪声华旧，三朝道义尊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529361'>微言真自乐，博识更谁论。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529361'>翰墨馀千载，哀荣付九原。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529361'>松杉倚幢节，愁绝暮烟昏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529361'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529361_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529362?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529362'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529362'>文章千古事，富贵百年身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529362'>并世今馀几，如公孰拟伦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529362'>轩裳清梦破，丘壑此心亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529362'>叹息常编旨，无从举似人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529362'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529362_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　居归安。为施钜之父作墓志铭。作品：宋故右朝奉郎致仕施府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故右朝奉郎致仕施府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220382")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220382'>府君讳某字某，姓施氏，湖州武康人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220382_comment'></div>曾大父某，大父某，父某，皆有潜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220382_comment'></div>家素儒，初未有大其门者，府君教子益力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220382_comment'></div>子钜体府君志，克励于学，艺业有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220382_comment'></div>丁年擢第，蚤通朝籍，为尚书郎、三院御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220382_comment'></div>未几，以御史出守括苍，奉府君之官，优游郡斋，就养无阙，士夫荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220382_comment'></div>阅岁得微疾，常膳少损，遽谢医，且笑曰：「吾闻高医能已疾，不闻能治老也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220382_comment'></div>既曰语家人：「吾欲静念空王境，以归宿吾心，毋怛我化」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220382_comment'></div>遂瞑不复言，实绍兴十七年四月一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220382_comment'></div>时府君累封至右朝奉郎，年七十有六矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220382_comment'></div>御史护丧归乡闾，以明年某月某日葬于县之东北大原乡京子之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220382_comment'></div>将葬，见属为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220382_comment'></div>府君天性纯孝，笃于奉亲，自始及终，苟可以顺适其意者，虽躬服劳不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220382_comment'></div>遇乡党和而辨，久而不媮，虽复犯己，不校如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220382_comment'></div>冲淡寡欲，一室萧然，不设属钥，未尝有姬妾之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220382_comment'></div>独喜翻贝叶书，偶方士语，不则与宾客衔杯漱醪，至一斗不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220382_comment'></div>襟抱怡怡，人莫见其有忧愠之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220382_comment'></div>振人之急，囊无留赀，而乡里言长者必归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220382_comment'></div>配周氏，先府君若干年卒，至是合祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220382_comment'></div>男三人：长曰铸，实任家事，不以毫发累府君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220382_comment'></div>钜其次也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220382_comment'></div>季曰蕴恭，为浮屠氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220382_comment'></div>女二人，适丁光祖、陈继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220382_comment'></div>孙男五，曰良友、良弼、良臣、良能、良辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220382_comment'></div>孙女三，适吴经、沈纯臣、张康，皆名进士，张为左迪功郎、德清县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220382_comment'></div>曾孙男女二十五人，曰沈康臣者，曾孙婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220382_comment'></div>余与御史俱为乡校诸生，晚而同朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220382_comment'></div>御史明粹简默人也，居家有曾、闵之孝，为吏有龚、黄之政，他日自见于世，又有大焉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220382_comment'></div>信乎，府君之积庆在兹也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220382_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1220382'>灵曰归与，京子之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220382_comment'></div>州演迤而纡馀，若顾吾而欲留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220382_comment'></div>山周卫而丛集，若旗旄之导乎前，骑卒之拥于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220382_comment'></div>与乡坐而拜者，兹青乌氏之卜与，曰君所自择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220382_comment'></div>惟永宁，以福于而子孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1220382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　居归安。刘一止从妹夫江寓卒，有墓志铭。作品：江仲宏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江仲宏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220378")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220378'>余从妹之夫江君寓字仲宏，年六十有三，绍兴十八年七月某甲子卒于官舍，以某年九月某甲子葬于湖州乌程县登静乡郑村某山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220378_comment'></div>再岁，其孤请铭，所不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220378_comment'></div>江氏世居衢之开化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220378_comment'></div>仲宏之裔高祖讳铭，任谏议大夫，为时吏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220378_comment'></div>曾祖枢，祖泊，父法，皆以世禄得官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220378_comment'></div>母赵氏系出玉牒，封宗城院君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220378_comment'></div>仲宏幼颖异，有识趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220378_comment'></div>数岁而孤，自念我母以己为命，益致志于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220378_comment'></div>未冠，游太学，试选屡优，见推辈行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220378_comment'></div>其文粹而雅，实深于经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220378_comment'></div>累举于礼部，乃不得志，归以所学教授弟子，以养其母，且训其子为孝为忠，言皆可则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220378_comment'></div>初自太学闻东浙有寇难，亟弃籍归奉其母居仪真，后迁居吴兴，岁久益困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220378_comment'></div>以时恩试居前列，授登仕郎，调贵州推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220378_comment'></div>庙堂故人以其母老难于远适，改除监通判支盐仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220378_comment'></div>处贪吏黩货之地，仲宏凛凛如冰霜，囊无一钱之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220378_comment'></div>部使者列荐于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220378_comment'></div>寻以忧去，服除，升右从事，调镇江府之金坛县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220378_comment'></div>位虽卑，有忧民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220378_comment'></div>将受代得疾，请致仕以卒，恩迁右宣义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220378_comment'></div>自君之来吴兴也，余始获拜宗城君于堂上，初未知其为宗胄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220378_comment'></div>吾妹在傍，钜细必禀，至米盐靡密之事，往复问语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220378_comment'></div>妇姑怡怡，意色相授，且顺且慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220378_comment'></div>察其服用饮食简陋之状，虽窭人子有不堪者，余心愕焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220378_comment'></div>容貌加肃，生于坐中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220378_comment'></div>既又察之，仲宏之爱其亲也笃，而我妹奉以周旋，故上下能相亲，且有礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220378_comment'></div>至其俭勤，实出天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220378_comment'></div>仲宏二子，曰崌、崃，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220378_comment'></div>一女尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220378_comment'></div>江之源出于岷山，分以崌崃，仲宏以命二子，欲其不忘本始，益疏而大之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220378_comment'></div>余每见二甥清臞可怜，言必道先训，诚有意于学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220378_comment'></div>服母丧，旦暮号泣，血溢两眦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220378_comment'></div>仲宏调官辇毂，仅留千钱为二子齑盐之费，比其还也，二子复归之，余以是叹仲宏之有子，其必有君子之归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220378_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1220378'>呜呼仲宏，闲遂敦庞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220378_comment'></div>积庆之源，有如此江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220378_comment'></div>衍而流之，远而大哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220378_comment'></div>我谂之铭，以诏崌崃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1220378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　居归安。有题跋。作品：跋司业许公墨帖后。<div id='poem_1220345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋司业许公墨帖后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220345")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220345'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220345'>司业许公在太学时，某为诸生，实相先后，因获从师德游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220345_comment'></div>公行义文学，一时宗师，非但乡里后进如某者知敬慕而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220345_comment'></div>逮今逾五十年，前辈轨迹既不可追，师德又下世，而得此卷轴于师德之令子，展读感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220345_comment'></div>谨识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1220345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年2月</a>　居归安。李正民卒，有诗。作品：李方叔侍郎一首。<div id='poem_529363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李方叔侍郎挽诗一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529363")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529363'>论议当今耸外庭，英英人物照丹青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529363'>文章共道追千古，训诂曾看媲六经。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529363'>畴昔鹓行今几在，异乡薤露不堪听。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529269'>古寺疏钟<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作烟）</span>里，因依孰并游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
