ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年7月4日</a>　居归安。复秘阁修撰致仕，上谢表。作品：谢复秘阁修撰致仕表。<div id='poem_1220258' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220258?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢复秘阁修撰致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年7月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220258")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220258'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220258'>投老乞身，既达由衷之请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220258_comment'></div>疏恩出綍，复叨遇主之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220258_comment'></div>感惧交怀，周章失次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220258_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣受性愚暗，逢时休明，以田野固陋之安，冒禁省论思之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220258_comment'></div>报效何有，践历已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220258_comment'></div>粤从去国以来，犹窃奉祠之秩，及兹疾疚，斗觉支离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220258_comment'></div>学无艺苑之工，职在书林之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220258_comment'></div>不图得谢，乃更增华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220258_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下天地之德曰生，日月之光必照，俛怜末路，不忍弃遗，始终保全，委曲成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220258_comment'></div>而臣迹居穷壑，绝望修门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220258_comment'></div>纳禄辞名，期少延于喘息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220258_comment'></div>击瓶拊缶，尚同乐于升平。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220258_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年9月24日</a>　居归安。上中兴圣德诗，擢敷文阁待制，有辞免状。作品：辞免除敷文阁待制状。<div id='poem_1220240' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220240' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220240?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除敷文阁待制状<span class='inlineComment2'>（致仕后再除。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220240")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220240_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220240'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220240'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220240_comment'></div>右，臣今月某日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣敷文阁待制者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220240_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220240_comment'></div>伏念臣性识暗陋，人地卑凡，叨冒以来，无补丝发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220240_comment'></div>中自知愧，一时得谢，归老山林，获与田夫野老歌咏圣化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220240_comment'></div>不自揆度，希慕前哲，作为颂诗，仰尘乙览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220240_comment'></div>冒昧进越，方惧严诛，敢图睿慈，骤加宠灵，俾参从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220240_comment'></div>天地父母，恩重不赀，粉骨碎身，何以称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220240_comment'></div>然而次对之职，位秩优隆，岂臣么微所宜躐处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220240_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣諴悃，追寝误恩，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220240_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220240_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220240_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年9月24日</a>　居归安。上中兴圣德诗，擢敷文阁待制，有谢表。作品：谢除敷文阁待制表。<div id='poem_1220259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除敷文阁待制表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220259")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220259'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220259'>乞身故里，已叨从欲之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220259_comment'></div>通籍甘泉，更冒踰渥之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220259_comment'></div>自天锡命，蹐地靡容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220259_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣逢时休明，受性暗漏，误膺识拔，荐被使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220259_comment'></div>报无丝发之微，德有丘山之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220259_comment'></div>辞荣纳禄，既逾七十之年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220259_comment'></div>穷思毕精，莫辨三千之牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220259_comment'></div>不量浅薄，辄露悃诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220259_comment'></div>采田夫野老之谣，述帝德王功之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220259_comment'></div>乾坤之大，日月之明，岂绘画之所能，顾迂愚其已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220259_comment'></div>敢云宏度，俛鉴懦衷，俾列职于近班，以增华于末路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220259_comment'></div>得此殊遇，繄臣何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220259_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下躬聪明睿智之资，蕴广大精微之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220259_comment'></div>疏观百王之法，超视三代之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220259_comment'></div>总揽化枢，激扬士类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220259_comment'></div>有如么么，亦在甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220259_comment'></div>骤颁涣汗之新，垂记生成之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220259_comment'></div>而臣迹居穷壑，望远修门，心未替于倾葵，誓独存于结草。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年9月24日</a>　居归安。上中兴圣德诗，擢敷文阁待制，上谢启。作品：致仕除敷文阁待制谢启。<div id='poem_1220308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致仕除敷文阁待制谢启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220308")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220308'>涣恩骤至，成命莫回，拜赐逡巡，省躬怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220308_comment'></div>伏念某曩膺识拔，出自寒微，初无寸长，服在近列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220308_comment'></div>惟践更之既久，曾效见之靡闻，病且不支，老当以退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220308_comment'></div>不图得谢，乃更增华，方寓直于书林，遽躐升于从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220308_comment'></div>湔摩昏眚，诵纶告之温慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220308_comment'></div>扶掖拘挛，服腰镮之焕丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220308_comment'></div>闾里赞喜，亲旧改容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220308_comment'></div>顾惟何人，有此侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220308_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官量涵海岳，诚贯幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220308_comment'></div>有周公成王家之忠，迈伊尹格皇天之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220308_comment'></div>功高不伐，位重益谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220308_comment'></div>谓才能皆可陶镕，虽疵贱亦归覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220308_comment'></div>重惟无似，特受深知，始终保全，委曲成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220308_comment'></div>叨踰已甚，惧弱植之弗胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220308_comment'></div>报称谓何，独此心之不昧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　居归安。为郑绩之父作墓表。作品：宋故右朝请大大郑君墓表。<div id='poem_1220389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故右朝请大夫郑君墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220389")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220389'>君讳某，字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220389_comment'></div>五代祖昱为湖州长兴令，子孙家焉，因是为长兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220389_comment'></div>曾祖某，故任睦州遂安令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220389_comment'></div>祖某、父某，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220389_comment'></div>君以其子绩仕班朝籍，累封右朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220389_comment'></div>绍兴十一年十一月二十七日卒，享年八十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220389_comment'></div>明年三月丙申葬于归安县开化里，后十年赠至右朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220389_comment'></div>绩语余曰：「先君幼失怙恃，嶷然自立，力学不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220389_comment'></div>梦有所授，乃自晦，弃科举，独玩意浮屠氏之学，读其书甚广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220389_comment'></div>中年有得，心意融释，视死生如昨梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220389_comment'></div>平时邃于天文地理卜筮之说，一日语人曰：『吾生丁酉，月日时皆火属，合岁在辛酉，火以类至，其死矣，白难之年也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220389_comment'></div>继得疾，屏药谢医，炷香沃盥，曰：『明日入辛酉，吾终于此矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220389_comment'></div>复戒绩曰：『葬用山地之险也，有甚吉必有甚凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220389_comment'></div>吾以是得夷坦之地，为安我葬，从汝母之旁善矣，且我自卜也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220389_comment'></div>绩奉治命惟谨，独隧者之铭未立，私心恧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220389_comment'></div>顾畴昔官学相追，其言可信于后世者十不一二存，今不子求而求之谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220389_comment'></div>固将以表诸墓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220389_comment'></div>既而闻之乡老曰：「君学道坚决，若与物无心，而事所当为，靡不周尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220389_comment'></div>律身俭勤、教子孙甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220389_comment'></div>遇宗族乡党甚信且厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220389_comment'></div>居长兴时，有宅一区、田一顷，在归安之琏市，仅足了伏腊即徙焉，捐其先居之产，悉以与族人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220389_comment'></div>其后赀稍裕，葬族党亲故者十数，与隆寒苦雪闾里之不能衣食者，持薪米缯絮往周之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220389_comment'></div>一饭之德必报，其人虽亡，见其子若孙，则如其人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220389_comment'></div>性实刚介，朋友或愆于义，必面折无隐情，故所至皆亲重之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220389_comment'></div>余是以益知君为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220389_comment'></div>配朱氏，与君俱学道，志行坚确，前君若干年无疾坐逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220389_comment'></div>男二人：绩，右朝奉大夫、新两浙东路安抚司参议官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220389_comment'></div>道如，祝发为僧，住临安府天井山普应禅院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220389_comment'></div>孙一人，嗣执，业进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220389_comment'></div>曾孙三人，膺、胥、脩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220389_comment'></div>余不及识君，而从绩游有年数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220389_comment'></div>绩脩洁博习，时辈所推，既登科，名闻诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220389_comment'></div>尝被选擢，自中都官出为部使者，及佐师间，其进未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220389_comment'></div>余既得君善行，而绩见属意甚厚，不敢以固陋辞，姑叙所闻，以诏后人云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1220389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　居归安。为刘尧佐之母向氏作墓志铭。作品：宋故魏国太夫人向氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故魏国太夫人向氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220385")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220385'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220385'>故和众辅国功臣、太傅、护国镇安保静军节度使、杨国公、赠太师、谥武僖刘公讳某之室曰向氏，以绍兴二十一年十二月四日薨于赐第之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220385_comment'></div>明年五月十九日葬钱塘之排山，合祔于太师公之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220385_comment'></div>其子尧佐以书抵一止，曰：「吾母既葬矣，隧未有铭，敢以为请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220385_comment'></div>一止昔者尝侍太师燕席，且从向氏伯仲游，稔夫人懿行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220385_comment'></div>矧一代名将相之家，声实昭人，于纪述无愧，所不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220385_comment'></div>惟向氏其先河内人，后家于开封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220385_comment'></div>自汉晋以来，屡有闻人，然未克光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220385_comment'></div>至我朝秦文简公讳某，始相真宗皇帝，翊赞太平，功德甚盛，流泽演迤，溢于孙子，是生钦圣宪肃皇后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220385_comment'></div>夫人文简五世孙，钦圣之侄孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220385_comment'></div>以故定国军节度观察留后、追封秦王、谥康懿讳经者为大王父，以故检校少保、保平军节度使、开府仪同三司、充中太一宫使、汉东郡王、赠太师讳宗回者为王父，以故朝议大夫、通判河中府讳子章者为考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220385_comment'></div>夫人生十二岁，以后恩封济阳郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220385_comment'></div>朝议以其有异相，择所宜适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220385_comment'></div>时太师从父鲁公镇西陲，居幕府中，年少英特，资貌粹温，甚武且文，朝议一见伟之，以夫人归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220385_comment'></div>刘氏族大且显，皇姑葛氏性严介有家法，不以色假诸妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220385_comment'></div>夫人若寠人子，执礼益恭，姑特贤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220385_comment'></div>太师父子以威名雄陕右，国家倚之，隐如长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220385_comment'></div>其后遭时多艰，执戈卫社，多立奇绩，仕通显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220385_comment'></div>夫人勉以忠孝，不绝于口，每言国恩，举手加额者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220385_comment'></div>故太师礼之如宾，赖之如良友朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220385_comment'></div>每奉命专征，不顾其家，内外数百口，合屯营部曲室家，无虑数千万，繄夫人是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220385_comment'></div>建炎中敌入江浙，太师以御营副使镇江州，留家江西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220385_comment'></div>时寇盗四起，摽掠旁近，部曲惶践少自安，夫人劳之曰：「尔等无恐，寇至我躬见之，彼知吾家，必不敢肆暴也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220385_comment'></div>而寇至，知太师营，旋即散去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220385_comment'></div>绍兴三年，太师军池阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220385_comment'></div>明年，大敌窥江，诏全师控乌家渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220385_comment'></div>敌退，策勋，上以夫人能相其夫绥靖部曲，致士卒无返顾，效死克敌，加封魏国夫人，仍月赐汤沐赀如内职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220385_comment'></div>太师三辞，不获命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220385_comment'></div>尝入见，上面谕曰：「夫人相家子，又钦圣近属，非他人比」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220385_comment'></div>继称贺慈宁宫，太后顾曰：「夫人习气不凡，柔嘉可则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220385_comment'></div>一时命妇，咸歆艳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220385_comment'></div>凡疏封者十，晋、康、秦、楚、润、蜀等皆所封之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220385_comment'></div>晚以二子登朝籍，进封魏国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220385_comment'></div>享年六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220385_comment'></div>夫人端懿淑茂，寡笑与言，不见愠喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220385_comment'></div>壸政甚修，中外井井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220385_comment'></div>相春秋之事，视涤濯羞簠簋，斋庄待旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220385_comment'></div>御族党信且厚，有疾病不克扶持，与贫不能嫁娶丧葬者，斥赀财与之，所赖以济者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220385_comment'></div>视妾媵若己子，疑妒之念不萌于胸中，忿恚之色不形于颜貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220385_comment'></div>薰然慈仁，有犯己者，初若不闻，人自愧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220385_comment'></div>平居励其子以学，俾从贤士游，且曰：「贤者非礼意不辱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220385_comment'></div>虽有甚费，不靳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220385_comment'></div>故其子咸有可观，文行彬彬，好古惇雅，缙绅称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220385_comment'></div>奉夫人孝谨，岁时胜赏，方舟安舆，颐指办具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220385_comment'></div>人谓夫人虽不登上寿，而雍容閒居之乐，无所恨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220385_comment'></div>男四人：曰尧臣，武德郎、閤门宣赞舍人，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220385_comment'></div>曰尧佐，右承议郎、直敷文阁、赐紫金鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220385_comment'></div>曰尧仁，右宣议郎、直敷文阁、赐紫金鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220385_comment'></div>曰尧勋，右宣议郎，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220385_comment'></div>曰球，右承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220385_comment'></div>女四人，宁国军承宣使、浙东路副都总管满温卿，右承议郎、通判筠州军州事吴希祥，右承议郎、宗正丞张宗元，其婿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220385_comment'></div>其一未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220385_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1220385'>向望河内，名人间出，自我文简，始大赫奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220385_comment'></div>流泽演迤，于后有溢，是生明德，光俪宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220385_comment'></div>国有父母，家有壸则，侃侃夫人，是训是式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220385_comment'></div>归嫔钜公，曰惟太师，太师奕代，镇于西陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220385_comment'></div>智略纵横，且文且武，隐如长城，实固吾圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220385_comment'></div>逮时艰虞，执戈卫主，凛然向敌，身先其旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220385_comment'></div>闻命引道，寘家江浒，盗发四旁，小大惴惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220385_comment'></div>屯营室家，我则恩之，效死固守，罔敢叛携。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220385_comment'></div>克相君子，懋以忠赤，寅奉其先，蘋藻是职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220385_comment'></div>侈泰矜夸，不见于色，斥其馀帑，拯难扶疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220385_comment'></div>以询其子，必时名儒，文行彬彬，左琴右书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220385_comment'></div>水有方舟，陆有安舆，岁时胜赏，款款舒舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220385_comment'></div>汤沐之封，十更名国，始终哀荣，孰与伦匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220385_comment'></div>排山几几，将相之阡，过者下车，铭在墓前。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1220385'></div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1220385_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　居归安。为闻人作墓志铭。作品：宋故闻人府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故闻人府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220388")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220388'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220388'>余曩以柱史失职罪黜，寓家德清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220388_comment'></div>暇日浮扁舟，访川岩于邻邑，中流遇风，命拽舟傍林墅，暮夜不得所栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220388_comment'></div>问亭传，曰无有，独酒垆在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220388_comment'></div>问主垆为谁，曰闻人君，长者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220388_comment'></div>余得假宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220388_comment'></div>访主人，曰适他墅矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220388_comment'></div>质明将兴，则奴奉匜在户外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220388_comment'></div>余沃盥仅毕，君出迎有礼貌，自言：「昨暮无他适，盖窥公于屏间，识公非尘凡人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220388_comment'></div>固欲饭余，具甚设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220388_comment'></div>自是识君，率间岁一相过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220388_comment'></div>坐客有及求田事者，余以囊无金谢之，君窃听若不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220388_comment'></div>阅数日持券来，曰：「乡公与客语田事，寻物色其处，以缗钱千为公得之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220388_comment'></div>余惊谢不敢留者七八，君曰：「他日以直归我，未晚也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220388_comment'></div>如是十馀年，仅能偿半，余刺促不自安，君无半辞及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220388_comment'></div>一日扶羸过余，曰：「吾得疾且病，故来取别」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220388_comment'></div>久之，出笔札相授，曰：「向所负已折券，惧吾子若孙不察吾意，或相督取」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220388_comment'></div>余曰：「自吾居里间，虽甚困，不贷人一钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220388_comment'></div>所见士大夫，有急叩人门，虽甚薄少不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220388_comment'></div>今君捐数十万钱不取，如弃涕唾，授受之际不应如是之轻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220388_comment'></div>君以笔札抵案，径不返顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220388_comment'></div>余愧其意，每从人言之，知君者皆云，闻人君乐善好义，辞气质直，不为表暴，意所欲，必为之，类此颇众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220388_comment'></div>然非余意也，念终当偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220388_comment'></div>又三岁而君卒，其子颀袖书来乞铭，余固欲表其事，不复辞，且使后人知君所为槩可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220388_comment'></div>君讳誉，字声甫，世居湖州之武康，曾大父永，大父亿，父济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220388_comment'></div>君未尝业儒，而举动不愆于礼义，奉亲孝谨，承颜顺旨，生事死葬，无毫发可恨，乡里称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220388_comment'></div>振贫恤孤，不见所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220388_comment'></div>自幼至老，属意浮屠氏之学，以精进布施为实行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220388_comment'></div>建殿阁、严像设者十数，诵内典、饭缁流不可以数计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220388_comment'></div>名山桥梁应创，与通衢径街、并岩险仄应布砖，虽绵亘甚远，皆独任之，行路受其赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220388_comment'></div>平时多从方外有道者游，晚岁若有得，临终索汤沐，炷香敛念，语旁观曰：「闻人某有道行与否，在今日矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220388_comment'></div>实绍兴二十三年八月戊寅也，享年七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220388_comment'></div>以其年十一月壬寅葬于所居之南二十里崇仁乡南岳山之原，从先君之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220388_comment'></div>室李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220388_comment'></div>男二人：颀泰州助教，早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220388_comment'></div>顺从信使出疆，补官，转承节郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220388_comment'></div>女三人，适邑人姚惇、施良佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220388_comment'></div>孙男六，良贵、良臣、良翰、良心、良器、良才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220388_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1220388'>川可回，石可泐，惟兹铭，诏罔极。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1220388'></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1220388_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　居归安。为张旬作墓志铭。作品：宋故左朝请大夫致仕张府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故左朝请大夫致仕张府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220390")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220390'>君讳旬，字述功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220390_comment'></div>其先居吴郡，后徙青墩镇，遂为秀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220390_comment'></div>逮君之考，复卜筑湖之乌墩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220390_comment'></div>曾大父叔和、大父宗祐晦迹不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220390_comment'></div>考育，以君叙封至朝散郎致仕，累赠右正议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220390_comment'></div>母丁氏，追封硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220390_comment'></div>君自少颖异，不肯碌碌，尝语人曰：「家以儒为名，未有显者，吾甚恨焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220390_comment'></div>折节读书，游学亲师友，不惮寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220390_comment'></div>掌教者伟其文，每揭示诸生，而以为轨则，故同学者皆自知不敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220390_comment'></div>已而荐名乡书为第一，登崇宁五年进士第，授将仕郎，调婺州兰溪县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220390_comment'></div>大观中用八宝赦恩转登仕郎，终更，用荐升通仕郎，乃授杭州钱塘丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220390_comment'></div>府郎、部使者以文字知君，荐书交相上，改京秩，知严州桐庐县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220390_comment'></div>吏戴谅者为奸，隐欺税租，君具按治得实事上闻，与赏格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220390_comment'></div>时户部辟监麦科下第一界，君以道远不便亲养，丐监越州盐仓司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220390_comment'></div>遇渊圣皇帝及今皇帝践祚，迁二官，授签书宁国军节度判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220390_comment'></div>于考功格，应赐绯衣银鱼，君以亲老侍养无几日，自列于朝，愿以身章贲其亲，有旨从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220390_comment'></div>未赴宁国间，丁父忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220390_comment'></div>免丧，监行在所诸司粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220390_comment'></div>将之官，君自念禄不逮亲，欲出疏乞闲，再更宫祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220390_comment'></div>会有旨侍从官各荐贤能，君在荐中，除知南剑州，寻易徽州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220390_comment'></div>任满造朝，除知严陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220390_comment'></div>俄得肺疾，乞以郡易奉祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220390_comment'></div>踰年请老，以疾终于家，实绍兴二十三年十二月六日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220390_comment'></div>享年七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220390_comment'></div>自改京秩，九迁至左朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220390_comment'></div>君妙年初仕，于吏道已若素习，遇事精敏，老吏竦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220390_comment'></div>在兰溪时，民有甲乙争田中水沟者，甲曰田有沟旧矣，乙曰券有塍耳，宁后沟耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220390_comment'></div>讼久不决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220390_comment'></div>君呼耆老问之，水沟异名谓何，曰「俗谓之圳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220390_comment'></div>又问，曰「中径田俗谓之塍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220390_comment'></div>君取券熟视，曰：「我得之矣，易圳为塍，是殆匿沟为己有也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220390_comment'></div>争者语塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220390_comment'></div>杭为会府，往来多要人，寺僧义闻假权要势，占民产，官吏拱默不敢决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220390_comment'></div>君官小无所顾望，一绳以法，闻者韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220390_comment'></div>桐庐县剧，政率以猛，君独本以恩信，追科不烦，而事悉办给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220390_comment'></div>民健讼，相侵渔，尺度不明，君未尝委官吏按视，曰：「是徒为纷纷扰民尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220390_comment'></div>命图状来上，反覆问诘，往往情露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220390_comment'></div>民甚爱君，比其去也，遮道借留，不减古人，至绘像祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220390_comment'></div>其治徽亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220390_comment'></div>奉行宽诏，谓德意不下逮，为承流宣化者之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220390_comment'></div>或言郡经费不足，君曰：「郡经费出于民，而有艺极者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220390_comment'></div>民赋输无爽而用不足，是必有弊欺不归公上者，弊在吏胥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220390_comment'></div>久之尽得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220390_comment'></div>邻郡狴犴有留系不决，部刺史悉以委君，涣然尽释，皆自以为不冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220390_comment'></div>初除严州，民相贺曰：「是尝为桐庐矣，惠且及我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220390_comment'></div>君蚤失母，事父孝谨，每仕，以亲养为急，不汲汲于进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220390_comment'></div>父死将葬，日者以岁庚申，君生之年也，盍避之，君斥去，曰：「吾岂以拘忌私己之说易吾意耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220390_comment'></div>律身严，家政肃，小大井井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220390_comment'></div>平居未尝废书，为文粹美，自其少时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220390_comment'></div>有集三十卷藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220390_comment'></div>课子弟学，朝暮谆谆，故亲族与计偕、取高第者相踵于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220390_comment'></div>晚岁手抄释氏典殆百卷，神情恬悦，若有得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220390_comment'></div>以明年正月丙申葬于湖州长兴肆惟新乡龙潭坞之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220390_comment'></div>娶濮氏，封宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220390_comment'></div>子庇，右迪功郎、前监潭州南岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220390_comment'></div>孙男女六人，颜将仕郎，颁、顷、頔，女尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220390_comment'></div>君历任久，既官其子孙，又以明堂赦与致仕恩及其兄弟之子二人，曰席曰庶云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220390_comment'></div>前事之月，庶以其弟康之状求君铭，始得尽其平生，且恨施用之未既也，铭其可辞哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220390_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1220390'>君生弱龄，秉志自强，谓家世儒，厥问不扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220390_comment'></div>折节读书，艺业益励，隆师尚友，以开后继，奕叶有光，自君起第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220390_comment'></div>粤初筮仕，宛若素习，健决力行，老吏惴慄，深年之讼，一讯语塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220390_comment'></div>奸贪婪攘，或怙权贵，官吏拱默，罔敢有异，君虽位卑，了不顾忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220390_comment'></div>桐庐之政，恩信并立，追科不烦，民用宁壹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220390_comment'></div>豪强兼并，尺度晦匿，君曰委吏，是益蟊贼，命图来上，反覆问诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220390_comment'></div>彼民爱君，于今不忘，岁时奉尝，有如桐乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220390_comment'></div>君之治狱，岂弟舒舒，僚吏以苦，经费是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220390_comment'></div>君曰此民，不足赋输，弊岂在民，弊在吏胥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220390_comment'></div>抉摘蔽欺，谨所应入，曾未几时，用度有溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220390_comment'></div>惟君孝友，出自天性，仕每便亲，不急于进，暨服亲丧，志乃不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220390_comment'></div>既久得疾，请老于朝，尚期季年，燕居逍遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220390_comment'></div>迹君行能，与名与位，小见于时，用则未既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220390_comment'></div>龙潭之原，卜云其臧，纳铭墓中，以永厥藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_71_1220390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　居归安。为钱观后作墓志铭。作品：宋故左朝散郎赐绯鱼袋钱君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故左朝散郎赐绯鱼袋钱君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220393")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220393'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220393'>君讳观复，字知原，平江常熟人，于吴越王钱氏为疏属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220393_comment'></div>忠肃王举图入朝，君奕世为士，不与恩泽侯之列，独赐田在常熟之李墓，因家焉，后徙居邑中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220393_comment'></div>曾祖训、祖仁贵，隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220393_comment'></div>父衍，累赠右朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220393_comment'></div>君天资颖异，自少小知务学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220393_comment'></div>一日大书谷梁子「成童不就师」之语于门，朝议公惊喜，招延名士教之，读书制文，度越流辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220393_comment'></div>年十七当赴举，会祖母李氏将葬，君不就赴以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220393_comment'></div>或勉之，则曰：「祖母恩我厚矣，今不与执事，后悔何及」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220393_comment'></div>是夕，梦有告以岁若干当登科，自是益自信，不以毫发非正干定命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220393_comment'></div>由郡学升辟雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220393_comment'></div>政和九年，以行艺两优释褐，赐上舍及第，授将仕郎，调越州诸暨县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220393_comment'></div>已而用释褐第三名，特恩改授从事郎、温州府学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220393_comment'></div>温号多士，君风励程督，学者知劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220393_comment'></div>岁终，以教悉溢额循文林郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220393_comment'></div>终更过瑞安，巨寇方腊猖獗，道梗不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220393_comment'></div>县令王公济，君素所厚也，往赞之，讲画备御，悉自君出，公济信之不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220393_comment'></div>时旁郡邑皆焚剽，流民归瑞安，相属于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220393_comment'></div>或议驱出境，君曰：「孰为善境？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220393_comment'></div>驱之适资寇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220393_comment'></div>并海有洲，徒流者数十辈居焉，载粮就廪，绝其航渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220393_comment'></div>顷之，流民自献其能，鍜冶兵械一新，又募鎗杖手之趫捷果悍素有称者用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220393_comment'></div>贼沮败，不敢犯境，公济推君功第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220393_comment'></div>君不自言辄止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220393_comment'></div>次调湖州司户曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220393_comment'></div>郡守治尚严察，吏阴拱以观，不一启口论当否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220393_comment'></div>事有愆于情法者，君独力争，初不谓然，已而悔服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220393_comment'></div>同郡富人朱姓勔名者，以附丽得官，骤致通显，其力足以福祸人，内外搢绅咸畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220393_comment'></div>以君登巍科，为时闻人，愿以女归君，君不答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220393_comment'></div>同舍谓君盍俯就之，当得美仕为亲荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220393_comment'></div>君曰：「吁，是何言欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220393_comment'></div>吾虽贫，持菽水奉亲，亲乐也，有如假托非类以进，岂吾亲意也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220393_comment'></div>苟如子言，适取辱，何荣之有」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220393_comment'></div>闻者韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220393_comment'></div>至是报罢，莫测其由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220393_comment'></div>或曰：「此朱氏力也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220393_comment'></div>久之，调楚州司户曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220393_comment'></div>到官七月，丁朝议公丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220393_comment'></div>君生理不给，既服丧归，益困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220393_comment'></div>时郡县计民税输钱，官自贸绢取赢，资甚厚，县尹怜君贫，愿以千缣归君输，俾自收其赢，君戄然谢之，固穷如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220393_comment'></div>服除，调衢州军事判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220393_comment'></div>虏骑犯江浙，衢当路冲，君白郡守，纵民老弱毕出户，留一丁，不留与留而残弱不堪任者罪如军法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220393_comment'></div>其后卒徒欲乘时为变，顾城中金帛子女，无可冀获，乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220393_comment'></div>以劳循儒林郎，秩满，再除衢州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220393_comment'></div>未赴，丁继母恭人范氏忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220393_comment'></div>服除，改左通直郎，除国子监丞，寻改充诸王宫大小学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220393_comment'></div>满岁，相继除太常丞、秘书郎、尚书户部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220393_comment'></div>君仕州县久，谙练庶事，居省户若素习，吏不敢欺，声名赫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220393_comment'></div>意且用矣，俄以言罢，主管台州崇道观，前后八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220393_comment'></div>起知广德军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220393_comment'></div>始至，访民利害，立罢行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220393_comment'></div>地居高陆，岁上供，民输建平仓，由湖转江入丹阳闸以达行在，所道回远，复加歛为赀费，号水脚钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220393_comment'></div>君亟请于朝，寄廪湖之四安，相距才五十里，民不病劳，循运河至国门不过五日，费减大半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220393_comment'></div>或谓地产竹木，官吏失讥察，逸税籍甚多，君以细民肩荷手持，冀十百以活妻子，其忍扼取之，且惧开端为后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220393_comment'></div>雨旸小愆，斋祷于神，致礼甚恭，虽历旬月无倦色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220393_comment'></div>至民俗用巫觋语，屠割埋瘗，不合典常，卜非神意者，悉命禁绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220393_comment'></div>岁饥，议发常平仓，部使者屡抑君，君手书谕属邑振廪济民，且曰：「民命在朝夕，吾能不独任擅发之责乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220393_comment'></div>旱益甚，境内田十损八九，复请于朝，愿尽捐岁租以活一方，后卒如君言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220393_comment'></div>大抵君为政，以爱利百姓为心，惟恐弗及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220393_comment'></div>苟利民，力行之，不顾己私，类若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220393_comment'></div>君在郡，忧劳成疾，比满秩归，增剧，以绍兴二十四年十一月十二日终于家之正寝，享年六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220393_comment'></div>累官至左朝散郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220393_comment'></div>娶徐氏，故吏部尚书铎之女，封安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220393_comment'></div>男四人：曰俣，左迪功郎、新绍兴府山阴县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220393_comment'></div>曰佃，左从政郎，池州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220393_comment'></div>曰佖、曰僩、学进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220393_comment'></div>僩后一岁以哀毁卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220393_comment'></div>女二人，长适右迪功郎、监潭州合同茶场陈大年，次适左宣教郎、新筠州州学教授徐廷献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220393_comment'></div>诸孤以二十二年正月辛酉葬君于县虞山之南，距大父茔五百弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220393_comment'></div>君有志节，执义坚固，不曲意求合，以希荐引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220393_comment'></div>平居简重，临危健决，智略横出，皆契事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220393_comment'></div>事亲孝谨，求所以顺适其意者不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220393_comment'></div>初，朝议公尝称债于人至三百万，晚岁赀产耗，无以偿，忧见于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220393_comment'></div>君窃诣予钱家，以己名就易券，别示必偿，朝议意乃安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1220393_comment'></div>其后予钱家更兵火，子孙散亡，契验不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1220393_comment'></div>君躬俭勤，抑损妄费，生理稍葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1220393_comment'></div>他日持六十万钱归郡人朱氏，朱氏以不闻父祖遗言拒弗受，君曰：「若不闻，如吾知之何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1220393_comment'></div>既而次第访寻，遍偿之，不负一钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1220393_comment'></div>人有急扣门，不以事为解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1220393_comment'></div>尤不喜修怨，尝有说君者，加谤讟甚至，君弗校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1220393_comment'></div>异时其家凋零，子若孙来归，率报礼之，未尝及前事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1220393_comment'></div>尝自谓出仕久，狃习世故，失其性真，及奉祠累年，意泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1220393_comment'></div>惟老学不衰，无顷刻废书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1220393_comment'></div>或探内典，究死生性命之说，自号「正静居士」，且名其所居之堂，以谕诸子甚笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1220393_comment'></div>故俣、佃游太学为名士，试选屡优，朋类敛衽，知不敌，相继登第，乡里荣之，以为君操履之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1220393_comment'></div>君邃于经，溢于文辞，尤喜为诗，有文集十五卷，《论语解》二十卷藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1220393_comment'></div>前葬四月，长子俣以余与君有一日之雅，稔君出处，细书造门，以铭见属，辞情恳迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1220393_comment'></div>余老病，神意昏耗，屡谢不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1220393_comment'></div>俣曰：「先君治命，且吾母朝夕冀也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1220393_comment'></div>其忍辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1220393_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_1220393'>君少之时敏而文，励且勤，以发厥身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1220393_comment'></div>仕更阅，志刚决，以昌其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1220393_comment'></div>任不过尚书郎，官不登上大夫，有蕴未输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1220393_comment'></div>孰使然欤，命也，吁！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1220393'></div><div id='poem_sentence_92_1220393_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年12月11日</a>　居归安。应召赴行在，朝廷欲起用。刘一止上辞免状，以老且疾力辞。作品：辞免召赴行在状。<div id='poem_1220241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220241?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免召赴行在状</a><span class='authorDate'>（乙亥年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220241")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220241'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220241'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220241_comment'></div>右，臣今月某日准尚书省劄子，十二月十二日三省同奉圣旨，刘某可落致仕，召赴行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220241_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220241_comment'></div>伏念臣才疏识陋，无长可录，遭遇圣明，冒忝近班，更践既多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220241_comment'></div>及兹老病，纳禄里居，获与斯民歌咏德化，在臣之分，可谓过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220241_comment'></div>不图圣恩，垂记疵贱，猥加召命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220241_comment'></div>仰戴眷怜，粉骨碎身，不足报塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220241_comment'></div>然臣行年七十有八，疾病耗昏，两耳重听，兼曾因坠伤，右腿筋挛，拜跪不得，于今累年，难以朝见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220241_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣愚悃，匪出伪为，特降睿旨，追寝误恩，许臣依旧致仕，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220241_comment'></div>所有召命，不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220241_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220241_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年12月25日</a>　至临安国门，除敷文阁直学士，复上辞免状。作品：谢除敷文阁直学士表。<div id='poem_1220260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除敷文阁直学士表<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年12月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220260")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220260_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1220260_0'>① 落致仕，召赴行在，恳辞至再，除职，依旧致仕。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220260'>祗承严召，怅旅力之久愆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220260_comment'></div>加贲恩章，许馀生之自佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220260_comment'></div>仰拜自天之锡，俯增蹐地之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220260_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>伏念臣奋由寒乡，出迎盛旦，以儒生之固陋，尘法从之高华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220260_comment'></div>悉出误知，不由他力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220260_comment'></div>粤从去国，旋自乞身，犹辱记其姓名，俾复趋于表著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220260_comment'></div>而臣老随年至，形以病羸，驱驰徒有于此心，跪起惧乖于常度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220260_comment'></div>达忱诚之恳款，荷聪听之矜从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220260_comment'></div>直内阁以跻荣，驾安车而遄反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220260_comment'></div>缙绅改观，闾里生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220260_comment'></div>惟初终被遇之过优，虽顶踵縻捐而莫报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220260_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁深覆载，明并照临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220260_comment'></div>察臣曩岁之遭逢，粗存忠谨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220260_comment'></div>知臣今日之疲曳，非敢怀安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220260_comment'></div>矧当圣政之新，尤以人材为急，凡在搜扬之数，举兴奋励之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220260_comment'></div>独臣数奇，赋分至薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220260_comment'></div>正周室任贤之日，既自至于不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220260_comment'></div>遇汉家好老之朝，又阻陪于在列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220260_comment'></div>时哉难得，命也奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220260_comment'></div>念虚受于宠灵，曾莫酬于寸尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220260_comment'></div>望云注想，永怀恋慕之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220260_comment'></div>击壤成歌，愿述治安之乐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1220260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年12月25日</a>　至临安国门，除敷文阁直学士，复上辞免状后，诏依旧致仕，上谢表。作品：辞免除敷文阁直学士恩命不允批答。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年5月27日</a>　居归安。有湖州石冢村青莲院记。<div id='poem_1220362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州石冢村青莲院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年5月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220362")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220362'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220362'>出城南行五十里，少东有村曰石冢，其梵刹曰青莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220362_comment'></div>唐大顺二年始建，乾宁中得额为「报恩禅院」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220362_comment'></div>至国朝治平二年赐今额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220362_comment'></div>环水为院，四无居邻，盖栖心学道之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220362_comment'></div>初若无路，惟轻航短楫至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220362_comment'></div>粥鱼斋鼓，闻于傍近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220362_comment'></div>禺中而食，则孤烟突起于云水渺㳽之间，望之郁然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220362_comment'></div>余未及造也，问诸道傍：「彼僧院者何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220362_comment'></div>曰：「院不至崇大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220362_comment'></div>已而规制整整，精丽明洁为可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220362_comment'></div>异时垣颓壁败，栋宇倾挠，左右撑柱，更阅岁久，观者悸心，如将压焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220362_comment'></div>今院僧慈济人师齐岳，尽彻其故而一新之，盛矣哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220362_comment'></div>余同识岳：「是妙于医者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220362_comment'></div>曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220362_comment'></div>岳自少习卢华之术，通金匮石室之书，以是济人，亦以自养身，余尝赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220362_comment'></div>一日过余，始询其事，岳曰：「吾受业自院，既而游方累年，稍倦而归，视所谓受业之区，几为荒墟，惕然动容，寝不安席，炷香自誓，勉励其术，以所得赀财，次第建立，不敢有一毫之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220362_comment'></div>是吾之发是心也，以疾扣门者加众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220362_comment'></div>吾潜心以思，思则得之，疾无重轻，赋药授方辄验，可期以时日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220362_comment'></div>又有知我之有是心者，乃力而交助之，市木于某乡，采石于某山，有不受赀而愿施者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220362_comment'></div>自绍兴戊午距今十有九年，而众工释用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220362_comment'></div>初营三门，再岁而办斋厨次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220362_comment'></div>厨成，而二时清众合食堂上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220362_comment'></div>僧舍钟楼、观音大士殿又次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220362_comment'></div>最后建转轮宝藏，极一时金碧之工，灿烂升离，夺人眸子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220362_comment'></div>吹螺击鼓，铿鍧于庑廊之下，施利日至，斋厨之费，赖此以给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220362_comment'></div>布砖累甓，内外前后，纤悉备具」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220362_comment'></div>余怪而问之：「是何成之易耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220362_comment'></div>岳曰：「吾志于成矣，然成之者非吾也，意其有阴相焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220362_comment'></div>何以云然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220362_comment'></div>吾之术不加于昔也，而灵于人若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220362_comment'></div>事既济矣，自今以往，不自料吾之术复能灵于其身若此其易者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220362_comment'></div>以是知世之怀自利之私，求得于人，而偶得之，以为吾能彼不能者，妄也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220362_comment'></div>余闻其言而韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220362_comment'></div>岳求记于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220362_comment'></div>余年七十有九，病且昏，岂复能文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220362_comment'></div>既赏其勤，且有感于其言，而为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220362_comment'></div>余于世间之见，固未能超出也，又欲于此警夫后之人，可哂也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220362_comment'></div>绍兴二十六年五月丁卯记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1220362_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年6月4日</a>　居归安。俞俟卒，有诗挽悼。作品：俞居易阁学二首。<div id='poem_529377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>俞居易阁学挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529377")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529377'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529377'>事业更中外，论思契冕旒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529377'>年虽濒钓渭，志不在封留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529377'>慈爱平生念，欢愉末路收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529377'>遥知谢公客，挥洒<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作泪）</span>过西州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529377'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529377_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529378?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月4日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529378'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529378'>奕世论交地，红花巷陌春<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：仆所居，旧称红花园。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529378'>扬雄一区宅，晏子百年邻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529378'>游倦归相踵，身闲意更亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529378'>那知从此别，老泪损天真<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《苕溪集》卷八）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529378'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　居归安。为钱观后妻徐氏作墓志铭。作品：徐氏安人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐氏安人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220396")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220396'>安人徐氏，世莆阳人，徙居吴郡，故尚书户部员外郎同郡钱君观复之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220396_comment'></div>时户部之亡也，安人命长子俣来吴兴，以户部遗意属铭于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220396_comment'></div>葬未几，俣再至拜且泣曰：「天不悔祸，吾母又弃诸孤，俣不即死者，以窀穸之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220396_comment'></div>今克葬矣，而铭未立，顾怜我而深悲之，且察吾母之素志而赐之以铭，匪公其孰赖」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220396_comment'></div>余心感焉，不敢以老且病为辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220396_comment'></div>安人讳温字德柔，曾祖真枢，故不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220396_comment'></div>祖模，赠正议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220396_comment'></div>父铎，熙宁中廷对魁天下士，仕至吏部尚书，赠少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220396_comment'></div>安人则少师之季女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220396_comment'></div>生有令姿，性识通敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220396_comment'></div>母吴国夫人莫氏知其非凡女子也，甚爱之，重于择对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220396_comment'></div>于时太师蔡鲁公于少师为同里，愿得安人为子妇，吴国辞焉，私语其子：「吾女当妻士人，终不与势家子以苟名位，尔等志之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220396_comment'></div>户部时为太学生，以上舍两优解褐，名声烨然，盖常拒势家之求姻者，或以安人闻，乃自喜，以为得所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220396_comment'></div>两家事适相契，乡里至今艳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220396_comment'></div>安人之归钱氏也，事舅如父，事姑如母，宗族内外，礼意周洽，被服简素，如寠人子，相夫必以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220396_comment'></div>户部佐州郡有能称，旁近有疑讼，久不决者往往委之，吏牍堆几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220396_comment'></div>安人尝戒左右，毋得以他事关白，俾之尽心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220396_comment'></div>或从旁赞决，言动得理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220396_comment'></div>前所舅朝议之葬，营奉久之不能具，或劝累甓代椁，安人曰：「不然，天或者见假，生理未泯，而追念今日之阙，虽悔何及」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220396_comment'></div>斥所御簪珥等鬻之以佐其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220396_comment'></div>户部感服，以为：「吾意亦及此，而不言者，恐汝难之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220396_comment'></div>其后赀费益窘，安人意虑精密，重以俭勤，寸积铢累，十有馀年，遂克成家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220396_comment'></div>叹曰：「吾有屋可居，有田可业，不啻足矣，尚何求」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220396_comment'></div>凡言利道者，皆谢弗听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220396_comment'></div>平居不妄费一钱，至宾祭馈遗不敢少简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220396_comment'></div>人以艰危见咨，未尝辄拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220396_comment'></div>闺阃事井井秩秩，不亟不徐，而人自祗率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220396_comment'></div>喜释氏学，治钟饭僧，崇饰佛像，费不可计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220396_comment'></div>阅贝叶书数千卷，晚有得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220396_comment'></div>绍兴二十六年六月十七日卒，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220396_comment'></div>诸孤以其年十月壬申葬于虞山之西，祔户部之兆，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220396_comment'></div>安人以户部升朝，遇郊祀恩封至安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220396_comment'></div>男四人，曰俣，左迪功郎，曰佃，从政郎，皆太学名士，相踵登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220396_comment'></div>曰佖、曰僩，业进士举，僩先夫人十月卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220396_comment'></div>女二人，适右迪功郎、监潭州合同茶场陈大年，左宣教郎、新筠州州学教授徐廷献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220396_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1220396'>呜呼安人志曷伟，率德蹈义佐君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220396_comment'></div>被服简素心不耻，肉视菜荠甘且美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220396_comment'></div>服勤于家岁其几，高门峥嵘雄我里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220396_comment'></div>郎君竞秀名煌炜，积金满籯不足喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220396_comment'></div>志业克就谁与比，为善之庆有如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220396_comment'></div>苍山同穴不踰礼，我谂之铭光女史。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1220396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年2月10日</a>　居归安。为居慧和尚《四会语录》作序。作品：慧和尚四会语录序。<div id='poem_1220341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慧和尚四会语录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年2月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220341")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220341'>师讳居慧，吴兴人，俗姓吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220341_comment'></div>早岁习天台教，已而更复入丛林，从甘露长灵卓公得道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220341_comment'></div>寻出世为人，阅四名刹，曰天圣、曰灵名山崇因、曰何山宣化、曰道场山护国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220341_comment'></div>既示寂，门人道枢集四会演畅语句成编，俾信士刊行散施，开悟后学，属余序之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220341_comment'></div>余尝谓释迦之亲付饮光，单传心印，不立文字，谓之教外别传，是不容声矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220341_comment'></div>然从上祖师一时言言流传世间，已既甚多，为有言耶，为无言耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220341_comment'></div>世尊良久，外道得入，既不在言语有无之间，亦不离言语有无之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220341_comment'></div>或曰，此有得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220341_comment'></div>则知从上祖师与师之心一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220341_comment'></div>师住道场最久，学徒四集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220341_comment'></div>观其与人处，倾囷倒廪，无所盖藏，老婆心且于是为至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220341_comment'></div>古德云「尽大地是解脱门，把手拽不入」，师意直欲出一只手，一时拽入耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220341_comment'></div>余恐得入者并门失之，是乃师之意也欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220341_comment'></div>绍兴二十七年二月十日，太简老人刘某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1220341_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　居归安。春，张元干从西湖至吴江，曾过湖州，未访，刘一止因而次韵。作品：张仲宗判监别近三十年经由馀不访余有诗次其韵。<div id='poem_529233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张仲宗判监别近三十年经由馀不访余有诗次其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529233")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529233'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529233'>乱前犹省当时事，乱后浑如隔世人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529233'>得见升平且欢喜，莫将心念到亨屯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529233'>衔杯倘办中山醉，觅句谁如小庾新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529233'>三十年前痴半<span class='inlineComment2'>（朱本作半痴）</span>黠，相逢终不忘天津。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529233'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年8月</a>　居归安。有跋南宫唱和诗后。<div id='poem_1220347' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220347' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220347?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋南宫唱和诗后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220347")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220347_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220347'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220347'>太仆公最先得诗名，后来宗英皆莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220347_comment'></div>计与东坡先生同官时，距今七十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220347_comment'></div>中间某居太学，不敢以姓名累典谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220347_comment'></div>晚乃得此卷轴于公之曾孙师醇，某年已八十矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220347_comment'></div>追前辈事，三叹而归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220347_comment'></div>绍兴丁丑八月上浣，吴兴刘某题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220347_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220347_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　居归安。为湖州德清县慈相院新钟作铭。作品：湖州德清县慈相院新钟铭。<div id='poem_1220368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州德清县慈相院新钟铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220368")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220368'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220368'>湖州德清县僧庐曰慈相，居县治之北，岩壑低昂之间，号为胜刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220368_comment'></div>冶铁为钟，有年数矣，器小声细，不足为是邑朝昏之儆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220368_comment'></div>院僧用琳始欲改作，而武康信士闻人誉施钱三十万以为观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220368_comment'></div>率范铜壶百三十三钧三分钧之一，求募辛苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220368_comment'></div>范成而琳亡，道俗悯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220368_comment'></div>越再岁，长老僧道或与其俦道殊、本立、怀仁、行辉惜功用之中废，悼前作之孔艰，合力经营，散募邑众，几用钱四百万，始克周备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220368_comment'></div>匠胡元美其名者，妙得于志，知名浙江，以绍兴二十八年八月丁巳一冶而就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220368_comment'></div>随叩响发，铿鍧雄浑，溢于四境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220368_comment'></div>观者叠足，巷无居人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220368_comment'></div>咸谓宜有款识，以诏来者，属同郡太简居士刘一止为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220368_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1220368'>我佛如来，方便微妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220368_comment'></div>考钟弗先，谓失枢要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220368_comment'></div>惟者祗园，具存典则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220368_comment'></div>大士圆通，多从闻入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220368_comment'></div>声彻幽途，咸息苦趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220368_comment'></div>问故以然，罪性空故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220368_comment'></div>佳哉妙工，一冶而就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220368_comment'></div>出以机轴，铿鍧随叩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220368_comment'></div>我愿闻者，了自闻闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220368_comment'></div>声念相发，于彼朝昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220368_comment'></div>六用既泯，返流得源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220368_comment'></div>是闻与声，俱满大千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220368_comment'></div>吁此气宝，作镇山邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220368_comment'></div>期亿万年，与宋无极<span class='inlineComment2'>（《苕溪集》卷二四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220368_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1220368'>者：似当作「昔」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1220368_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　居归安。为湖州德清县慈相院新钟作疏。作品：铸钟疏。<div id='poem_1220425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>铸钟疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220425")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220425'>黑业现前，冥途长夜，众生自息，罪性乃空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220425_comment'></div>惟钟声之远闻，发耳闻之深省，岂独脱苦趣于沈沦幽暗之域，抑将回净念于醉梦颠倒之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220425_comment'></div>此是藏教，苦口丁宁，只要檀那，甘心布施，共成兹事，幸弗失时。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1220425_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1160')">1159-1160年</a>　居归安。有题跋。作品：跋孙求仁运属梦记石刻后。赵陈都官墓芝亭石刻后。跋莫用之书藏经。题费校书被召书命轴后。<div id='poem_1220346' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220346' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220346?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋孙求仁运属梦记石刻后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年6月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220346")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220346_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220346'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220346'>求仁三岁而孤，又二岁丧所恃，寄养外家，世间可悲悯事，无越于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220346_comment'></div>当是时，人其谓我能自奋身，大其家风，种学绩文，为多缙绅，光贲泉壤，如今日之懿乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220346_comment'></div>成否有命，虽求仁亦不敢自必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220346_comment'></div>抑其先德有以见符，见于梦寐，殆诚孝所感发云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220346_comment'></div>绍兴二十九年六月辛丑，吴兴刘某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1220346_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题陈都官墓芝亭石刻后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220350")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220350'>某弱冠游太学，从师左间得前辈制科进卷读之，其题曰《太平有为策》者，盖贤良都官陈公之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220350_comment'></div>观其极论天下民物利疚，慷慨熟复，鄙心慕焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220350_comment'></div>今六十年矣，尚能记其髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220350_comment'></div>公以嘉祐四年召试贤良方正能直言极谏科，自秘阁至廷对，皆为第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220350_comment'></div>十馀年，始为越州山阴宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220350_comment'></div>上书论青苗事忤时相，一斥不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220350_comment'></div>公自谪废，便无仕进意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220350_comment'></div>当是时，诋新法得罪去朝者如中丞吕公讳诲、殿中侍御钱公讳顗、某伯祖杂端讳述，同时出国门，至南京饮酒三日而别，且相戒不复出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220350_comment'></div>公官卑又早世，士论悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220350_comment'></div>公之亡，盖某始生之年，独幸与其孙商彦俱为太学生，得公之文独多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220350_comment'></div>商彦以文学驰声庠序，士类推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220350_comment'></div>既仕宦，不苟进，怀抱怡然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220350_comment'></div>诏某曰：「我自得官，应迁转者并用考功格计岁月而升，未尝侥倖一日恩赏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220350_comment'></div>中间尝丞秘书，为显州之阶，已而补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220350_comment'></div>其忠节之高，不辱其祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220350_comment'></div>史臣称魏谟挺挺有烈祖风，余于商彦亦云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220350_comment'></div>芝亭之瑞，前诸公论之详矣，兹不徒言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220350_comment'></div>绍兴己卯六月丙午，刘某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220350_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋莫用之书藏经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220348")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220348'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220348'>同郡莫用之未老而请老，好閒而得閒，予甚喜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220348_comment'></div>久不得面，一日，持所书释氏藏典曰《宝积》、《华严》、《涅槃经》及《大智度论》等累四百五十馀卷，通为四十八函见示，以荐其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220348_comment'></div>又于报本禅院创修轮藏以贮此经，累岁而后办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220348_comment'></div>呜呼，亦良苦矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220348_comment'></div>予真为之喜，三叹而归之曰：用之于今，志愿已毕，真得閒矣，真得老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220348_comment'></div>绍兴二十九年七月丙戌，刘行简书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220348_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题费校书被召书命轴后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220349")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220349'>毗陵费懿恭校书之子错为归安丞，一日过余，出其先君同陈去非大参、张彦实舍人召对书命，于今三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220349_comment'></div>三君子皆一时名士，士之畏服者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220349_comment'></div>其后，陈、张二公位通显，懿恭仅居三馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220349_comment'></div>已而归隐锡山，再召不起，盖其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220349_comment'></div>世人以进退议得失，余以谓士各有志，亦有命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220349_comment'></div>苟遂其志，均为得也，何失之有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220349_comment'></div>独喜懿恭有子，能世其家，若相乘除云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220349_comment'></div>绍兴三十年正月，吴兴刘行简书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1220349_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。胡伋妻莫氏卒。刘一止应伋子沂之请为莫氏作墓志铭。作品：宋故太宜人莫氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故太宜人莫氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220397")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220397'>太宜人莫氏，会稽馀姚人，故赠右通直郎同邑胡君讳伋字浚明之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220397_comment'></div>曾祖某、祖某、父某，皆隐晦不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220397_comment'></div>太宜人自少小知书，浸长，作诗论文，如慧男子，女工之事，不学而能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220397_comment'></div>年三十始嫁，与其夫以文字相磨切，甚自乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220397_comment'></div>浚明负才气，谓富贵功名可以拾取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220397_comment'></div>初以乡书试礼部不偶，因肄业太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220397_comment'></div>阅三岁，归省其母宣夫人，寻奉母命成婚于莫，仅旬日，复如京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220397_comment'></div>太宜人不夺其志，每致书问，无恙外必以母养勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220397_comment'></div>既又龃龉，及慨然言归，辟馆舍，受乡党子弟之愿学者，躬自教授，或衣食之，太宜人实喜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220397_comment'></div>子二人，曰沂、曰汾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220397_comment'></div>方沂之在母也，太宜人夫妇危坐相对，多诵经史，用古人胎教之说，沂生而资性敏悟绝人，督教之甚严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220397_comment'></div>汾慕好亦如其兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220397_comment'></div>客过其门，闻诵读讲演之声，叹曰：「有是夫也，有是妇也，有是子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220397_comment'></div>沂未弱冠，试补太学，为选首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220397_comment'></div>绍兴五年中进士甲科，自是奉亲就养官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220397_comment'></div>二十八年，以沂为尚书郎，遇郊祀恩，封太安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220397_comment'></div>明年，显仁皇太后覃八十之庆，加今封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220397_comment'></div>三十年五月晦，以疾终，享年八十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220397_comment'></div>时沂为尚书户司员外郎兼国史院编修官、校中书门下省检正诸房公事，护丧既归，贻书乞铭于余，将以其年十二月壬申葬于邑之翁湖之原，祔浚明之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220397_comment'></div>建炎己酉，余尝学会稽，既终更，闻寇难越江浙，未知避地之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220397_comment'></div>外亲或告余距县三十里有胡氏，世业儒，兄弟好客急义，有贤称，盍往依焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220397_comment'></div>余舟楫至门，皆出望余舟迎，谓仆夫曰：「此教官刘姓者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220397_comment'></div>于是开其傍舍见授，凡饮食器用，纤悉备具，其至如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220397_comment'></div>余不自意恐惧流落中得此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220397_comment'></div>已而见太宜人于堂上，而余之室乃获朝夕从太宜人游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220397_comment'></div>见其勤俭有家法，奉祭祀，睦姻族，周人之急不少靳，谈人之善如己出，其所居之轩名曰「清净」，悉足以为法，每为余言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220397_comment'></div>其后浚明以其妹归余长子峦为姻家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220397_comment'></div>孙男七人，振、拱、挺、抑、抗、括、抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220397_comment'></div>孙女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220397_comment'></div>尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220397_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1220397'>侃侃宜人，行中轨则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220397_comment'></div>归嫔儒家，伉俪连璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220397_comment'></div>朝暮见闻，《诗》《书》《礼》《易》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220397_comment'></div>惟善之为，曾靡有忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220397_comment'></div>晚而就养，既寿既秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220397_comment'></div>夫岂人谋，阴报其必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220397_comment'></div>家山相望，墓木拱揖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220397_comment'></div>我谂之铭，州里是式。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1220397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　在归安。名所居为“太简斋”，有诗自抒怀抱。作品：太简斋即事二首。<div id='poem_529330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529330")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529330'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529330'>太简老人家似客，室中犹恨未空虚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529330'>筋挛步涩常须酒，日入中昏始废书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529330'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529330_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529331?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529331'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529331'>晓来人报雪遮门，委巷萧条郭似村。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529331'>自酌瓮醅能软饱，借人布被得奇温。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529331'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529331_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。赋诗小斋。作品：小斋即事二首。<div id='poem_84593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_84593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/84593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小斋即事二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_84593")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_84593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_84593'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_84593'>怜琴为弦直，爱棋因局方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_84593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_84593'>未用较得失，那能记宫商。<div id='poem_sentence_1_84593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_84593'>我老世愈疏，一拙万事妨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_84593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_84593'>惟此二物随，不系有兴亡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。赋诗小斋，自抒怀抱。作品：居士竂一首。<div id='poem_529263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>居士寮一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529263")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529263'>龙钟居士相，落魄宰官身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529263'>长史风吹帽，林宗雨垫巾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529263'>安心惟壁观，乞米赖僧邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529263'>曾并鸳行立，当时梦不真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529263'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529263_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。居家自赞。作品：又自赞。<div id='poem_529381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又自赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529381")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529381'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529381'>居闲无所乐，从仕无所愧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529381'>忽作此两言，自省过去事。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529381'>害性多矣晚乃安，苦心至矣晚乃甘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529381'>咄，我无初终得丧兮，又何乘除于其间。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_529381_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_529381'><span class='label'>按：</span>《苕溪集》卷二四。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_529381_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。次韵吴兴守见赠。作品：次韵吴兴守到官见贻一首。<div id='poem_529238' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529238' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529238")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529238_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529238'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529238'>步武初辞玉笋中，旌麾疑是到珠宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529238'>窗间岩岫如争<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作争如）</span>入，笔下云烟洗不空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529238'>千里喜深车后雨，一堂仁浃扇时风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529238'>宾筵浪许陪真赏，底用蹒跚一秃翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529238'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529238_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。次韵吴兴守雨中即事。作品：次韵吴兴守雨中即事一首。<div id='poem_529239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵吴兴守雨中即事一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529239")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529239_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529239'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529239'>雨槛风檐欲垫巾，护花常恐减青春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529239'>融怡已复生頩颊，料峭真应恕老人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529239'>睡鸭吹香空结恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作篆）</span>，远峰攒碧似凝颦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529239'>野棠泪湿愁如许，半面徐妃不受匀。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。次韵吴兴守抒怀。作品：次韵吴兴守春日抒怀。<div id='poem_529266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529266' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_529266'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529266'>百榼偿春酒，人言有别肠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529266'>披风醒午醉，撷蕊眷馀芳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529266'>白日何曾短，游丝得许长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529266'>向来情浩荡，今者<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作老）</span>梦微茫。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。送吴兴守诗十首。作品：送吴兴太守行十绝句。<div id='poem_529320' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529320' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_529321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529321'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529321'>海内文章说大门，故宜生长此儿孙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529321'>玉昆金友总秀出，历块过都不足论。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529321'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529321_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_529322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529322'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529322'>人言此邦公所私，教我子弟等父师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529322'>大书深刻岂足纪，愿奏宣布中和诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529323_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529323'>尔身在外心王室，咫尺应须入告猷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529323_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
