id='poem_sentence_0_529325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529325'>词剧清新过小庾，情多儿女笑张华。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529325'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529325_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_529326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529326'>此日偶同元凯癖，他年倘忆郑公乡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529326'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529326_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_529327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529327'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529327'>垂老何堪此别离，感公情义独心知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529327'>故应他日汀洲泪，独立难忘捩棹时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529327'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529327_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529328?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529328'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529328'>鸡皮鹤发病龙钟，误入林宗裁鉴中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529328'>平生气概今如此，自对青铜惜此侬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529328'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529328_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_529329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529329'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529329'>且尽离筵酒一杯，贵臣宁许我重陪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529329'>他时翊赞升平事，赋与林下歌康哉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。赋诗识舟亭。作品：识舟亭一首（渺渺归帆江北渚）<div id='poem_529078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>识舟亭一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529078")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529078'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529078'>渺渺归帆江北渚，脉脉相望那得语。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529078'>舟中贾客婵娟女，朝乐潇湘暮荆楚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529078'>我欲招之问计然，浮名唾去如飘烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529078'>买鱼沽酒啸俦侣，槌鼓弄笛凋残年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529078'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529078_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。湖州报恩光孝禅寺新建观音殿，为作记。作品：湖州报恩光孝禅寺新建观音殿记。<div id='poem_1220361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220361?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州报恩光孝禅寺新建观音殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220361")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220361'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220361'>湖州报恩光孝禅寺，在郡治东北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220361_comment'></div>地势亢爽，土木雄胜，门序殿舍，斋宫宿庐，规制井井，他伽蓝莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220361_comment'></div>盖陈永定中，后家舍宅建焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220361_comment'></div>初曰「龙兴」，后曰「孝义」，至唐复为「龙兴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220361_comment'></div>吴越钱氏易为「天宁」，以其女为比丘尼，遂为尼宫凡一百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220361_comment'></div>大朝崇宁二年，始复为十方禅刹，曰「崇宁万寿禅寺」，后又易「崇宁」为「天宁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220361_comment'></div>绍兴七年更赐今额，恭为固改，荐灵社也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220361_comment'></div>旧有观音大士像，在寺西偏两楹之间，郡人张氏病痿三年，一夕梦白衣女子告曰：「若臂不举耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220361_comment'></div>吾亦若此，若能拯我臂，吾亦拯若臂，且寿若矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220361_comment'></div>张问所居，则曰：「居天宁西廊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220361_comment'></div>翌日，张舆掖诣寺，得大士像如梦所睹，瞻仰感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220361_comment'></div>察大士右臂为坠木所伤，命工拯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220361_comment'></div>张病随愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220361_comment'></div>自是郡人归心，以疾痛苦见于求拯者，日不下数十，应感事迹，不可疏举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220361_comment'></div>而所处闇陋迮迫，不副人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220361_comment'></div>今道师居久与其徒慧智募众出财，谋建别殿奉安妙相，而患栋干之伟，求之山林，未易以日月冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220361_comment'></div>或告之曰：「近郊曰宝溪者有故侯第，今去弗居，盍往图之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220361_comment'></div>慧智亟往，则其家已先见梦告于其主，欣然许焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220361_comment'></div>于是廊庙之前左建殿屋四楹，前为复廊，与旁两庑，深明壮丽，具妙庄严，盖前住持经画累岁而不克成者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220361_comment'></div>道俗欢喜，竦踊赞叹，咸若有所依归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220361_comment'></div>久以其事求记于余，以侈其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220361_comment'></div>余曰：「吾闻观音大士，性相等空，无刹不现，身光互涉，有感必通，于诸众生，悲心不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220361_comment'></div>是故身为三十三应，因事摄化，利益见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220361_comment'></div>则我之身与子之身，一为比丘，一为居士，俱在三十三应之内，真源实济，视此大士为二为一，为同为别？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220361_comment'></div>以是思惟，大士众生，体本圆成，无二无别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220361_comment'></div>以无二无别，故随众生心想所感，周遍无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220361_comment'></div>则是大士非但无我，亦无我所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220361_comment'></div>而子独以象设区宇为所依归，则利益众生为有择欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220361_comment'></div>久曰：「不然，大士身相无边，固无我所，而彼信士心想乡慕，则有所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220361_comment'></div>我观道俗至前，摄衣俛伛，炷香膜拜，陈其疾痛苦死，种种希求之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220361_comment'></div>诚意所教，汗泚颜间，言出肺肝，感通梦寐，初若一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220361_comment'></div>我是以崇其向慕之所，为之庄严，以益其信心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220361_comment'></div>若彼信心一念回光，睹色明空，入佛知见，则知夫亡不起于座，周遍十方，在在处处，无非道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220361_comment'></div>而此道场实无所在，利益众生，亦无受者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220361_comment'></div>如我所说，为有择欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220361_comment'></div>为无择欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220361_comment'></div>如是问答，亦无实义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220361_comment'></div>余曰：「是名实义，是名大士，悲心救物，无二无别，子言似矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220361_comment'></div>是用识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220361_comment'></div>始于某年某月某甲子，成于某年某月某甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220361_comment'></div>后若干日，太简刘某居士记，并说偈言：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1220361'>我闻大士观世音，具大功德妙庄严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220361_comment'></div>初从闻中入三昧，闻空觉空空亦灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220361_comment'></div>惟有一念悲众生，三十三应为说法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220361_comment'></div>法施无尽身无边，周遍十方河沙土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220361_comment'></div>母陀罗臂如虚空，云何示此疾痛缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220361_comment'></div>以众生痛我亦痛，究观起灭无处所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220361_comment'></div>伟哉宝殿严睟容，清净绚丽光夺目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220361_comment'></div>惟导师久善方便，谓彼众生心想殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220361_comment'></div>要令睹想生实解，入佛知见如诸掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220361_comment'></div>在在处处皆道场，而此大士实无在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220361_comment'></div>一一众生蒙利益，亦无受此利益者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220361_comment'></div>我知信施及见闻，决定同證无上道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1220361_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　居归安。戏作。作品：任公子言其先君奉观音大士有感供果不枯而长太简居士刘某戏作此偈。<div id='poem_1220369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>任公子言其先君奉观音大士有感供果不枯而长太简居士刘某戏作此偈</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220369")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220369'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220369'>无根柢而生，不雨露而泽，是事云何，诚意感格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220369_comment'></div>当知世间，明暗空色，种种形相，从心地植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220369_comment'></div>我问公子，承谁恩力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220369_comment'></div>若个是空，若个是色？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220369_comment'></div>公子不言，一笑而答。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1220369_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年12月4日</a>　居归安。以疾终于家。<br /></div>
-----end

开封

DetailSwitch("a31ccd4c47564883b1c66b286b6a0a38");'><span id='a31ccd4c47564883b1c66b286b6a0a38_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　与邵子非同学，却于晚年才相识交游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1109')">1104-1109年</a>　在开封，游太学。<br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1115')">1112-1115年</a>　在开封，游太学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年7月12日</a>　在太学。连襟吴橐卒，刘一止有诗哭悼之。作品：哭吴亦虚一首。<div id='poem_529340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭吴亦虚一首<span class='inlineComment2'>（用方时敏韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年7月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529340")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529340'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529340'>髯吴少年日，轻车驾飞黄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529340'>授简千人中，风流蔼东梁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529340'>根植苦不牢，一朝陨清商。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529340'>谁者不归尽，我独哀此郎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529340'>人物秀且美，叔夜惭龙章。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529340'>眼看一抔土，瘗此白璧光。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529340'>空馀百篇诗，老语惊摧藏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529340'>孤儿将谁赖，门户如冰霜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529340'>我非山巨源，感念徒悲伤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529340'>恨墨慰九泉，别语尚微茫<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：亦虚临别，属余为铭。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529340'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_529340_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　在太学。为岳父臧询作行状。作品：臧记室行状。<div id='poem_1220370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220370?labeling=true' target='_blank'>臧记室行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220370")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220370'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220370'>曾祖、祖、父/公讳询，字公献，湖州安吉人，世居于梅溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220370_comment'></div>少孤，事母朱夫人以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220370_comment'></div>诸兄觅举，以公任家事，公意不怿，私取书读之，皆通其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220370_comment'></div>经理内外，不废孝养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220370_comment'></div>诸兄怜而教焉，始授之书，淹贯如老成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220370_comment'></div>未几肄业大学，声称籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220370_comment'></div>及元丰二年进士第，调歙州黟县尉，再调睦州桐庐县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220370_comment'></div>丁母夫人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220370_comment'></div>服除，朝廷以公元丰舍选，除汾州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220370_comment'></div>任满，改宣德郎、知淮阳军下邳县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220370_comment'></div>遇今上登极，转奉议郎，赐五品服，授签书广信军判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220370_comment'></div>未赴，时相荐公，有旨召对，除太仆寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220370_comment'></div>踰年，迁鸿胪丞，坐太仆误支马事免所居官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220370_comment'></div>更二年，始复除管勾元丰库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220370_comment'></div>明年，迁诸王府记室参军，中间序进，及经八宝赦恩至朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220370_comment'></div>大观四年冬以疾请致仕，卒于京师，享年六十，实十一月壬辰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220370_comment'></div>公性资警悟，筮仕不习文法，尝曰：「儒者安事三尺，顾理之所在何如耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220370_comment'></div>事无钜细，应声剖决，徐质以法，往往契合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220370_comment'></div>信道自将，不惮强贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220370_comment'></div>在桐庐时，使者行部，令而下敛板道左，使者在舆，仰视不降接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220370_comment'></div>公挽寮佐无得前揖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220370_comment'></div>使者怒，麇县事无所得，复阴遣吏伺公短，吏因缘扰民，公呼治之，以闻，使者心嘉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220370_comment'></div>县有兵官绳治卒伍差峻，东南卒素骄，至是衔怨连结，谋入县盗库兵为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220370_comment'></div>邑人大恐，告公，公曰：「宁有是事」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220370_comment'></div>翼日方揽讼牒，卒百馀辈联裾相属，骤至于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220370_comment'></div>左右股慄不自持，公若无睹，徐呼前曰：「而辈遽至庭下，顾令不揖，且无所言，岂令有负汝乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220370_comment'></div>皆曰：「令无负我，官兵实见虐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220370_comment'></div>公曰：「我以为令负汝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220370_comment'></div>若官兵见虐，令其为汝移半纸檄请于郡，即黜之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220370_comment'></div>且吾闻边陲士卒冒矢石、忍冻饿，至相腕藉以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220370_comment'></div>而辈寒则索裘，饥则命饷，父母妻子嬉怡在前，官家恩汝厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220370_comment'></div>吾恐汝不能有此逸乐，将自祸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220370_comment'></div>公反覆谕以祸福，卒众相视，解裾罗拜，既而犹偶语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220370_comment'></div>公谬为动其官状，及遣所亲阴白诸郡，郡识公意，即日檄兵官去，卒众遂解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220370_comment'></div>其后稍移易，离其谋党，得渠魁十馀人治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220370_comment'></div>邑人以谓非公机辩敏给，变在漏朝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220370_comment'></div>同寮有坐累去官者，累重不能归京师，至乞食于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220370_comment'></div>公闻之，出俸钱，并拉僚佐，得二十万，遣人访之，乃依古祠宇问方役人，丐百钱活旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220370_comment'></div>及得所赠，涕泗交下，贻书谢公，并致弓矢，且曰：「吾乞食寒陲，寄此为命者将数十年，以君能活我，故用为报」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220370_comment'></div>公反其弓而纳其矢焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220370_comment'></div>其周人之急类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220370_comment'></div>下邳郡民有所逋责之急，缢死田间者，其妻引富人为仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220370_comment'></div>公按问无状，即日出之，已而果谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220370_comment'></div>闻者叹伏，曰：「是公明可及也，果敢不可及也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220370_comment'></div>公家甚贫，持身益廉，收养孤甥及族党之贫不能婚姻者，以身任之无难色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220370_comment'></div>中间仕宦龃龉，困于京师，亲戚仰给有不安者，公喻曰：「业已托我，虽饮冰不相舍也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220370_comment'></div>与人交，握手出肺肝，了不见畦畛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220370_comment'></div>抵掌谈辩，杂以诙笑，听之衮衮，令人忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220370_comment'></div>得酒辄醉，万事都捐，便若超出世外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220370_comment'></div>其为文章不蹈袭前辈一语，落笔数千言，淹顷可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220370_comment'></div>尤喜为诗，辞藻雄丽，士大夫往往传诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220370_comment'></div>有文集十卷藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220370_comment'></div>公三娶，初许氏，封旌德县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220370_comment'></div>次舒氏，寿安县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220370_comment'></div>次裴氏，南华县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220370_comment'></div>一子宁，以公致仕，补将仕郎、明州奉化县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220370_comment'></div>二女，长适将仕郎、江宁府上元县尉吴橐，次适从政郎刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220370_comment'></div>孙男一人曰协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220370_comment'></div>宁以明年某月某日葬公于某县某乡某山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220370_comment'></div>既葬五年而宁卒，协以宁命，属某状公之行，将丐名于一时钜公，且表之墓上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220370_comment'></div>呜呼，以公之器业宏远，不大用于世，而蹭蹬以死，岂命也夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220370_comment'></div>异时执政盖有知之者，且将峻擢，公出语劲直，不能委曲伺人意，用是中辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220370_comment'></div>尝曰：「吾以胸中介介者与言语文字卜知，干人则是非所能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220370_comment'></div>幸见用，敢不勉，不然姑已耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220370_comment'></div>呜呼，其贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220370_comment'></div>谨叙其事如左，以俟择采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220370_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1220370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　在太学。上书卢襄。作品：寄提刑卢察院书。<div id='poem_1220294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄提刑卢察院书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220294")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220294'>吴兴进士刘某再拜上书提刑察院阁下：某闻天下之物不可以私求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220294_comment'></div>非不可求也，求之实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220294_comment'></div>岂其物之理然哉，抑造物者不与其私也而阴夺之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220294_comment'></div>是何言也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220294_comment'></div>某无似，生长于世，三十有九年矣，自少小读书，求为古人之事业盖甚笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220294_comment'></div>齿浸长，身名不列于搢绅，而学为科举之文，与韦布士群试有司，决是非于蒙昧之中，亦幸其有得，亦可谓求之公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220294_comment'></div>然名六上于春官，一宾兴于学校，卒不得志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220294_comment'></div>乃退而思之，凡某所谓科举之文，率不量力，务为表表异众者，为诡窃声称之计，抑私也，造物者弗与也，又何怪乎不得其求也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220294_comment'></div>于是始作而叹曰：物之不可以私取，果如是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220294_comment'></div>今则已矣，不复有求于世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220294_comment'></div>然宿习馀气，有不可远遣者，独惓惓于言辞文字之间，而求其嗜好之合者而折衷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220294_comment'></div>譬诸草木，吾之臭味也，则往而求之，以益其所未闻，信其所已得，且将乐此以终其身，富贵声名之慕不存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220294_comment'></div>然则某之所求，亦可谓易与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220294_comment'></div>怀此以行于世，既有年于兹，闾巷之士，其穷似己，可得而友者固少，而先达富贵某之愿慕而请事者又无阶而进焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220294_comment'></div>则又退而思之，我之于人，不求于天下之同，而求于嗜好之独，抑私也，造物者弗与也，又何怪乎不得其求也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220294_comment'></div>虽然，某之自疑若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220294_comment'></div>观今天下之士，驰骋衒鬻，达于观而敏于望者，小足以钓声名，大足以致爵位，身名泰然，意气横出，视造物者如可自措气使，其定计岂尽出于公耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220294_comment'></div>而某之区区，乃独私于言语文字之间，与彼之所争不同辙也，造物者又夺之，不已甚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220294_comment'></div>是以忘其所自疑，而不知止焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220294_comment'></div>某故岁闻诸士大夫，东浙有隽人曰毛曰冯，与执事而三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220294_comment'></div>异时获识二公于京师，独不得一望执事之数，窃以为恨，而得二其文于科举，固已超绝时辈，足以信其所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220294_comment'></div>然犹未也，去岁客虽旬，又得执事一二诗文于宗族兄弟间，一读心醉，不自知神忽忽而若驰，足踆踆而欲进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220294_comment'></div>未几，闻执事以御史出领外台，某窃自计倘得以私愿请于门下，是天假其便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220294_comment'></div>日者执事按临敝邑，又属有负薪之疾，不得造前，益自怅恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220294_comment'></div>然某之愿慕求进若不及者，诚觊执事察其私而辱教之，进其未能，信其所疑，而归之于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220294_comment'></div>然执事以文章道义公天下，至则受之，又何私之有哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220294_comment'></div>而某之私则在是，不识傥与之进乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220294_comment'></div>如其不然，是造物者真夺之矣，不复望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220294_comment'></div>故先以是说卜焉，庶几执事他日不以其无谓而来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220294_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1220294_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1119')">1117-1119年</a>　在开封，游太学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在开封，入太学上舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在开封，有诗赠别归安周县丞。作品：赠别归安周县丞二首。<div id='poem_529101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠别归安周县丞二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529101")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529101'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529101'>自我居里间，连墙绝未去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529101'>非我敢杜门，客实莫我顾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529101'>颓然坐空庐，习懒已成痼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529101'>惟有一束书，遮眼慰迟暮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529101'>周郎来何许，文字得我怖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529101'>渊源笑鲵桓，采色隐豹雾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529101'>追随古河<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作汀）</span>洲，山色入幽步。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529101'>诗文互徵逐，酒鸾及时具。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529101'>如我众弃馀，君意独何慕。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529101'>入兰不<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作室）</span>知芳，逐臭无乃误。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529101'>君亦忘机人，足迹乱鸥鹭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529101'>堂前种白莲，心境涵净土。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529101'>观空本无说，因<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作目）</span>物自吐露。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529101'>往来忘时节，相对两如寓。<div id='poem_sentence_13_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_529101'>屈指说去官，始忆三年住。<div id='poem_sentence_14_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_529101'>冁然同一笑，岁月真脱兔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_529101'>我不记前三，更问末后句。<div id='poem_sentence_16_529101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_529101'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_529101_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529102?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529102'>庭前百个竹，眼见三陨箨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529102'>不知如许久，已复东<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作束）</span>行橐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529102'>君初无<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作先）</span>住想，脱<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作晚）</span>去亦不恶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529102'>官身等出家，随牒即行脚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529102'>笑傲云烟间，何适非至乐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529102'>嗟我独奈何，生理自窘缚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529102'>四十三年非，酝造此大错。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529102'>从今便上上，万事付莫莫。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529102'>张公留衣钵，绿蓑与青箬。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529102'>会当老扁舟，相与同啐啄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529102'>更看后五日，放过前一著。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529102'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_529102_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在开封，进士及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在开封，登第后，监秀州都酒务，不卑其官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在开封，出仕后，尝拜谒姨母于堂上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在开封，刘一止有诗赠和何薳，自嘲已老。作品：五十少公卿赠何子楚居士。<div id='poem_529155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五十少公卿赠何子楚居士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529155")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529155'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529155'>五十少公卿，三十老举子。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529155'>世间老与少，不必较年齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529155'>我观宦达人，颜色自丰美。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529155'>癯者忽易腴，变化一日耳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529155'>人言老再少，信是有此理。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529155'>我为老诸生，流落逾二纪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529155'>四十又过四，淟涊百僚底。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529155'>说老已十年，何况真老矣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529155'>壮气推<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作摧）</span>幽忧，发白面目缁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529155'>宁有再少时，一衰乃如此。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529155'>何郎穷过我，齿发亦相似。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529155'>闲居傲轩裳，臞腹满经史。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529155'>时时吐光焰，丽句落窗几。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529155'>谁家肯终惠，试此足千里。<div id='poem_sentence_13_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_529155'>空令坐穷独，阁户今扫轨。<div id='poem_sentence_14_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_529155'>宦达世共慕，闲旷我所喜。<div id='poem_sentence_15_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_529155'>丈夫生世间，要自发奇伟。<div id='poem_sentence_16_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_529155'>富贵何足云，功名半张纸。<div id='poem_sentence_17_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_529155'>古来傲世士，良是穷乃止。<div id='poem_sentence_18_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_529155'>未有如子年，忼慨隐廛市。<div id='poem_sentence_19_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_529155'>我不愧公卿，愧此少居士。<div id='poem_sentence_20_529155_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_529155'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_529155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在开封，有诗赠葛胜仲。作品：次韵维心赠葛鲁卿待制求花栽一首。葛鲁卿待制二首。<div id='poem_529220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529220?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵维心赠葛鲁卿待制求花栽一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529220")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529220_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529220'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529220'>此日宁无健步移，春前行近着花时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529220'>故园乐地今馀几，小县风光客不知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529220'>剩买名裁令乱眼，却嫌芳思只撩诗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529220'>属公归赋丹青手，问圃寻农独我宜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529220'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529220_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>葛鲁卿待制挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529365")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529365'>先皇隆教育，师席重朝绅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529365'>模楷归元礼，纷纶仰大春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529365'>壮图初未究，归意久逾真。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529365'>丘壑平生事，何人得此身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529366?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529366'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529366'>论议超今昔，文章适典彝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529366'>老成嗟已远，后学欲谁师。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529366'>封域南阳旧，交亲北陌悲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529366'>他年门弟子，下马识丰碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529366'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529366_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
嘉兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3776cd3bcc554ec7b57a2cb0850a0c2d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3776cd3bcc554ec7b57a2cb0850a0c2d");'><span id='3776cd3bcc554ec7b57a2cb0850a0c2d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1123')">1122-1123年</a>，45-46岁</div><div id='3776cd3bcc554ec7b57a2cb0850a0c2d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　任秀州监酒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年1月15日</a>　元夕，在秀州有词。作品：醉蓬莱（正官桥柳润）<div id='poem_84634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_84634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/84634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>醉蓬莱 秀城元夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_84634")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_84634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_84634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_84634'>正官桥柳润，候馆梅开，暮云凄冽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_84634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_84634'>泽国春归，是烧灯时节。<div id='poem_sentence_1_84634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_84634'>吹绽红蕖，挽低星斗，共水光澄澈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_84634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_84634'>霜瓦楼台，参差似与，蓬壶相接。<div id='poem_sentence_3_84634_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_84634'>千骑遨游，万家嬉笑，帘卷东风，弄妆成列。<div id='poem_sentence_4_84634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_84634'>慢舞尊前，看轻盈回雪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_84634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_84634'>来岁今宵，舜韶声里，对六鳌双阙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_84634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_84634'>凤检飞来，玉骢去踏，青门华月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_84634_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在秀州，上书蔡嶷。作品：见经制使书。<div id='poem_1220292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>见经制使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220292")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220292'>迪功郎、监秀州在城都酒务刘某，谨再拜上书经制龙学阁下：某尝谓天之生才，地之生材，一也，不中道夭于斧斤，未有不堪于用者，非必邓林数寻之栝柏、千尺之豫章，然后为材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220292_comment'></div>凡可以为杗为栋，为欂栌侏儒者，皆材也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220292_comment'></div>夫才亦然，不中道夭于聋盲跛蹇，则亦恶有无用于世者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220292_comment'></div>然其命则寄于匠氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220292_comment'></div>所谓匠氏者，以规矩为方圆，以绳墨为曲直，定规矩绳墨于器量大小长短，而用之无废材者，天下之良工巧匠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220292_comment'></div>以道义为规矩，以行艺为绳墨，量大小长短而用之无废材者，天下之宗工大匠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220292_comment'></div>然则材与才者皆不可无所归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220292_comment'></div>虽不可无所归，亦不可不审其所归，何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220292_comment'></div>力之所任，质之所处，有衡纵燥湿之殊，宜纵而衡任之，宜燥而湿处之，则所任所处皆不得久焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220292_comment'></div>物固有不幸失其所者，此其所以为寄命于匠氏，则非特匠氏择材也，材固有择匠氏之理矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220292_comment'></div>虽然，何世而无才，何地而不生材，其轮囷离奇，弃委于道傍，槁死于岩壑，而不见录用者，盖十五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220292_comment'></div>幸见用，则听其所为而已，又恶能有择于其间哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220292_comment'></div>是不然，天下无真匠师则已，使诚有之，亦无恶于物之择己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220292_comment'></div>至于有择焉而不见录，则抑有命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220292_comment'></div>窃惟阁下受真主之知，当数路之寄，器使职官，黜陟能否，居宰相之功半，于兹再岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220292_comment'></div>进则成规，退则成矩，若与人而为谋，左以画方，右以画圆，盖以心而为匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220292_comment'></div>凡其人之才，所谓大小长短，孰处孰任，未有能以形逃者，阁下之规矩绳墨，诚先定于心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220292_comment'></div>今有人焉，读圣贤之书，求为古人之事，气盖甚笃，淟涊学校，周旋二纪，而始得寸禄，行年四十有五矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220292_comment'></div>其所事则糟浆曲蘖，瓮盎薪米之间，铢争而籥计，自旦暮与屠沽小人为敌雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220292_comment'></div>虽食其食，不敢忘其事，然非其性之所能，则谓失其所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220292_comment'></div>昔者强，今者惫，昔者腴，今者瘠，岂端使然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220292_comment'></div>呜呼，其亦可怜也已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220292_comment'></div>某窃自思念，生长于世，幸未至聋盲跛蹇，而其心事曲折，粗能裨大贤君子之忽忽忘者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220292_comment'></div>今遇匠师，而不能自窜于规矩绳墨之间，尚安往而可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220292_comment'></div>某虽小物，盖知审所择矣，独未知阁下能无恶于物之择己，且哀其情而受之否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220292_comment'></div>若其大小长短与所处所任，则某不能知也，知归焉而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220292_comment'></div>至于求归焉而不得，则是真有命焉，某也敢不知命？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220292_comment'></div>干冒台严，不胜悚惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220292_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1220292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年3月</a>　刘一止在秀州有词赠路允迪出使高丽。作品：望明河(华旌耀日)<div id='poem_84620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_84620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/84620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望明河 赠路侍郎使高丽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_84620")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_84620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_84620'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_84620'>华旌耀日，报天上使星，初辞金阙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_84620'>许国精忠，试此日傅岩，济川舟楫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_84620'>向来鸡林外，况传咏、篇章雄绝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_84620'>问人地、真是唐朝第一，未论勋业。<div id='poem_sentence_3_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_84620'>鲸波霁云千叠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_84620'>望仙驭缥缈，神山明灭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_84620'>万里勤劳，也等是壮年，绣衣持节。<div id='poem_sentence_6_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_84620'>丈夫功名事，未肯向、尊前伤轻别。<div id='poem_sentence_7_84620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_84620'>看飞棹、归侍宸游，宴赏太平风月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_84620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在秀州，有上侍郎书。作品：见国信侍郎书。<div id='poem_1220296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>见国信侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220296")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220296'>迪功郎、监秀州在城都酒务刘某，再拜上书国信侍郎阁下：某观之，士之怀才抱艺而不见试用，犹病痒者而钳其肘，假人之爬搔以为快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220296_comment'></div>至其甚者，若心腹之有隐痛，非但假人以为快而已，将旦暮大其声而疾呼，且祈人之哀己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220296_comment'></div>以韩子之贤，宜为一世所归重，方且自荐于时宰，至于再上书而不通，三及门而不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220296_comment'></div>其说以谓，古之士重于自进者，以其于周不可则去之于鲁，于鲁不可则去之于齐，于齐不可则去之宋之郑之秦之楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220296_comment'></div>今天下一君，四海一国，舍乎此则夷狄矣，去父母之邦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220296_comment'></div>呜呼，其辞亦可谓切矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220296_comment'></div>某尝哂之，所谓士者读古人之书，行古人之道，用则进，不用则退，用固可喜，不用何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220296_comment'></div>虽天下一君，四海一国，非若战国之士，可以出彼而入此，然为天子进退人才者，宜非一人也，执政大臣、两禁要近，皆可以荐贤于天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220296_comment'></div>顾己之所挟，诚足取知于人而用于世，会当有所归，不得于甲则得于乙，不得于乙则得于丙，与之宋之郑之秦之楚何有异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220296_comment'></div>若皆无所合，则有命焉，何至汲汲自售，号呼乞怜，若是其切耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220296_comment'></div>持此以阅人，盖有年于兹，非特其身之不有合也，又深计而熟思之，然后知今之士与战国之士异者，抑其操术不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220296_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220296_comment'></div>战国之士以诡谲权变取世资，俯吊仰贺，朝合暮离，饰人之心，易人之虑，非秦之衡人则赵之从长也，非谈天衍则雕龙奭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220296_comment'></div>甚是视富贵可唾手取，虽受辱不耻，曰：「吾舌在，足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220296_comment'></div>商鞅以帝王霸道干其君，而世谓之以三术钻孝公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220296_comment'></div>彼三术者何术也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220296_comment'></div>究其用心，乃今市道之人类能之，曰傲、惑、佞是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220296_comment'></div>以秦孝公而告之帝道，是傲之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220296_comment'></div>及其不合，则更说以王道，夫孝公之志岂在是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220296_comment'></div>抑帝王之道何择焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220296_comment'></div>是惑之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220296_comment'></div>至于末说于霸道，则佞而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220296_comment'></div>前者之不合，知后者之必合也，盖侈其说以要其君，蕲信用之笃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220296_comment'></div>今士以君子之道律其身，以仁义忠信之说加乎人，而曰「我必有合」，吾知其不可冀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220296_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220296_comment'></div>遇合诚难，而操术未易用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220296_comment'></div>脱或遇其人，有其时，是安得不恢恢于求售？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220296_comment'></div>以韩子之贤，而上书自荐，类于祈哀，无足深怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220296_comment'></div>某吴兴晚生，行年四十有六，连遭于趋进之途，徬徨于寂寞之滨，不可谓不久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220296_comment'></div>挟其术以行于世，每举而每不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220296_comment'></div>尝窃自念，遭盛治之世，非若战国之士可以出入宋齐梁楚之间，又不能用商鞅之术以肆其诡谲权变之说，又受辱不能不耻，而独有意乎以君子之道、仁义忠信之说，侥幸万有一者之合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220296_comment'></div>呜呼，其亦可谓不知量矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220296_comment'></div>然而不能自已者，亦岂有待乎哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220296_comment'></div>某故岁居学校，服阁下重望，而诵记其文，以为矜式，非一日，与其操履论议，得之缙绅之间为加详，而某之定计求归焉者抑审矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220296_comment'></div>特门墙之阻，邈在天上，曾不得趑趄其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220296_comment'></div>乃者阁下以使事道二浙，某始作而言曰：是行也，归当复于吾君，则必以人才为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220296_comment'></div>此韩子自荐之时也，天其假余便哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220296_comment'></div>书不必再上，足不必三及门，一见于此决矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220296_comment'></div>遇也有命，抑自信其操术果足以求合也，今遭其时，遇其人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220296_comment'></div>否亦有命，抑自悔其闻见之陋，不足以取知于大君子之门也，今遭其时、遇其人，而失之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220296_comment'></div>二者非某之所敢必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220296_comment'></div>谨录所为近诗杂文一编，藉手以见，惟阁下进退之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220296_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1220296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在秀州期间，尝有代秀守首文。作品：代秀守请交代致语。<div id='poem_1220464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代秀守请交代致语</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220464")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220464'>楼船飞下，暂遣北阙之星辰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220464_comment'></div>瑞节初临，增焕南州之风景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220464_comment'></div>欢声在路，和气生春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220464_comment'></div>恭惟知府某官川岳英姿，圭璋粹质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220464_comment'></div>绣衣持斧，荐更使驿之光华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220464_comment'></div>锦帐握兰，夙著丹墀之闻望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220464_comment'></div>谓持荷之下远，始剖竹以均劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220464_comment'></div>特借经行，少劳坐镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220464_comment'></div>一方濡槁，共知甘雨之随车；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220464_comment'></div>千里嘘枯，已觉仁风之在扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220464_comment'></div>知府某官恭迎旌旆，喜接清光，情深契阔之私，义重夜承之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220464_comment'></div>愿尽举觞之礼，少延挥麈之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220464_comment'></div>某等不揆荒芜，上献口号：楼船叠鼓破烟轻，欣见儿童竹马迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220464_comment'></div>锦帐握兰乘宠眷，绣衣持斧茂威声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220464_comment'></div>共知甘雨随车到，已觉仁风逐扇行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220464_comment'></div>自是玉皇香案吏，肯容萧散寄江城。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1220464_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在秀州期间，尝有代贺启。作品：代贺秀州通判启。<div id='poem_1220319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220319?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺秀州通判启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220319")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220319_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220319'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220319'>伏审祗膺明命，出贰使藩，理楫戒途，蠲辰视印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220319_comment'></div>伏惟某官器全英特，识洞几微，论议得于心成，事业由于世济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220319_comment'></div>休有闻誉，见于践更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220319_comment'></div>谓宜揖逊于熙朝，尚尔驰驱于别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220319_comment'></div>昔者大郑小郑公以父子继治，大冯小冯君以兄弟相循，并载民谣，号为盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220319_comment'></div>今见二难之步武，未踰三载之星霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220319_comment'></div>岂惟人望之知归，抑想风流之是似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220319_comment'></div>某江湖寒族，天地畸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220319_comment'></div>侵寻五十之年，老之将至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220319_comment'></div>淟涊百寮之底，拙亦宜然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220319_comment'></div>窃有所依，敢后其喜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220319_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4ce8c0917ad14af98dfaa8a4599ec0a8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ce8c0917ad14af98dfaa8a4599ec0a8");'><span id='4ce8c0917ad14af98dfaa8a4599ec0a8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1127')">1124-1127年</a>，47-50岁</div><div id='4ce8c0917ad14af98dfaa8a4599ec0a8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　迁越州州学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　在会稽，上书宇文粹中。作品：上执政书。<div id='poem_1220293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上执政书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220293")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220293'>从政郎、新差充越州州学教授刘某，再拜上书尚书右丞阁下：某尝谓遇合之难，古今所同，非直其得之难也，得其心之所趋乡而归焉者为尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220293_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220293_comment'></div>宰相大臣，以进贤退不肖为职事之求归焉者也，然有其实者辞其名，崇其名者或忘其实，故士有幸不幸，其幸焉者得其归，又得其心之所趋乡，而不流于非义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220293_comment'></div>其不幸则反是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220293_comment'></div>昔公孙丞相号为好士，起客馆，开东阁，以收贤俊，而曾不知所收者何士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220293_comment'></div>当是时，如主父偃辈宜在翘材之列矣，顾弃不取，又谮杀之，迁董仲舒胶西，皆丞相力，然则丞相所收，其无乃宾客故人而已耶，若夫收贤则未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220293_comment'></div>偃不见收于丞相，而卫将军乃荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220293_comment'></div>且卫将军何为者，而能知偃耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220293_comment'></div>偃之遇丞相而从将军，固不系幸不幸，要非求用之本心焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220293_comment'></div>柳宗元、刘禹锡一时之杰，而附离匪人以进，在清议所不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220293_comment'></div>然当是时，丞相如杜佑盖尝延集士类制《通典》，而二子乃不在顾盼中，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220293_comment'></div>呜呼，士之抱负志业而不见试用，假人之力以推挽之，其有甚于焚溺者之求拯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220293_comment'></div>不幸不为当世显人所录用，则往往汩丧廉耻，为不义之归，身负恶名，若腹心之抱痈疽，首领之婴木索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220293_comment'></div>呜呼，亦岂其初心然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220293_comment'></div>故曰：得其心之所趋乡而归焉者为尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220293_comment'></div>某为太学生逾二十年，仰阁下道德，读其书与窃听其论议非一日矣，盖自昔者以古人之事望阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220293_comment'></div>独愚不肖，无以自奋发而取知当世大君子之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220293_comment'></div>今老矣，犹喋喋然动其心，亦何为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220293_comment'></div>朅来京师，问诸贤缙绅，皆曰天下利疚，人才升黜，赖阁下与一二公力持风裁，尽踞弊习，且闵闵焉有忧国爱民之心，士之欲伸其说而求其归者莫先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220293_comment'></div>盖闻之审矣，于是叹阁下真能为古人之事，而不负其所学者也，士归焉而得其所趋乡者也，有其实而辞其名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220293_comment'></div>某虽愚且老，亦恶能无意于斯时哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220293_comment'></div>惟阁下稍进之，赐之坐语，顾心事曲折，岂无以裨执事万一者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220293_comment'></div>谨并录旧所为诗若干首，藉手以见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220293_comment'></div>惟是逆旅手自缮写，不能谨好，辱赐览观，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220293_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1220293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　在会稽，有诗送陈商彦。作品：览镜一首。<div id='poem_529262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>览镜一首<span class='inlineComment2'>（寄陈商彦秘丞）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529262")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529262_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529262'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529262'>契阔三年梦，飘零一寸心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529262'>青青今变雪，种种仅齐簪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529262'>览镜浑相似，弹冠各不任。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529262'>论交如许酒，情寄一杯深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529262'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529262_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　在会稽，有诗次韵刘焘。作品：次韵寄酬无言兄颁政二章。<div id='poem_529098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵寄酬无言兄颁政二章<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529098")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529098'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529098'>凤不出丹穴，姬孔叹且思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529098'>忽来乃为时，不计身安危。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529098'>采色炫世眼<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作服）</span>，鸣声漏天机。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529098'>高梧寄孤巢，俯仰反自悲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529098'>矧复鴳雀俦，妒喘如筒吹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529098'>我知盛名下，忧惙甚井眉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529098'>宠辱更事耳，何异秦晋饥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529098'>生身等<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作寄）</span>世间，宁免相贷资。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529098'>公乎岂人谋，天特相兹时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529098'>奈何不自量，径欲力撼之。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529098'>如我实助喜，良是昔所期。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529098'>蜀笺冰不如，忽枉洒兰辞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529098'>三复重太息，无术可肉飞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529098'>要看<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作安着）</span>笔如椽，涂<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作空）</span>改生民诗。<div id='poem_sentence_13_529098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_529098'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_529098_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529099?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529099'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529099'>自公之出矣，岂不旦夕思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529099'>人情剧险艰，太行未足危。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529099'>十年江湖心，鸥鸟识忘机。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529099'>却来鹓鹭行，方寸交喜悲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529099'>晚被天语温，习如和风吹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529099'>凡公宿昔交，谁不胜两眉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529099'>如我故陆沈，笔耕遇比<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：音频。）</span>饥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529099'>胸腹抱介介，何以取世资。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529099'>时哉今唐虞，不出斯无时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529099'>苕之水洋洋，我饥实乐之。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529099'>如何磊落人，颇复误见期。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529099'>谁能叩人门，受彼在亡辞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529099'>吸饮风露寒，身轻会<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作令）</span>孤飞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529099'>明时自嗟拙，敢赋衡门诗。<div id='poem_sentence_13_529099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_529099'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_529099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　在会稽，有诗次韵刘焘卜筑。作品：次韵无言兄卜筑二首。<div id='poem_529231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵无言兄卜筑二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529231")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529231'>求田问舍岂徒为，晚悟前言不我欺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529231'>地占玉杯初应卜，门临苕水宛分枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529231'>乡关怪客归何早，圣主思贤降<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作出）</span>不迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529231'>磊落胸中三万字，不应无意拯时危。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529231'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529231_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529232?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529232'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529232'>石枕方床绿浪藤，清谈散带似怀冰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529232'>蔬盘尚杂水中蟹，羽翣莫挥瓜上蝇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529232'>五斗为贫真世业，一廛归隐岂人能。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529232'>冥鸿万里今何慕，应笑饥飞侧翅鹰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529232'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529232_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在会稽，有训导之文。作品：下武。立政。说命下。<div id='poem_1220355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>下武讲义</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220355")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220355'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220355'>经纬天地曰文，文所以立德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220355_comment'></div>戡定祸乱曰武，武所以济功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220355_comment'></div>以武继文者，以功济德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220355_comment'></div>周家之兴，太王肇基王迹，王季其勤王家，文王克成厥勋，非无功也，以德为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220355_comment'></div>武王于此，将以昭三后之功，顾必有圣德，然后能集天命，则功不期昭而昭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220355_comment'></div>《大明》之诗曰「文王有明德」，故天复命武王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220355_comment'></div>此诗曰：「武王有圣德，复受天命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220355_comment'></div>然则天命所在，在兹德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220355_comment'></div>所谓德者，宜若在我，而诗以谓天之复命武王，乃自于文王之有明德，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220355_comment'></div>盖天方授周，则世有哲王以相缵述，克就大业，岂人之所能为哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220355_comment'></div>诗曰：「笃生武王，保佑命尔，燮伐大商」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220355_comment'></div>推本言之，则武王之能昭先人之功也，抑天而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220355_comment'></div>哲者知之，加乎人主所为，不如是，不足以昭德塞违，临昭百官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220355_comment'></div>先王以是造始，后王以是续终，故曰「下武维周，世有哲王」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220355_comment'></div>《书》曰：「兹商多先哲王在天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220355_comment'></div>所谓在天，言其神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220355_comment'></div>于三后言在天，则知武王所以配之者以圣德而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220355_comment'></div>惟武为足以继三后之文，惟圣为足以配在天之神，故曰「三后在天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220355_comment'></div>诗言「命此文王，于周于京」，则天为将命文王君天下于周京之地，武王之作镐京，于是配行其德焉，故曰「王配于京」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220355_comment'></div>夫孝者善继人之志，善述人之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220355_comment'></div>曰「世德作求」者，盖作而求先王之欲，善继志者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220355_comment'></div>曰「昭哉嗣服」，善述事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220355_comment'></div>《书》曰：「其在四方，用丕式见德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220355_comment'></div>《老子》曰：「常德不式，为天下式」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220355_comment'></div>君人者孰不欲天下之丕式哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220355_comment'></div>上无以配天命，则下无以立信于民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220355_comment'></div>下无以立信于民，则欲其式之也难矣，故曰：「永言配命，成王之孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220355_comment'></div>成王之孚，下土之式」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220355_comment'></div>孝子不过乎物所谓则者，性之物则而已，故曰：「永言孝思，孝思维则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220355_comment'></div>曰「媚兹一人」，则道足以媚上下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220355_comment'></div>曰「应侯顺德」，则德足以应民物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220355_comment'></div>《易》曰：「天之所助者顺也，人之所助者信也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220355_comment'></div>履信思乎顺，是以上天佑之，武王所以得天人之助者，以此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220355_comment'></div>夫然，故百姓与能，而天降之福焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220355_comment'></div>非徒与之，又将来贺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220355_comment'></div>非徒贺之，又将奔走而佐助之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220355_comment'></div>曰「昭兹来许」，则许其能昭先人之功焉，百姓与能者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220355_comment'></div>曰「于万斯年，受天之祜」，天降之福者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220355_comment'></div>曰「受天之祜，四方来贺」，非徒与之，又将来贺者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220355_comment'></div>曰「于万斯年，不遐有佐」，非徒贺之，又将奔走而佐助之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220355_comment'></div>《孟子》曰：「得道者多助，失道者寡助」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220355_comment'></div>多助之至，天下顺之，况其近者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220355_comment'></div>寡助之至，亲戚畔之，况其远者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220355_comment'></div>呜呼，昭先人之功至于四方奔走而佐助之，斯真有道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220355_comment'></div>验于《诗》《书》，以四方则无思不服，以诸侯则不期而会，鹰扬之师起于渭滨，献獒之贡及于西旅，微卢彭濮称戈而辅，九夷八蛮通道而至，侯卫骏奔而奉祀，巢伯来朝而向方，则其奔走来佐可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220355_comment'></div>窃尝原诗之意，所以臻此，有两言焉，哲见于外，孝存诸内而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220355_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220355_comment'></div>自昔创业守文之君，未有不本于哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220355_comment'></div>世有哲王，非特周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220355_comment'></div>《酒诰》曰：「在昔商先哲王，迪畏天显小民，经德秉哲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220355_comment'></div>《无逸》曰：「自商王中宗及高宗及祖甲，及我周文王，兹四人迪哲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220355_comment'></div>然则其来尚矣，于此欲以昭先人之功，顾非哲不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220355_comment'></div>《中庸》曰：「武王其达孝矣乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220355_comment'></div>又曰：「武王缵太王、王季、文王之绪，壹戎衣而有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220355_comment'></div>身不失天下之显名，尊为天子，富有四海之内，宗庙飨之，子孙保之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220355_comment'></div>于是诗见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220355_comment'></div>然则得天与民，顾非孝不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220355_comment'></div>不然，是诗何以首言哲王，屡言孝思也哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1220355_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>立政讲义</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220356")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220356'>明王立政，不惟其官惟其人，则政之所由立也无他道焉，得人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220356_comment'></div>是道也，三代共之，莫不皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220356_comment'></div>而周公于成王又告戒熟复若是其至者，以用人之际，不容于或失也，国之强弱以之，国之治乱以之，国之兴亡以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220356_comment'></div>然则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220356_comment'></div>亦曰审择而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220356_comment'></div>审择之要，必自近始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220356_comment'></div>王左右之臣，其近者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220356_comment'></div>所谓左右之臣者，常伯也，常任也，准人也，缀衣也，虎贲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220356_comment'></div>常伯，庶官之长，所谓在位者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220356_comment'></div>常任，任事之臣，所谓在我者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220356_comment'></div>准人非伯非任，王所取以为准者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220356_comment'></div>缀衣则内侍之类皆举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220356_comment'></div>虎贲则外卫之类皆举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220356_comment'></div>是五者，宜王之所尤审择，而周公之所当先告也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220356_comment'></div>故曰「王左右常伯、常任、准人、缀衣、虎贲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220356_comment'></div>抑尝观夏之事矣，「宅乃事，宅乃牧，宅乃准」，所谓三宅者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220356_comment'></div>抑尝观汤之事矣，「用三有宅，曰三有俊」者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220356_comment'></div>以夏商之事为未至也，又以文王、武王「克知三有宅心，灼见三有俊心」告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220356_comment'></div>所谓三宅者，居常伯、常任、准人之位，而既用者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220356_comment'></div>三俊者，有常伯、常任、准人之才而将用者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220356_comment'></div>在夏之君则居之而安矣，故曰「宅乃事，宅乃牧，宅乃准」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220356_comment'></div>其商之君则用之而就其事，称之而就其才矣，故曰「用三有宅，克即宅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220356_comment'></div>曰三有俊，克即俊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220356_comment'></div>在周文、武则又能克知灼见其心，故曰「克知三有宅心，灼见三有俊心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220356_comment'></div>所谓强弱以兹者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220356_comment'></div>曰「古之人迪惟有夏，乃有室大竞」，则以无其人为不竞也，非强弱以之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220356_comment'></div>所谓治乱以兹者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220356_comment'></div>曰「其在商邑，用协于厥邑」，则以无其人为不能协厥邑也，非治乱以之者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220356_comment'></div>所谓兴亡以之者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220356_comment'></div>于文、武曰「以并受此丕丕基」，则以无其人为不足以共兴起也，非兴亡以之者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220356_comment'></div>强弱也，治乱也，兴亡也，其因则人，而其成则天，得天在乎得民，得民在乎得贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220356_comment'></div>故夏之尊帝，商之丕釐，周之钦事，皆以有是三宅三俊而得乎民，得乎民盖所以得天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220356_comment'></div>非特左右之臣也，自王庭以及乎都邑之臣，自诸侯以及乎夷狄之官，皆以得人为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220356_comment'></div>自三宅至百司庶府，王庭之官也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220356_comment'></div>自艺人至于尹伯，都邑之官也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220356_comment'></div>司徒、司马、司空、亚旅，诸侯之官也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220356_comment'></div>夷微、卢烝、三亳阪尹，夷狄之官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220356_comment'></div>内之王庭，外之都邑，远之诸侯，又其远之于夷狄，皆得常事之士，以充其任，此文武所以并受大业之基也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220356_comment'></div>三代之政，皆以得人为本，则为成王以继其后者当何如哉，益求人以自辅而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220356_comment'></div>故以庶言、庶狱、庶慎，则戒之以思成德之彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220356_comment'></div>于立政、立事，则戒之以其惟吉士，又戒之以「克用常人」，然后内足以相国家而成文武之业，外足以诘戎兵而陟夏禹之迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220356_comment'></div>然既曰成德之彦矣，既曰吉士矣，又终之以「继自今立政，其惟克用常人」，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220356_comment'></div>是篇语名官之意，皆取其有常德焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220356_comment'></div>曰常伯、常任、准人，则非有常德之人不可以居是选也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220356_comment'></div>常之为义大矣哉，荀卿论曰：「天有常道矣，地有常数矣，君子有常体矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220356_comment'></div>君子道其常，小人计其功」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220356_comment'></div>《中庸》曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1220356", 1220356, "Clauses/141/Comments/1")'>庸德</span>之行，庸言之谨，有所不足，不敢不勉，有馀不敢尽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220356_comment'></div>皆取诸常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220356_comment'></div>《恒》卦之《象》曰：「雷风，恒，君子以立不易方」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220356_comment'></div>至于「不恒其德，或承之羞」，则其失见于九三常有之次五曰天地之常，君臣常也，至于月不常，臣失幸也，则其咎见于次曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220356_comment'></div>《都人士》谓有常以齐其民，《常武》言有常以立武事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220356_comment'></div>《语》曰：「人而无恒，不可以作巫医」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220356_comment'></div>《缁衣》曰：「人而无常，不可以为卜筮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220356_comment'></div>然则取诸人以立政也，其可以无常乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220356_comment'></div>曰吉士，曰常人，其揆一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220356_comment'></div>此篇曰「庶常吉士」，《皋陶谟》曰「彰厥有常，吉哉」，则知吉士未始不有常德，而常德所以为吉士焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220356_comment'></div>虽然，得常吉之士矣，有一憸人间之，则政亦无自立焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220356_comment'></div>是书告戒尤详于君子小人之际，曰「用憸人不训于德，是罔显在厥世」，又曰「其勿以憸人」，又曰「时则勿有间之」，言憸人不容有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220356_comment'></div>盖君子小人并立于朝廷之上，而小人者以其类至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220356_comment'></div>此无他，君子之道刚，小人之道柔，君子未尝谋小人，小人必谋君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220356_comment'></div>《夬》之为卦，以五阳决一阴，故曰：「夬，决也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220356_comment'></div>君子道长，小人道忧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220356_comment'></div>夫以五君子决一小人，不曰小人道消者，小人之道不得行焉，非无小人也，小人之道消也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220356_comment'></div>在《泰》之时，上下交而志同，虽有小人，恶得行其道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220356_comment'></div>若乃君子乘小人衅，则小人之道忧而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220356_comment'></div>惟其有忧，则将谋之，虽以一小人之寡，或能为众君子之害，正复有待焉耳，此所以不容有也，故曰「勿有间之」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1220356_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说命下讲义</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220357")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220357'>自「王曰来汝说」以下，高宗以师道命傅说自说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220357_comment'></div>「曰王人求多闻」以下，傅说以学告高宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220357_comment'></div>自「王曰呜呼说四海之内咸仰朕德」以下，高宗知说所以教而更命之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220357_comment'></div>「说拜稽首曰敢对扬天子之休命」，则傅说知高宗所以命而终成之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220357_comment'></div>《君奭》曰：「在武丁时，则有若甘盘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220357_comment'></div>则高宗尝学于甘盘，而不终其业矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220357_comment'></div>《无逸》曰：「旧劳于外，爰暨小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220357_comment'></div>作其即位，爰知小人之依」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220357_comment'></div>则遁于荒远，而险阻艰难备尝之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220357_comment'></div>其所以有望于傅说者，盖困而知学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220357_comment'></div>酒醴不能自发，有以发之者曲糵也，犹才不能自达，有待于达之者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220357_comment'></div>羹不能自和，有以和之者盐梅也，犹德不能自成，有待于成之者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220357_comment'></div>曰「交修予，罔予弃，予惟克迈乃训」，则许之以受教而不拒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220357_comment'></div>说于是乎可以语学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220357_comment'></div>学之道莫先于求多闻，求多闻所以学古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220357_comment'></div>不通于古则处经事而不得其正，莅变事而不知其权，亦恶能有所建立哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220357_comment'></div>非特不足以建立，抑将坠先王之绪而不克永久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220357_comment'></div>故曰：「王，人求多闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220357_comment'></div>时惟建事，学于古训，乃有获；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220357_comment'></div>事不师古，以克永世，匪说攸闻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220357_comment'></div>惟学则知道，知道然后乐循礼，故曰「逊志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220357_comment'></div>学如不及，犹恐失之，故曰「务时敏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220357_comment'></div>学自外至，故曰「厥修乃来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220357_comment'></div>至是，则日知其所亡，月无忘其所能，故曰「道积于厥躬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220357_comment'></div>不足则学，有馀则教，故曰「惟敩学半」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220357_comment'></div>《记》曰「教学相长」，此敩学半之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220357_comment'></div>始于学，终于教，学不可已也，故曰「念终始典于学」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220357_comment'></div>积善在身，犹日长加益，而人不知，故曰「厥德修罔觉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220357_comment'></div>汤之于伊尹，学焉而后臣之，故不劳而王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220357_comment'></div>然则高宗之务学，可不以成汤伊尹之事为监乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220357_comment'></div>则说当「式克钦承」，以辅王之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220357_comment'></div>非特克式钦承也，又「旁招俊乂，列于庶位」，以成交修之志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220357_comment'></div>高宗于是乎知识，所以教而更命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220357_comment'></div>所以更命之者，先正保衡，俾厥后惟尧舜，悯一夫之不获，其自任以天下之重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220357_comment'></div>又其效至于「佑我烈祖，格于皇天」，则今安得有愧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220357_comment'></div>于是乎「罔俾阿衡专美有商」，「克绍乃辟于先王，永绥民」，则非特说无愧于阿衡，我亦无愧于先王矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220357_comment'></div>是乃说所以教而欲成之之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220357_comment'></div>故曰「敢对扬天子之休命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220357_comment'></div>窃尝论之，事不可以不师古；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220357_comment'></div>苟师古，不可以不务学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220357_comment'></div>苟务学，不可以不隆师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220357_comment'></div>古之贤君所以能大过人者，无踰于此三言者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220357_comment'></div>且君之于臣也，岂特臣之而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220357_comment'></div>有不得而臣者则友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220357_comment'></div>费惠公曰：「吾于颜般则友之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220357_comment'></div>王顺、长息则事吾者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220357_comment'></div>有不可得而友之者则事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220357_comment'></div>子思曰：「古之人曰事之云乎，岂曰友之云乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220357_comment'></div>曰，事者师焉而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220357_comment'></div>《经》曰：「能自得师者王，谓人莫己若者亡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220357_comment'></div>传曰：「其君贤君，而有师者王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220357_comment'></div>其君中君，而有师者霸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220357_comment'></div>然则固不可以无师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220357_comment'></div>黄帝学于务成，禹学于西王国，汤学于伊尹，文王学于畴子斯，武王学于郭叔，周威公学于宁越，齐小白学于管仲，魏文侯学于子夏，晋献公学于祖朝，燕昭王学于孙膑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220357_comment'></div>何必高宗，古之人皆然，至于功德有远近，成就有大小，所学有贤不贤，则系乎人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220357_comment'></div>然则固不可不学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220357_comment'></div>尝观尧舜之为君，禹、皋陶之为臣，都俞吁咈，共济于一堂之上，宜必有甚高难行之法度，不可逮及之谋谟，更新一时，焜耀来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220357_comment'></div>不然，何以得圣君贤臣之名于霄壤间哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220357_comment'></div>及考《书》之所载，不称其能作古，而称其能稽古，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1220357", 1220357, "Clauses/163/Comments/2")'>曰「若</span>稽古帝尧」，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1220357", 1220357, "Clauses/164/Comments/2")'>曰「若</span>稽古帝舜」，<span class='link'
