onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1220357", 1220357, "Clauses/165/Comments/2")'>曰「若</span>稽古<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1220357", 1220357, "Clauses/165/Comments/3")'>大禹</span>」，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1220357", 1220357, "Clauses/166/Comments/2")'>曰「若</span>稽古皋陶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220357_comment'></div>君臣之间，皆称稽古焉，然后知虽圣帝贤臣，未有不本于师古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220357_comment'></div>所谓学者学此也，所谓教者教此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220357_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「不愆不忘，率由旧章」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220357_comment'></div>《书》曰：「无作聪明乱旧章」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220357_comment'></div>然则事不可不师古明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220357_comment'></div>由得师以务学，由务学以师古，以至于建立无愧乎先王，此高宗之所以为贤君者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220357_comment'></div>孟子曰：「天有为之君，必有所不召之臣，欲有谋焉则就之，其尊德乐道，不如是不足与有为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220357_comment'></div>呜呼，所谓大有为之君，盖不世出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220357_comment'></div>然而无是君则已，苟有是君，未有无其臣焉，此殆若符契之合，故曰「必有所不召之臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220357_comment'></div>高宗即位之初，精诚感格，梦赉良弼，得说于傅岩，置说于左右，以版筑之贱位冢宰，以人臣之卑处师道，君任之而不疑，臣居之而无畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220357_comment'></div>此非有神契默会，恶能臻于是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220357_comment'></div>文王之得臧丈人，高宗之得傅说，原其遇合，盖有异于人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220357_comment'></div>宜其相得之深，无所疑畏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220357_comment'></div>然说之始对高宗曰「畴敢不祗若王之休命」者，彼以臣之事责我也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1220357_comment'></div>卒曰「敢对扬天子之休命」者，彼以师道望我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1220357_comment'></div>谓之对扬，则若与为敌焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1220357_comment'></div>有道之士，处辞受之间，无可苟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1220357_comment'></div>且当其任不辞其责，有是实不辞其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1220357_comment'></div>孟子之于齐王，且将以师道自居也，而况有高宗之君乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1220357_comment'></div>汤之于伊尹，学焉而后臣，高宗之于说，臣焉而后学，其事虽殊，然其成功一也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1220357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年4月</a>　在会稽，有诗赠卢襄。作品：送吴兴太守卢给事赴兵部侍郎召四首以邦家之光为韵。<div id='poem_529133' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529133' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529133?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吴兴太守卢给事赴兵部侍郎召四首以邦家之光为韵<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529133")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529133_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529133'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529133'>东风催行舻，旌旗转修扛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529133'>千骑如登仙，我心岂得降。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529133'>嗣学初元年，德意孚万邦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529133'>不战屈丑虏，威声疾奔泷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529133'>眷言帷幄旧，分符隔涛江。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529133'>尚书古司戎，名实尚谁<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作能）</span>双。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529133'>折冲要从容，谈笑空酒缸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529133'>帝曰汝遄归，谋国资敦庞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529133'>无庸斗大州，洪钟受微撞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529133'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_529133_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529134' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529134' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529134?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529134_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529134'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529134'>汀洲初楫迎，红紫烂朝霞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529134'>及兹理旋舻，绿阴已笼沙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529134'>使君如东君，来去不恋家。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529134'>独持五色笔，摛辞灿芳华。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529134'>明年凤凰池，春风浩无涯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529134'>须公赋丹青，去路不可遮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529134'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_529134_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529135?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529135'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529135'>公来临我邦，天意若见私。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529135'>从容坐席间，风化已四驰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529135'>民曰吾二天，士曰得我师。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529135'>庶几少淹留，子弟公教之。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529135'>如何如<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作去）</span>不顾，公岂要我思。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529135'>不见溪上山，旦暮发妍姿。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529135'>及兹有行色，风日含悽悲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529135'>公亦何负渠，欠渠百篇诗。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529135_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529135'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_529135_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529136' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529136' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529136?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529136_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529136'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529136'>西雍拜颜色，振鹭俱分行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529136'>绣衣浙江滨，再上君子堂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529136'>首尾二十载，持橐侍明光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529136'>厌看南朝山，易绾吴兴章。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529136'>煌煌朱两轓，照我梓与桑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529136'>怪我衫始青，怜我鬓<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作发）</span>已苍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529136'>颇复见劳苦，感慨激中肠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529136'>向来官如泥，葡萄换西凉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529136'>剪翎但鸣悲，坐阅百鸟翔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529136'>公为世良师，医国有禁方。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529136'>颇闻药笼中，臭味久已尝。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529136'>小草存<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作在）</span>远志，未用出声妨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529136'>采掇公弗疑，结根稔风霜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529136'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_529136_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年10月</a>　在会稽，刘一止有启谢翟汝文举荐。作品：谢翟内翰荐举启。<div id='poem_1220302' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220302' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220302?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢翟内翰荐举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220302")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220302_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220302'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220302'>顷以孤生，获从下吏，于左右乏半辞之助，居职业无一日之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220302_comment'></div>独乡者慕用之诚，盖不图见顾之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220302_comment'></div>荐论误及，跼蹐靡容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220302_comment'></div>惟士之适时，犹女之从聘，一遇知己，殆将终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220302_comment'></div>虽云待礼而后行，常恐失身而晚悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220302_comment'></div>岂聘者实重其选，抑从者亦择所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220302_comment'></div>古道悠哉，斯言已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220302_comment'></div>伏念某学陋而闻寡，志大而术疏，及此衰年，始縻寸禄，间关自笑，慷慨受知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220302_comment'></div>在古人以为甚难，而晚进岂容骤致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220302_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官三代豪杰，一时宗师，国论以为指南，吾道之所寄命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220302_comment'></div>捃收气类，振挽滞淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220302_comment'></div>何期流落之馀，乃得依归之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220302_comment'></div>正使自择，宁复有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220302_comment'></div>某敢不益励宿心，仰酬谬眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220302_comment'></div>仕才如此，或未惭君子之归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220302_comment'></div>巧固有之，不敢贻门下之辱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1220302_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年11月</a>　在会稽，刘一止有诗谢翟汝文临学行乡饮酒之礼。作品：谢会稽守翟内相临学行乡饮酒之礼。<div id='poem_529208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529208?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢会稽守翟内相临学行乡饮酒之礼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529208")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529208'>清晓传呼振戟衣，泮林云日炫旌旗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529208'>风尘贴妥投戈后，色笑雍容劝学时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529208'>先世流芳今有继，圣衷图旧正畴咨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529208'>王褒愿草得贤颂，可但中和宣布诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529208'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在会稽，自作真赞。<div id='poem_529380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自作真赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529380")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529380'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529380'>枯木寒岩，形影相依。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529380'>禄食而臞，孰与遁肥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529380'>四十九年，我知其非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529380'>已往不谏，来者庶几。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529380'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_529380'><span class='label'>按：</span>《苕溪集》卷二四。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_529380_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年5月1日</a>　在会稽，有文贺赵构即位改元。作品：皇帝登极赦祭诸庙文。<div id='poem_1220415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝登极赦祭诸庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220415")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220415'>皇帝总师靖难，勤劳王家，功大德备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220415_comment'></div>念历数之有在，审讴歌之已归，乃以五月朔旦登受大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220415_comment'></div>天地交感，日月扬光，赦令既颁，泽及幽显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220415_comment'></div>远近臣吏，下逮黎元，扶老携幼，手足蹈舞，或至感泣，愿少须臾无死，以观中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220415_comment'></div>岂惟臣民，神亦永有依归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220415_comment'></div>各率乃职，用劢相我国家，其无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月</a>　在会稽，闻杭州乱，有诗。作品：闻杭州乱二首。<div id='poem_529148' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529148' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529148?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻杭州乱二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529148")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529148'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529148'>饥来命饷寒索衣，官家养兵如养儿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529148'>时平军律久玩弛，辕门笑歌骄莫随。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529148'>往时金陵囚刺史，今者杭州<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作城）</span>漕臣死。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529148'>稽天烈<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作狂）</span>焰穷朝昏，千丈红霞炫江水。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529148'>邻州之兵如此兵，呜呼此难何时平。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529148'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_529148_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529149?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529149'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529149'>缓<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作缒）</span>城将母走者谁，吾宗贵人丞相儿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529149'>高门潭潭深如海，一朝赤脚踏路岐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529149'>吁嗟身世本何<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作何所）</span>有，金帛满家那得守。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529149'>衣冠自古皆贼仇，玉石俱焚无好丑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529149'>呜呼安得贫富受用势略齐，无庸悬绝产祸机。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529149'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_529149_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月</a>　在会稽，上讨贼状给翟汝文。作品：与越帅议讨杭贼状。<div id='poem_1220286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与越帅议讨杭贼状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220286")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220286'>某窃闻杭州兵士闭城门，夺守帅，杀监司，纵火大掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220286_comment'></div>继闻阁下遣卒徒数辈入贼招谕，晓以祸福，且令出降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220286_comment'></div>使者再往返，贼辞卑屈而未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220286_comment'></div>彼自以罪大，不宜遽出，入窃大府子女玉帛之欲，未厌于其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220286_comment'></div>彼非不知吾帅治吾州如古人御军士，有恩信劳来衣食之甚厚也，盖势穷力屈而后降耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220286_comment'></div>日者又闻阁下以为贼不足平，方将发属郡之兵，自将往讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220286_comment'></div>绝江济师，某窃疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220286_comment'></div>或曰：信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220286_comment'></div>或曰：兵家固有先声后实，此殆为先声者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220286_comment'></div>或曰：阁下谋府靓深，非吾徒所能料也，然不然未可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220286_comment'></div>且贼夺守帅，杀监司，变之大者，阁下受朝廷之寄，当一面之重，讨之宜也，顾未知所以讨之之策安出耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220286_comment'></div>自军律废弛，吾州之兵与属郡之兵，其旧存者骄肆狠悖，犹杭之兵也，然今日之势，在彼为死士，在我为骄卒，彼一以当我百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220286_comment'></div>若新募之兵，又率皆田野之人，未尝阅习，姑使带弓剑执旗纛以守郛郭，絷犬豕而蒙以虎豹之皮，一露爪足，彼则咍之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220286_comment'></div>又杭起自江而济有二道，曰西兴，曰渔浦，率皆背水，未见其有异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220286_comment'></div>夫两军相拒于平原，敌向水，我背水，且不可，况背水而攻人之城哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220286_comment'></div>此兵家所谓危道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220286_comment'></div>某愚见以谓，莫若招衢、婺、温、台等州之民居山谷间号为土豪者，假以官称，诱以厚赏，使募鎗杖手，择精锐数千，选将统之，取道由富阳以进，并山遵陆，而无背水之窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220286_comment'></div>又檄浙西诸郡兵尅日俱集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220286_comment'></div>民出其左，浙西兵出其右，贼势穷迫，必面缚出降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220286_comment'></div>藉令不如所欲，在吾州固未有患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220286_comment'></div>某愚陋，诚重守帅之出，譬如将百万钱与人博，必三复投之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220286_comment'></div>若悉举而大投，有不胜则无继矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220286_comment'></div>兵家顾岂有必胜之理哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220286_comment'></div>方今国威未振，民卒幸乱，旁近窃发者非一，吾州之氓，以帅为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220286_comment'></div>今举一路之兵自将以往，不顾其后，以我之百当彼之一，而又履兵家之危道，诚恐非徒不足以靖乱，抑有不可知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220286_comment'></div>昔魏遣太子申自将攻齐，过外黄，外黄徐子劝太子还，既而曰：「彼劝太子战攻，欲啜汁者众，太子虽欲还，不得矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220286_comment'></div>伏望阁下熟计而审处之，无为欲啜汁之人所诖误也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220286_comment'></div>某越职妄议，罪在不贷，然今日之事非常事也，辄冒昧以献，无任怀惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1220286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在会稽，遇方允迪，有诗。作品：次韵方允迪秘监会稽相遇怀吴兴旧游二首。<div id='poem_529209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵方允迪秘监会稽相遇怀吴兴旧游二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529209")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529209'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529209'>故山畴昔奉英游，老去功名失路头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529209'>江海一官如许冷，田园三载不知秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529209'>谢公塘外千峰紫，何楷庐边一径幽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529209'>心折少陵存殁句，恨无酒力破劳愁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529209'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_529209'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_529209_0'>⑴ 自注：旧游方时敏、吴亦虚皆已物故。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_529209_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_529210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529210?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529210'>鉴湖列嶂自天开，云色岚光入酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529210'>忽遣同游有陶谢，故应交契拟陈雷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529210'>他乡日日典衣醉，公事时时牵马来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529210'>要买扁舟穷胜绝，共追樵径晚风回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529210'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529210_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在会稽，诗悼刘韐。作品：悼忠显刘公二首。<div id='poem_529347' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529347' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529347?labeling=true' target='_blank'>悼忠显刘公二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529347")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529347_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529347'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529347'>时相开边隙，膻胡入帝州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529347_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529347'>痛心惟主辱，何意辨身谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529347_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529347'>义气摧山岳，高居照斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529347_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529347'>天令光史册，为洗百年羞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529347_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529347'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529347_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529348?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529348'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529348'>重义何难死，知恩忍自欺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529348'>豫生真国士，南八是男儿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529348'>天地一朝黑，风霜千岁悲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529348'>至今瞻拱木，人口胜丰碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529348'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在会稽，为杨震作墓志铭。作品：宋故敦武郎知麟州建宁寨累赠太师秦国公杨公墓碑。<div id='poem_1220373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故敦武郎知麟州建宁寨累赠太师秦国公杨公墓碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220373")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220373'>杨氏望于关西，由汉魏隋唐以至国朝，世胄联延，列第分坊，博龟袭紫，人物门第之盛，莫与比伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220373_comment'></div>支分派别，散居四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220373_comment'></div>自公曾高而上，皆葬代郡，遂为代之崞县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220373_comment'></div>公讳震，字某，以明经上第，历保定、清源二县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220373_comment'></div>已而踰冠，恬养丘园，终承武郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220373_comment'></div>讳日新者，公之曾大父也，年少有声，九上礼部，再举明法中第，历临晋、孟、太谷三县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220373_comment'></div>贤而有吏能，为忠宣范公所器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220373_comment'></div>以宣德郎致仕，累赠太师、代国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220373_comment'></div>讳仲臣者，公之大父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220373_comment'></div>公之考讳宗闵，少读书有志者，尝曰：「吾祖居乡闾，岁饥，发仓粟粒价速售，俾籴者自拣斗斛不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220373_comment'></div>相阳辟邑牵，延乡先生教授邑子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220373_comment'></div>论者以为功利及人，宜自有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220373_comment'></div>吾意丈夫当以功名自见，章句之学不足以发身成业」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220373_comment'></div>既而以材武绝伦试艺殿廷，出卫士右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220373_comment'></div>仁宗皇帝伟之，补三班借职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220373_comment'></div>历事五朝，名闻西北二边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220373_comment'></div>建炎中，金人犯长安，守节以死，终武功大夫、贵州刺史、永兴军路马步军副都总管，累赠太师、魏国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220373_comment'></div>公励于学，能文善书，精骑射，质貌魁伟，沈塞有谋，魏公在诸子中特奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220373_comment'></div>既冠从戎，以斩馘功补三班差使，调河东经略司指教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220373_comment'></div>遇其下有恩，且诲且勉，阅世中程者多，部刺史交荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220373_comment'></div>秩满，改授庆州监酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220373_comment'></div>继授安边城巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220373_comment'></div>太原帅薛嗣昌遣将自丰州宁远、保宁等寨进讨西夏，公隶岚石路军马来承庆，至爬沙流遇敌，斩首三百馀级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220373_comment'></div>进至倾吴堆盘，生擒酋长屈闹，复斩级二百，以功转三班借职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220373_comment'></div>官制行，改承信郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220373_comment'></div>人有致馈于公者，公谢之，馈者曰：「我辈愿效之，何嫌」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220373_comment'></div>公曰：「始吾父命之名，实慕汉安平侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220373_comment'></div>公以清白遗子孙，且曰：『尔勉之，无爽四知之戒』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220373_comment'></div>自是我守此言，如护头目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220373_comment'></div>今尔以无名之赐加吾，其可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220373_comment'></div>及代城，或裒金以赆，曰：「微公，我辈无噍类」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220373_comment'></div>公一无所受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220373_comment'></div>政和中，朝廷议复减底河，命河东师任熙明会合诸军，自晋宁、绥德两界，分诸将校，骁勇者咸在，公居迁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220373_comment'></div>贼据山为城，下瞰我师动息，辄为所得，诸将三却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220373_comment'></div>寻募能土工者穴城，师再进，角楼自堕，公率数辈拔剑先登，斩击千百人，大军乘胜平其城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220373_comment'></div>上功第一，迁成忠郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220373_comment'></div>宣和初，河东帅奏公充平定军训练军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220373_comment'></div>三年，方腊盗据杭睦，朝廷姚平仲为都统制征之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220373_comment'></div>公从折可存自浙东追击，至三界河镇，与贼遇，斩首八千馀级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220373_comment'></div>追袭至剡、上虞、天台、乐清四县，取韦羌、朝贤、六远三洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220373_comment'></div>至黄岩，贼帅吕师囊据断头山扼险拒我，前辄下石，死伤者众，累日不能进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220373_comment'></div>可存问计安出，公以轻兵缘山背上，乘高鼓噪，矢石交发，贼大惊溃，复纵火自卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220373_comment'></div>公曰：「机不可失也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220373_comment'></div>乃被重铠及裤褶，与敢死士履火突入，生得师囊，乃斩贼首三千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220373_comment'></div>复有号余大翁者，以万众围永嘉踰月，公从平仲、可存兼驿星驰斛之，且曰：「太师贷胁从无知之民，不可以数计」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220373_comment'></div>师还，诸将请优加褒异，特进五阶，至脩武郎，叙迁敦武郎、知麟州建宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220373_comment'></div>户杂番汉，嚚讼难以理晓，公剖决曲当，上下悦服，主不忍欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220373_comment'></div>初，契丹骁将小鞠䩮奔于西戎，居清肃、河清军，招集散亡杂西北胡羌，众十数万，破丰州，攻麟府城寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220373_comment'></div>魏公统领麟府路军马屡摧败之，尽得其父母妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220373_comment'></div>靖康初，金人围太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220373_comment'></div>冬十月，驱幽燕叛亡与夏人、奚人等，与大至建宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220373_comment'></div>既合围，鞠䩮叩城语公曰：「尔父夺吾偏头独建之居，又败釜灶山，掩我骨肉，吾忍死至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220373_comment'></div>尔举城降我，全汝躯命，不然皆齑粉矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220373_comment'></div>时寨兵精锐悉从折可求死于交城之战，所馀才老弱百数，众守勿坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220373_comment'></div>公毅然晓众曰：「汝等父兄俱死于敌，于汝为仇，不待吾言而后喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220373_comment'></div>上报国恩，下雪亲冤，在此时矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220373_comment'></div>众乃听命，日夜奋励，缒城挠贼，斩获甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220373_comment'></div>贼怒，济师急攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220373_comment'></div>阅旬，城中矢尽，公向麟府再拜诀曰：「儿报国以身，不得复为孝子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220373_comment'></div>左右皆泣下，不忍仰视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220373_comment'></div>顷之，城陷，公挥短兵力战，殁于阛阓，时十有八日也，年四十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220373_comment'></div>二子死之，阖门俱陷于城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220373_comment'></div>初，魏公闻围建宁，曰：「吾儿死矣，其忠劲类我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220373_comment'></div>已而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220373_comment'></div>公熟古将方略，能洞敌情，每从魏公远徼出征，决策取胜，其功居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220373_comment'></div>志在立名，不苟求富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220373_comment'></div>浙东贼平，所师奇其材，欲以子女通婚，公谢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220373_comment'></div>或曰：「折氏求子，非子求折氏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220373_comment'></div>公曰：「不然，吾祖皆以器业自奋，安能倚姻家幸进，取非偶之讥」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220373_comment'></div>尝自谓：「吾平时所为，未尝有一事不可语人者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220373_comment'></div>其刻励坚正若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220373_comment'></div>建宁之祸，公之子存中从征河朔，独免于难，今为少傅、宁远军节度使、兼领殿前都指挥使职事、秦国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220373_comment'></div>累赠公之太师、秦国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1220373_comment'></div>祖妣檀氏、雍氏，妣贾氏、刘氏，配董氏、继室张氏，俱赠秦国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1220373_comment'></div>男四人，少傅其长也，居中、执中从父战殁，彦中未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1220373_comment'></div>女二人，长适乡贡进士王公宏，次未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1220373_comment'></div>孙男三人：契，左奉议郎、知大宗正丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1220373_comment'></div>倓，左承奉郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1220373_comment'></div>㒜，右承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1220373_comment'></div>孙女六人，长曰洞元，尝适右宣教郎、直秘阁、通判湖州军州事刘正卒，夫殁，弃俗为道士，年十九卒，诏赠冲妙鍊师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1220373_comment'></div>馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1220373_comment'></div>少傅以某年某月某甲子葬公于吴兴武康县崇仁乡杨村翔凤山之麓，张夫人祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1220373_comment'></div>一日，契以少傅公尝来请铭，某得公行实，读之三复慨叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1220373_comment'></div>尝观韩愈为田弘正作庙铭，载诏语曰：「维弘正父子继忠孝，予维宠嘉之，是以命汝愈铭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1220373_comment'></div>文辞至今焜耀简册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1220373_comment'></div>今魏公与公挺身许国，出万死一生之计，英烈凛然，精爽如在，与日月争光可也，岂田氏父子所得比耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1220373_comment'></div>宜得一世名儒，发扬遗懿，闳大俊杰，与韩子相后先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1220373_comment'></div>而少傅属铭，乃逮不敏，非理所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1220373_comment'></div>既辞谢不获，则又惟念少傅身卫社稷，为世宝臣，南渡以来，首挫强敌，以宽主忧，幽闺妇女，皆能道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1220373_comment'></div>祖孙三世勋德之茂，前古所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1220373_comment'></div>及兹升平，帝眷有加，位列九棘，宠数优异，盖事之称，抑又知天之所以报公父子者在兹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1220373_comment'></div>降及诸孙，俱励于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1220373_comment'></div>契以艺文取高第，兄弟彬彬，以切以磋，以光其宗，光大未艾，岂人力也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1220373_comment'></div>岂人力也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1220373_comment'></div>某诚固陋，然此而不铭，尚谁铭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1220373_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_1220373'>岳岳惟公，慷慨即戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1220373_comment'></div>沈毅伟杰，益习文业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1220373_comment'></div>急病逊夷，不见所难，与敌周旋，人后身先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1220373_comment'></div>爬沙减底，摧锋陷坚，义勇冠军，威名乃宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1220373_comment'></div>东南承平，骤罹寇警，既蹂杭、睦，连城巷哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1220373_comment'></div>公佐主帅，往靖东浙，披山剔洞，破其蚁结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1220373_comment'></div>维时黄岩，别酋固拒，凭高下石，士卒反顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1220373_comment'></div>公以轻骑，出贼之背，扬雄噪呼，贼大惊溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1220373_comment'></div>乃被重铠，蹈火突入，生致渠魁，窘不得逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1220373_comment'></div>逮居建宁，虏衔宿冤，抟虚麇至，叩城有言：「尔父迫我，掩我骨肉，亟以城降，尚贷尔僇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1220373_comment'></div>公曰「此身，惟国是许，不以膏血，为尔衅鼓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1220373_comment'></div>于时寨兵，仅馀老稚，感激听命，有死无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1220373_comment'></div>人谁不死，公死何尤，有臣若斯，不为国羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1220373_comment'></div>天监在下，报尔子孙，世公世师，有耀其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1220373_comment'></div>我作铭诗，大书深刻，用侈厥庆，诏于罔极<span class='inlineComment2'>（《苕溪集》卷四八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1220373_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_110_1220373'>相阳辟邑牵：未明其意，当有误。</div><div id='poem_sentence_110_1220373_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7f0da83ead3648e1b29b3f1bc08910d5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7f0da83ead3648e1b29b3f1bc08910d5");'><span id='7f0da83ead3648e1b29b3f1bc08910d5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1129')">1128-1129年</a>，51-52岁</div><div id='7f0da83ead3648e1b29b3f1bc08910d5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　在会稽，会晤张元干。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年5月</a>　在会稽，有高宗驻跸表。本年五月戊寅朔，高宗次常州。辛巳，次镇江府。乙酉，至江宁府，驻跸神宵宫，改府名建康。作品：车驾驻跸建康起居表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220265' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220265' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220265?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾驻跸建康起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220265")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220265_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220265'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220265'>展义时巡，观风都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220265_comment'></div>六龙所指，百神骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220265_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>恭惟皇帝陛下昧旦视朝，斋居决政，永念无疆之服，克安有截之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220265_comment'></div>乃眷建康，久腾王气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220265_comment'></div>龙蟠虎踞，宁论割据之英雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220265_comment'></div>地僻天开，赫有中兴之气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220265_comment'></div>远阻淮浸，近控江涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220265_comment'></div>苑长洲而沧海陵，既包吴分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220265_comment'></div>城方城而池汉水，仍拥楚疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220265_comment'></div>方将寻周瑜、鲁肃之师，倚王导、谢安之佐，内殄寇警，外威羌酋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220265_comment'></div>胜算可期，成功有韪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220265_comment'></div>后来无罚，已闻家室之宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220265_comment'></div>时迈其邦，终冀干戈之戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220265_comment'></div>臣身縻藩服，望远天威，莫参班瑞之荣，徒切摇旌之念。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1220265_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月</a>　在会稽，会晤过郡的李邴，李邴荐刘一止。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月</a>　在会稽，有高宗起居表。九月丙午朔，日有食之。谍报金人治舟师，将由海道窥江、浙。辛亥，次平江府。作品：车驾驻跸平江起居表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220266' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220266?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾驻跸平江起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220266")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220266_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220266'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220266'>展义楚疆，壮古都之胜势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220266_comment'></div>观风吴会，驻鸣跸之清尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220266_comment'></div>民物忻愉，山川震叠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220266_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>恭惟皇帝陛下受天明命，兴我有邦，躬尧帝之圣神，禀成汤之勇智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220266_comment'></div>念三年大聘，既享备于多仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220266_comment'></div>而五载一巡，实遵行于故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220266_comment'></div>俨汉官之容卫，慰夏谚之歌谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220266_comment'></div>方将整六师以修我戎，相上帝以遏乱略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220266_comment'></div>仰威灵之顿迩，觉藩翰以增雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220266_comment'></div>臣猥以谫才，误当分阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220266_comment'></div>万国玉帛，莫趋禹会之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220266_comment'></div>千里舳舻，想见摐扬之盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220266_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月</a>　在会稽，有迎接高宗表。本年十月癸未，高宗至杭州，复如浙东。庚寅，度浙江。壬辰，至越州。作品：车驾巡幸越州远迎奏表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾巡幸越州远迎奏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220267")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220267'>六龙在御，万骑前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220267_comment'></div>俾方岳之各朝，肆觐东后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220267_comment'></div>念室家之相庆，奚独后予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220267_comment'></div>颁诏幸临，载途呼舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220267_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>恭惟皇帝陛下励精庶士，若昔大猷，躬观风问俗之劳，振黜幽陟明之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220267_comment'></div>眷此名郡，实为奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220267_comment'></div>菲食卑宫，钦念禹功之远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220267_comment'></div>苦身焦思，俯怜越霸之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220267_comment'></div>曩览古以兴怀，见登堂而赋咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220267_comment'></div>惟时金石，既传帝作之歌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220267_comment'></div>今我臣民，果契天临之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220267_comment'></div>山川改观，日月扬光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220267_comment'></div>臣猥以匪才，辱在守土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220267_comment'></div>仰威灵之广被，知封略之再恢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220267_comment'></div>舞干羽于两阶，将见远夷之格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220267_comment'></div>执玉帛者万国，获陪近侍之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220267_comment'></div>心剧旌摇，耳倾鸣跸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1220267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月</a>　在会稽，有迎驾祭山川文。本年十月癸未，高宗至杭州，复如浙东。庚寅，度浙江。壬辰，至越州。作品：车驾巡幸祭山川文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾巡幸祭山川文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220416")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220416'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220416'>皇帝南巡诸侯，宠绥吴越，宽政毁关，薄歛已责，德意甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220416_comment'></div>于是命有司修柴望，谨故事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220416_comment'></div>惟山川之灵，各率乃职，用先后奔走，劢相我王家，妥安尔封疆，则尔神亦有光宠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1220416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在会稽，上书越帅李邺，录诗请教。作品：上越帅书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上越帅书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220297")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220297'>从政郎、充越州州学教授刘某，再拜上书帅坐待制阁下：某尝闻，言辞者，感于情而后发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220297_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐之七者之谓情，情也者，随遇而感，有感而发，亦若金石丝竹之有待而鸣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220297_comment'></div>其感发有浅深，故其辞有工拙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220297_comment'></div>人之论曰：欢愉之辞难工，穷苦之言易好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220297_comment'></div>是真有难易之辨乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220297_comment'></div>诗之变风变雅也，大抵皆循理之说，故读之想见乎其人，如出乎其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220297_comment'></div>有正人谊士愤切感激之气也，有迁客逐臣羁旅流落之叹也，有室家思怨尔汝昵昵之私也，有故国旧都凄凉绵绵之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220297_comment'></div>其言率有以感动人意，而喜诵说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220297_comment'></div>杜少陵遭时乱离，间关陕蜀，负薪采稆，餔糒不给，凡出处动息、劳逸悲乐之事，一见于诗，盖穷而益工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220297_comment'></div>屈原忧愁幽思而作《离骚》，庾信以悲哀为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220297_comment'></div>然后知欢愉之动情者浅，而穷苦之感情深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220297_comment'></div>某无似，生长于世，五十有二年，概其平生，抱百忧而无一娱，故流离辛苦之状，间见乎辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220297_comment'></div>虽不能如古人之工，而独知所谓感于情者深而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220297_comment'></div>又自更国难以来，益复忽忽不自料理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220297_comment'></div>悯天步之方艰，恫大耻之未雪，每一念至，则中夜起坐，当食失箸，悲来填膺，则揾下绿睫，视曩之所谓流离辛苦，盖又不足道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220297_comment'></div>乃者获吏麾下，侍坐席，聆謦欬，温然若将怜而教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220297_comment'></div>退而自思，顾无以借资受教于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220297_comment'></div>又平昔所为言语文字，率皆愁忧无聊之辞，独可为其穷似己者道，难与富贵利达者言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220297_comment'></div>既又思之，阁下以道行闻于乡，以文学世其家，以忠信勇决自见于时，奋自臞儒，亟登清近，作镇藩屏，貌舒徐而不矜，志刺促而当忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220297_comment'></div>此其中非苟以富贵利达为荣，故必有先天下之忧而忧者，安知不有似于闾巷穷苦之士哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220297_comment'></div>谨录新旧杂诗若干首，并用藉手以请，惟恕其僭率，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220297_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1220297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　居会稽期间，送僧游龟溪作诗。作品：独居会稽官舍送僧游龟溪因记寄声弊庐。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_529168' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529168' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529168?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独居会稽官舍送僧游龟溪因记寄声弊庐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529168")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529168_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529168'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529168'>老人年六十，生理常刺促。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529168'>归无一棱田，此事乱心曲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529168'>妻孥渺相望，幼稚炯在目。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529168'>师今遇龟溪，山水无尽绿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529168'>石壁严宝坊，泉甘宜杞菊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529168'>但恐斋厨空，眼饱不救腹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529168'>并山行<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作行山）</span>径微，草露湿人足。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529168'>师访老人家，门前有修竹。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　居会稽期间，与朱宾老游有诗。作品：次韵宾老过会稽访余同游禹庙龙瑞宫晚归二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span>次韵朱宾老过我对月小酌一首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_529270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529270?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529270'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529270'>十载江湖客，重来霜鬓侵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529270'>他时林樾底，归去话登临。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/529271?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529271'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529271'>禹穴徵前史，龙门访隐书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529271'>相携如故里，失喜问吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529271'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529271_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵朱宾老过我对月小酌一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529264")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529264'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529264'>老人论旧事，感慨思悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529264'>暗喜生眉宇，新凉入酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529264'>竹风谁汝和，檐月要人陪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529264'>此客非凡客，斯时得得来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529264'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529264_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　居会稽期间，有越州修庙文。作品：越州修城祭庙文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>越州修城祭庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220418")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220418'>郡介居江湖之间，环水为城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220418_comment'></div>山瀑暴集，冲垫圮剥，阅日滋久，襟抱亏疏，无所蔽障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220418_comment'></div>某承乏帅事，甫见吏民，问所先务，咸曰：「无城何以保民」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220418_comment'></div>虑事量功，所不敢后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220418_comment'></div>凡板干畚筑之具，土物远近之宜，分授有司，涓日创始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220418_comment'></div>惟神其相兹役，使工不劳病，期不愆素，以迄有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220418_comment'></div>惟神之休，敢不知谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　居会稽期间，有致语。作品：代请越帅致语。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1220469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代请越帅致语</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220469")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220469'>师徒取道，共知元帅之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220469_comment'></div>父老出郊，争睹藩侯之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220469_comment'></div>可无樽俎，少驻旌旄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220469_comment'></div>恭惟某官节厉冰霜，量涵江海，临难得仁者之勇，接人皆有德之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220469_comment'></div>更惠爱于六州，历光华于五閤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220469_comment'></div>惟兹旧治，实戴殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220469_comment'></div>孤城独存，赖鲁公忠义之力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220469_comment'></div>雅俗未改，服刘宽孝弟之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220469_comment'></div>故应清梦之馀，尚记甘棠之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220469_comment'></div>当年追饯，见攀辕卧辙之悲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220469_comment'></div>今日约行，有分阃建牙之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220469_comment'></div>某官甫迎舟舰，欣望光尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220469_comment'></div>十乘启行，难留于去传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220469_comment'></div>一觞为寿，少尽于群情云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220469_comment'></div>楼船十里驻郊坰，老幼扶持夹道迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220469_comment'></div>卧辙攀辕曾结恋，建牙分阃喜经行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220469_comment'></div>樽前歌舞皆亲按，眼界风烟特地明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220469_comment'></div>要看山公归倒载，莫辞芳醑线深倾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220469_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bc34930f2f714c3eb83c574a4b35485f_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月</a>　在会稽。到浙东提点刑狱任，有谢表。作品：谢提点刑狱浙东到任表。<div id='poem_1220249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢提点刑狱浙东到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220249")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220249'>不违颜于咫尺，拜宠知惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220249_comment'></div>送以礼而光华，岂臣敢辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220249_comment'></div>疾驱轺传，已见更新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220249_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣智昧知时，学不适用，误窃圣人之眷，尝跻清近之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220249_comment'></div>曾报主之不能，乃蠹书而何益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220249_comment'></div>粤从去国，寄江海以偷生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220249_comment'></div>自意此身，与草木而皆腐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220249_comment'></div>孰云记录，尚及孱微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220249_comment'></div>收五年闲放之心，总一道平反之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220249_comment'></div>岂独庶狱之当审，抑将荒政之是修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220249_comment'></div>任固匪轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220249_comment'></div>责何以塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220249_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下法尧言之清问，躬舜德之好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220249_comment'></div>怜臣寄孤，虽功名之难幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220249_comment'></div>谓臣朴拙，尚岂弟之有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220249_comment'></div>臣敢不深体设施，勉图后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220249_comment'></div>布宣宽诏，愿为慈惠之师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220249_comment'></div>销折奸萌，不愧安静之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220249_comment'></div>庶收寸尺，仰答生成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1220249_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_529280'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529280_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
