id='poem_title_529281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529281'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529281'>猛将心期箭有神，争前知贼不知身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529281'>圣恩令贷签军死，汝是中朝个里人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529281'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529281_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529282?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529282'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529282'>胡儿驱马意何忙，淮海暄风炫日光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529282_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529282'>心折关河归不得，而今底处是家乡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529282_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529282'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529282_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529283?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529283'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529283'>六代金陵是帝州，诸侯玉帛等山丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529283_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529283'>指挥大匠新宫阙，早晚鸣鞭向石头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529283_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529283'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529283_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529284?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529284'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529284'>胡儿岂敢易江沱，前日谋臣谬讲和。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529284'>为问奸谀羞死未，较量今者孰为多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529284'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529284_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529285?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529285'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529285'>红旌白马羽林儿，丝鞚当胸短策垂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529285'>归导鸣銮何太喜，腰间金印阿谁知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529285_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529285'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529285_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529286?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529286'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529286'>晓来鼓角动辕门，便觉升平气象存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529286'>他日两宫归就养，更看天子父兄尊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529286'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529286_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529287?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_529287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529287'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529287'>东风九市遍开场，梅柳参差近玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529287'>应许侍臣俱入贺，捧持春酒寿君王。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529287'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_529287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　在会稽。冬，有诗唱和傅崧卿。作品：雪夜一首呈傅舍人。<div id='poem_529123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪夜一首呈傅舍人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529123")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529123'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529123'>朔风无端卷入<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作人）</span>幕，短檠滉漾吹花落。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529123'>怪来觅句如斲冰，门外雪花如舞鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529123'>老妻自起倾残樽，麒麟活火红燉燉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529123'>凭君为唤诗肠温，他日有酒不足论。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529123'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　在会稽。方允迪卒，有诗。作品：方秘监允迪二首。<div id='poem_529351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方秘监允迪挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529351")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529351'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529351'>声名三纪在中州，身到蓬山最上游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529351'>笃行岂惟今代少，摛辞仍向古人求。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529351'>独嗟宣室催归晚，不料漳滨卧病留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529351'>慷慨严尤三策在，暮年谁识子心忧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529351'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529351_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529352' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529352' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529352?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529352_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529352'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529352'>同舍西雍四十春，乱离君我两身存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529352'>宁惟交道全金石，罕见人间此弟昆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529352'>雅志泽民终莫遂，微言忧国岂堪论。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529352'>鸬鹚渡口千峰合，悽断西风泪睫昏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529352'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529352_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年6月15日</a>　在会稽。沈与求卒，作行状。作品：知枢密院事沈公行状。<div id='poem_1220371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知枢密院事沈公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年6月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220371")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220371'>曾祖原，赠少保；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220371_comment'></div>曾祖妣方氏，赠荣国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220371_comment'></div>祖涣，赠太师、嘉国公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220371_comment'></div>祖妣孙氏，赠奉国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220371_comment'></div>父彦修，赠少师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220371_comment'></div>妣丁氏，赠淑国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220371_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1220371'>公讳与求，字必先，世为吴兴德清人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220371_comment'></div>按沈氏之先，于周为子男之国，其地即汉汝南平舆县沈氏是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220371_comment'></div>鲁昭公二十二年为吴所灭，已而复见，至定公四年又灭于蔡，沈遂不祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220371_comment'></div>其后子孙分散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220371_comment'></div>汉晋之世，著名简册者，盖有其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220371_comment'></div>至六朝而盛，家于武原之临溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220371_comment'></div>唐天宝间，析临溪为邑，是为德清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220371_comment'></div>国初虽稍微，而公之族祖暨诸父以儒学踵取名第，至公乃大光显望于吴兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220371_comment'></div>公自少颖异，读书属文，不烦教督，识虑辩诘，已如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220371_comment'></div>未冠，以艺业试乡校，流辈莫与争长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220371_comment'></div>公既丁少师公襄忧，自以家素贫乏，母夫人以己为命，相与致志于学，律身益严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220371_comment'></div>未几，荐名乡书，寻为太学生试选，屡魁多士，名称蔚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220371_comment'></div>及政和五年进士第，授濮阳县县学教授，以道远不便亲养，改常州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220371_comment'></div>任满，授秀州司兵曹事兼推勘公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220371_comment'></div>公治狱不以委吏，事皆躬决，多所平反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220371_comment'></div>再岁，丁母夫人忧，服阕，除太学录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220371_comment'></div>靖康改元，至京师，迁儒林郎，除太学博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220371_comment'></div>建炎初，车驾幸广陵，公始赴官，同荐改通直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220371_comment'></div>会罢太学，除通判明州，改两浙路提举市舶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220371_comment'></div>未赴，御史荐公，对便殿，除监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220371_comment'></div>上疏论执政过失，迁兵部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220371_comment'></div>公自劾，以为言苟不当，宜黜，不应得迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220371_comment'></div>上感寤，行公言，更除殿中侍御史，被旨鞠狱江外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220371_comment'></div>车驾巡海上，公还，趋行在所奏事，寻扈从至会稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220371_comment'></div>而敌寇尚留江左，公首陈追袭之计，不果用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220371_comment'></div>是时江浙创残之馀，盗贼继作，民蠹未除，吏奸滋甚，宪网阔疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220371_comment'></div>追论同知枢密院事、两浙西路宣抚使周望拥重兵于吴门，不能捍蔽，脱身先遁，以至连城陷没；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220371_comment'></div>与诸郡以城降贼，并缘为奸，掠取民财等事，乞正典法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220371_comment'></div>时占象者言，西北有赤气蔽天，中有白气如练，犯北斗、文昌、紫薇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220371_comment'></div>公极论时政得失，宜遣使省陵寝，定驻跸之地，宰相不可虚位，及用祖宗故事，令参知政事与宰相轮日知印，诸将兵各立军额，蠲租赋以宽民力，信赏罚以明功罪，凡十许事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220371_comment'></div>寻除侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220371_comment'></div>宰相以年少骤进，不更世务，公上疏极陈，恐误国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220371_comment'></div>上初难之，会近臣李陵献言，宜诏宰执于罪戾中选择实能，付之以事，仍咨台谏为国择人，勿复再言，出榜朝堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220371_comment'></div>公曰：「自古岂有禁台谏不言者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220371_comment'></div>复论列，其略曰：「任贤使能，人主之柄也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220371_comment'></div>献可替否，台谏之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220371_comment'></div>任使失当，则其祸移；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220371_comment'></div>献替失当，则其职旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220371_comment'></div>是以自古明哲之君，开广言路，所以防蔽塞而杜私邪，上下相须，乃成治道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220371_comment'></div>今乃诏宰执用罪戾之人，而令台谏不言，是必不识事体之人持浅狭自私之见，文巧伪观望之言以误陛下，使陛下虚负拒谏之名，是何不忠之甚也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220371_comment'></div>且自古以来，有责台谏以不言者矣，有旌台谏以能言者矣，未闻明揭榜使勿言也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220371_comment'></div>翌日上为降旨：「李陵身为侍从，乃复疑误朝廷，上言乞诏宰执用蔡京、王黼、张邦昌、苗傅、刘正彦等一时罪戾之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220371_comment'></div>钳闭台谏，使不得言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220371_comment'></div>欲收恶党之恩，遂陈迷国之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220371_comment'></div>可罢侍郎，与在外宫观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220371_comment'></div>沈与求上疏，乞明指献言之人，显行黜责，其论为当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220371_comment'></div>至云变朱成墨，指鹿为马，言太深切，使大臣不敢安位，可罢侍御史，除职与郡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220371_comment'></div>寻除直龙图阁、知台州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220371_comment'></div>待次累月，上思公，有旨召还，再除侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220371_comment'></div>上尝从容言：「王安石之罪在行新法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220371_comment'></div>公对曰：「王安石以己意变先帝法度，误国害民，诚如圣训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220371_comment'></div>然人臣立朝，未论行事之是非，先观心术之邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220371_comment'></div>扬雄名世大儒，主盟圣道，新室之乱，乃为美新剧秦之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220371_comment'></div>冯道左右卖国，得罪万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220371_comment'></div>而安石于汉则取雄，于五代则取道，臣以是知其心术不正，则奸伪百出，僭乱之萌，实由此起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220371_comment'></div>自熙宁、元丰以来，士皆宗安石之学，沈溺其说，节义彫丧，驯致靖康之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220371_comment'></div>污伪卖国，一时叛逆，尚逭典刑，愿陛下明正其罪，以戒为臣不忠者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220371_comment'></div>先是上欲究僣伪事，因公有言，上大感悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220371_comment'></div>公再居言路，附丽前宰相用事者意公悉论出之，公闻之，曰：「近世朋党，习以成风，凡人材不论贤否，皆视宰相出处为进退，盖上之人驱之使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220371_comment'></div>余待罪言路，荷上知遇，第当分别人之邪正能否而公言之，余之职也，岂可谓一时所用皆不贤，而使视宰相为进退哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220371_comment'></div>止择一二明附稔恶者，列于上，群情遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220371_comment'></div>明年春驾幸临安，迁御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220371_comment'></div>时军储窘乏，公极陈屯田利害，为《古今集议》上下二卷上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220371_comment'></div>上用其言，始定营田之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220371_comment'></div>禁卫单寡，兵机不在朝廷，公上言：「仰惟陛下移跸东南，将图恢复之举，先务之急，宜莫如兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220371_comment'></div>汉有南北军，唐自府兵彍骑之法既坏，犹内有禁兵，外有诸镇之兵，上下维持，使无偏重之势，其意远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220371_comment'></div>今图大举，而兵权不在朝廷，虽有枢密院及三省兵房、尚书兵部，但奉行文书而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1220371_comment'></div>愿诏大臣讲求利害而举行之，使人情不骇而兵政益修，助成经理中兴之志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1220371_comment'></div>浙郡淫雨害稼穑，公上疏云：「伏见中夏以来，霪雨过度，浙西数郡之田垂熟淹没者十七八，民有饥馑之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1220371_comment'></div>徽、严州水泉暴涌，浸城郭，漂庐舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1220371_comment'></div>比者临安火延民居，无虑万馀家，甚于去岁会稽之变，岂小异哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1220371_comment'></div>仰惟陛下遭时多难，厉精为治，宵衣旰食，靡遑靡宁，天地顾临，宜有福应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1220371_comment'></div>然阴阳乖和，灾异仍见，陛下亦尝于行事之际，思所未至者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1220371_comment'></div>苟未至焉，则亦加之以诚而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1220371_comment'></div>子思曰：『诚则形，形则著』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1220371_comment'></div>诚之至也，参天地，赞化育，况于行事之际，厥类章章，靡有不著者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1220371_comment'></div>今九庙丘墟，两宫隔绝，夷狄之祸未殄，僣叛之党未平，下民嗷嗷，厌乱思治，以日为岁，痛如焚灼，睹此灾异，心折骨惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1220371_comment'></div>而谈者至谓泽国夏潦，地气使然，火延民房，救者不力，宜不足勤圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1220371_comment'></div>臣恐此言日闻，诚意日替，臣是以泪流落而不自禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1220371_comment'></div>陛下诚以臣言思之，凡陛下所以畏天爱民，用人听言，追祖宗之法，惇骨肉之亲，薄阍寺之权，正宫闱之化，一出于诚，有勉强而行之者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1220371_comment'></div>畏天不以诚，则工祝虽具，近于致渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1220371_comment'></div>爱民不以诚，则诏令虽繁，终于失信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1220371_comment'></div>用人不以诚，则谗间日进，将以疑似而远正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1220371_comment'></div>听言不以诚，则阿谀日闻，将类忌讳，而恶直士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1220371_comment'></div>追祖宗之法而不以诚，则不无背戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1220371_comment'></div>惇骨肉之亲而不以诚，则不无猜嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1220371_comment'></div>薄阍寺之权而不以诚，则虽名为裁抑，而桀黠之辈不除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1220371_comment'></div>正宫闱之化而不以诚，则虽外示朴素，而奢靡之习犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1220371_comment'></div>凡陛下见于行事，臣固知一出于诚，而非勉强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1220371_comment'></div>然臣所谓譊譊者，愿陛下加之意而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1220371_comment'></div>诚意既修，则天地感格，阴阳和平，灾异之兴，转为福耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1220371_comment'></div>上嘉纳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1220371_comment'></div>两浙转运使徐康国自温州奏发宣和间所制间金锁、金屏障什物，上命上之，而康国已猝发至行在所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1220371_comment'></div>公曰：「吾君勤俭，德侔大禹，汉文帝以下不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1220371_comment'></div>异时驻跸广陵，有进而用华靡者，立命焚之通衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1220371_comment'></div>今康国不识事君之礼，尚习故态，欲以微物累盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1220371_comment'></div>乞用广陵故事斥而焚之，仍显黜康国，明示好恶，且为小人希指之戒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1220371_comment'></div>上悉从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1220371_comment'></div>公在言路，首尾四年，凡所论列，不避权要，颇忤时宰意，至是改除吏部尚书，兼权翰林学士兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1220371_comment'></div>未几除龙图阁学士、荆湖南路安抚使兼知潭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1220371_comment'></div>公以疾乞置閒散，改除提举江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1220371_comment'></div>明年，除知镇江府兼两浙西路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1220371_comment'></div>公到官，招集流亡，俾之复业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1220371_comment'></div>异时士卒凭陵居民，闻公威名，重足屏迹，无敢犯法，威德并行，内外绥安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1220371_comment'></div>秋八月，仍复以吏部尚书召，寻兼权翰林学士兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1220371_comment'></div>九月，除参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1220371_comment'></div>是时虏伪入寇，兵已压境，上决意亲征，讫有成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1220371_comment'></div>公居帷幄，实与其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1220371_comment'></div>上亲御翰墨，书《车攻》诗赐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1220371_comment'></div>再岁，乞奉祠，除资政殿学士、知明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1220371_comment'></div>疏再上，改提举临安府洞霄宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1220371_comment'></div>公之出也，以在政府，凡所议论，皆出臆见，无纤毫阿附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1220371_comment'></div>督府治兵，欲大举，公勿与闻，公曰：「此大事也，岂可身居近辅而独不与哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1220371_comment'></div>数上疏求去，上不得已而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1220371_comment'></div>驾幸平江，明年春，以提举万寿观兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1220371_comment'></div>寻召除同知枢密院事，从驾至建康，迁知枢密院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1220371_comment'></div>公首陈恢复之计，练兵市马，积粟聚财，分布将帅，以待机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1220371_comment'></div>而同列不察，疑公沮之，且冒昧欲举，率不克就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1220371_comment'></div>上忆公初言，决意召公，盖欲大用，仅阅累月，得小疾，一夕薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1220371_comment'></div>实绍兴八年六月甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1220371_comment'></div>上痛悼，辍视朝一日，赠左银青光禄大夫，赐水银龙脑以敛，又赐田十顷以恤其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1220371_comment'></div>以今年季秋之甲申，葬于邑之永和乡马鞍山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1220371_comment'></div>取同郡范氏，赠吴兴郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1220371_comment'></div>夫人有美德，先公四年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1220371_comment'></div>三子，曰云纪，右从事郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1220371_comment'></div>曰云章，右承务郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1220371_comment'></div>曰云卿，未任以官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1220371_comment'></div>息女三，长适左从事郎、两浙路转运司准备差遣元益，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1220371_comment'></div>公自被遇简知，历御史三院，于内外事知无不言，前后论列凡四百奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1220371_comment'></div>其间如收揽主权，爱惜名器，斥逐邪佞，亲近正人，未尝不反覆言之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1220371_comment'></div>至于纠官邪，劾赃吏，将帅得失，政事是非，与州县抑配扰民，狱讼过差，监司郡守选除不当，军兴以来进战退守之策、积谷训兵之要，不可概举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1220371_comment'></div>上以公论天下事淹练通达，克己听纳，言之切直，自敌以下有不能堪者，上不罪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1220371_comment'></div>一时台纲自公大振，武将训敕其下，必曰：「汝不识沈中丞耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1220371_comment'></div>其见惮如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1220371_comment'></div>大将入觐，有进缯帛方物者，既分赐六宫，公以谓此事虽微，自政和、宣和以来进献稍侈，今艰虞之时，不宜有此，乞斥还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1220371_comment'></div>时方暮夜，上得公疏，即命追取斥还，仍降札谕公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1220371_comment'></div>公感泣草谢，自以不世遭遇，蒙上听纳，无愧古人，顾未知效死地耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1220371_comment'></div>公自为执政，凡所规益，虽家人莫得闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1220371_comment'></div>所荐人才至多，受荐皆莫知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1220371_comment'></div>上每以知人称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1220371_comment'></div>自小官至宦达，攻苦食淡，处之晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1220371_comment'></div>天性孝友，所得俸禄以给宗族兄弟无难色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1220371_comment'></div>于文无所不能，晚岁益工，尤善为诗，引类托兴，有作者风气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1220371_comment'></div>凡人以为难者，公熟视落笔，便造壸奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1220371_comment'></div>有文集二十卷、奏议三十卷藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1220371_comment'></div>一止从公游踰三十年，自乡校至立朝，虽有出处契阔之异，而相厚之意不少衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1220371_comment'></div>公尝见荐为御史属官，初未尝言，心独识之，然知公莫详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1220371_comment'></div>窃尝叹息，以为君臣之遇，自古所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1220371_comment'></div>有听谏之君，又有能言之臣，然后君臣俱荣，名誉日彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1220371_comment'></div>不幸而无其臣，则君虽有屈己听纳之诚，而臣言不足以发之，遂至于两无称焉，可不惜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1220371_comment'></div>若魏徵之遇太宗，韩休之遇明皇，包拯之遇仁祖，公之遇主上，盖所谓君臣俱荣者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1220371_comment'></div>云纪属一止状公之行，将求诸立言大君子志公墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1220371_comment'></div>公名节之伟，议论之懿，缙绅所共知也，一止不敢私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1220371_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_159_1220371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　在会稽。冬，有诗次韵林季仲。作品：林懿成检正见贻次韵谢之林乃同年。<div id='poem_529226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529226?labeling=true' target='_blank'>林懿成检正见贻次韵谢之林乃同年</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529226")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529226_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529226'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529226'>集英唱第偶追攀，老着青衫独汗颜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529226'>富贵逼公那得谢，云泉招我久应闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529226'>鸾台看展经纶手，鳌禁行趋供奉班。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529226'>黄发故人空跂想，应无春梦到林间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529226'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529226_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　在会稽。任浙东提刑期间，有文多篇。作品：论私贩茶盐。乞令县丞兼治狱事。论重监司之选。论断罪囚。论禁戢私酒。答交代谢少卿启。<div id='poem_1220291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论私贩茶盐劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220291")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220291'>某窃见私贩茶盐者皆不逞之人，平时贱买贵卖于乡村，往往家至户到，不容其不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220291_comment'></div>而畏法者稍不从，必怀私憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220291_comment'></div>他日或败，置于有司，乃妄通豪民及素所雠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220291_comment'></div>傥或不能为，狱吏者必讽其为之，盖利豪民之赴狱而有所求索也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220291_comment'></div>及已断罪，追纳赏钱，或无所出，则又妄均摊于平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220291_comment'></div>所至官司虽知其诈，例皆容之，恬不为怪，重使良民被害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220291_comment'></div>欲乞自今后因茶盐干连无实状之人，不许留禁，止令知在供證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220291_comment'></div>其犯人果无财产可以充赏，不得乱有均摊，止监邻保备还所赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220291_comment'></div>狱吏绝于觊望，罪不及于无辜，且邻保者必加互察，不容其私矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220291_comment'></div>伏望朝廷详酌施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1220291_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220225' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220225' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220225?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令县丞兼治狱事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220225")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220225_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220225'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220225'>臣窃惟治狱之官，号为难能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220225_comment'></div>责任专一，俾得究心，犹不能保其不为奸吏所移，而况任之不专者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220225_comment'></div>县狱是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220225_comment'></div>狱之初，情实在于县，自县而达之州，虽有异同，要之以县狱所鞫为祖，利害不轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220225_comment'></div>今所谓县令者，旦朝受牒诉，暮夜省案牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220225_comment'></div>牒诉之多，或至数百，少者不下数十，案牍之繁，堆几溢格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220225_comment'></div>其间名为强敏者，随事剖决，不至滞淹，已不可多得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220225_comment'></div>傥复责其馀力，足办狱事，讯鞠得情，吏不敢欺，民不被害，诚恐百人之中，未必有一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220225_comment'></div>郡之狱事，则有两院治狱之官，若某当追，若某当讯，若某当被五木，率具检以禀，郡守曰可则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220225_comment'></div>至县则不然，令既不暇专察，佐官虽名通签，终以嫌疑，不敢侵预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220225_comment'></div>其追呼讯鞫，具名以禀，悉出吏手，故其事与州郡不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220225_comment'></div>臣恭惟陛下躬好生之德，视民如伤，宽诏屡下，未尝不以哀矜庶狱为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220225_comment'></div>如此，利害较然明白，而人莫敢以县邑专置狱官为请者，诚恐增员太多故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220225_comment'></div>臣愚见以为县狱之事，宜专委丞，如州郡两院之官，日入治狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220225_comment'></div>凡追呼枷讯等事，丞先以禀令，然后得行，其馀悉如旧制，则丞无侵预之嫌，令有同心之助，相为可否，其得必多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220225_comment'></div>借使为丞者未必皆能，其事不犹愈乎付之黠吏之手乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220225_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐详酌施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220225_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220225_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220226?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论重监司之选劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220226")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220226_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220226'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220226'>臣窃惟设官分职，内外小大，各有体统，轻重之势失之毫釐，则名已不正矣，况其实乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220226_comment'></div>国朝以来，诸路监司之官，于秩虽卑而责任则重，总按一道，纠察其奸而督其稽违，莫敢不肃者，以郡守之官其秩亦卑，得相临制之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220226_comment'></div>方今舆地未复，州郡数少，侍从加多，前日号为最小郡垒，往往以处侍从，而以庶官临之，轻重之势于是倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220226_comment'></div>汉制，部刺史秩六百石，今监司是也，而郡太守乃二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220226_comment'></div>故何武、翟方进论之，以为《春秋》之义，用贵治贱，不以卑临尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220226_comment'></div>刺史位下大夫而临二千石，轻重不相准，失位次之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220226_comment'></div>其事类今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220226_comment'></div>臣愚以为在今之日，宜增重监司之任，转运使副至提点刑狱并以曾任侍从官为之，提举茶盐市舶等并以曾任左右司郎中以上为之，庶几轻重相准，得位次之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220226_comment'></div>而况轻重之柄，实在朝廷，以为重则重，以为轻则轻，而亦何常之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220226_comment'></div>伏望圣慈下臣议，更赐详酌施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220226_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220226_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论断罪囚劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220227")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220227'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220227'>臣契勘州县，凡禁勘大辟公事，除深僻幽隐处行劫或谋杀外，其馀杀人，自有一时知见之人，自合一面研穷根勘，务尽情实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220227_comment'></div>其间却有豪强有力之家杀人公事，意在变易情节，嘱托官司，或贿承勘胥吏，多以知證通说未明为由，以乘差官体究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220227_comment'></div>而所差官亦止是一到地头，呼集邻社保甲询问供折而已，然因此得变易情节，出入人罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220227_comment'></div>又况豪右之家，所居乡村宗族，姻亲佃客之属常居其半，宛转为奸，符合供證，致使失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220227_comment'></div>臣愚以行下所属州县约束，应今后承勘大辟公事，并责令当职官先将犯人根问，一时知见之人，追取炤勘，以验囚辞，即不得辄差官体究外，深恐州县不得切遵依，欲望圣慈特降睿旨，立法施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220227_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220227_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220230' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220230?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论禁戢私酒劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220230")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220230'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220230'>臣契勘禁戢私酒及贩外界酒入禁地之法，率计胜㪷，私罪立赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220230_comment'></div>近因官吏申陈，增立告赏，比之绍兴法殆及数倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220230_comment'></div>内有一经告赏，以犯人所居舍屋什物并没官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220230_comment'></div>臣窃观著今有立定笞杖徒流四等，罪赏量所犯大小以为重轻，此不易之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220230_comment'></div>今以犯人所居舍屋什物没官，不分轻重，此何理哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220230_comment'></div>遂致州县行法之际，有所不忍，名为增严，其实废法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220230_comment'></div>臣愚见，欲将造贩私酒及贩外来官酒入禁地之人，如所犯止系笞杖罪，只依旧法赏格追赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220230_comment'></div>若罪至徒流，即行舍屋什物没官指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220230_comment'></div>庶几法意人情，皆得允当，且使可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220230_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220230_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220230_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答交代谢少卿启<span class='inlineComment2'>（任浙东提刑司）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220316")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220316'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220316'>宦游相踵，愧扬秕之在前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220316_comment'></div>王事有期，顾及瓜而当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220316_comment'></div>静言事契，燕及子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220316_comment'></div>夫何迟暮之年，乃有因依之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220316_comment'></div>恭惟某官被文相德，可用为仪，强识博文，足以华国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220316_comment'></div>自结圣神之眷，荐跻清近之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220316_comment'></div>智略辏于上前，风采闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220316_comment'></div>持橐簪笔，谓当入侍于清光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220316_comment'></div>揽辔登车，姑欲少偿于素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220316_comment'></div>岂容煖席，即庆赐环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220316_comment'></div>某猥以庸才，误当使指，阅时既久，责效无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220316_comment'></div>敢缘授受之私，终被含容之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220316_comment'></div>恳旌麾之已戒，罄履舄以非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220316_comment'></div>虽乏告新，庶几道故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220316_comment'></div>其为欣抃，曷既叙陈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220316_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年2月</a>　在会稽。权发遣常州，未赴。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　夏，过严陵，有词和李光。序云：和李泰发尚书泊舟严陵。作品：水调歌头（千古严陵濑）<span class='inlineComment2'>（宣和三年（1121），改睦州为严州。）</span><div id='poem_84596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_84596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/84596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>和李泰发尚书泊舟严陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_84596")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_84596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_84596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_84596'>千古严陵濑，清夜月荒凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_84596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_84596'>水明沙净，波面一叶弄孤光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_84596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_84596'>北望旄头天际，杀气遥昏楚甸，云树失青苍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_84596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_84596'>愁绝未归客，衰鬓点吴霜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_84596_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_84596'>听江边，鸣宝瑟，想英皇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_84596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_84596'>骑鲸仙裔，高韵清绝胜风篁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_84596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_84596'>醉入无何境界，却笑昔人底事，远慕白云乡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_84596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_84596'>不见咸阳道，烟草茂陵荒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_84596_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='29763e1fa36c46d0a2b3dc1aeaaada4f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("29763e1fa36c46d0a2b3dc1aeaaada4f");'><span id='29763e1fa36c46d0a2b3dc1aeaaada4f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，53岁</div><div id='29763e1fa36c46d0a2b3dc1aeaaada4f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　秋，刘一止迁居桐庐县鸬鹚源，沈与求有诗以寄，刘一止有诗唱和，并与方允迪、江子我唱和。作品：携家从允迪借居鸬鹚源上沈必先侍御有诗宠其行次韵并呈二公二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗题据《全宋诗》卷一四四八，第16698页。是以北京图书馆藏清擁万堂《苕溪集》为底本，又校以影印文渊阁《四库全书》本《苕溪集》，然《四库全书》本《苕溪集》卷五诗题中“携家”二字作“檇李”，《全宋诗》并未校出。）</span><div id='poem_529211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>携家从允迪借居鸬鹚源上沈必先侍御有诗宠其行次韵并呈二公二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529211")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529211'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529211'>飘零暮景今如许，惭愧高人久卧庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529211'>好客儿童总欢喜，多情草木自扶疏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529211'>百年梦幻真何有，一壑风烟尚借居。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529211'>寄谢南台温御史，此身休戚正关渠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529211'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529211_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529212?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529212'>向来多病更多忧，命与谁谋出怨仇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529212'>坐念甘泉方避暑，不知楚泽又悲秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529212'>长蛇肆毒心犹在，战马何时鞚暂休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529212'>横榻故人身卫主，素书能复讯侬不<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作不复讥侬）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529212'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529212_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　秋，刘一止迁居桐庐县鸬鹚源，有诗次韵沈与求，并寄郑唯心。作品：次韵必先侍御和忆梅并寄维心。<div id='poem_529215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529215?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵必先侍御和郑维心忆梅并寄维心</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529215")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529215'>紫梅溪上春先到，馀不沙边草未芳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529215'>五字真曾赋桑落，四弦犹忆调枫香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529215'>雪中孤艳应愁绝，竹外斜枝不掩藏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529215'>永望佳人在空谷，此时幽独未须伤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529215'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529215_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在桐庐鸬鹚源，有诗次韵沈次律。作品：再用韵寄沈次律学士。<div id='poem_529216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月23日</a>　在桐庐鸬鹚源。秋分，有诗次韵江子我。作品：次韵子我秋分一首。<div id='poem_529274' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529274' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_529274_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在桐庐鸬鹚源，有诗送方滋赴官浙西。作品：送方务德提干赴官浙西。<div id='poem_529228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送方务德提干赴官浙西一首<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在桐庐鸬鹚源，有词贺叶梦得寿辰。作品：蓦山溪（卿云衍苒）<div id='poem_84628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_84628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_84628_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_84628'>声名德业，汉代谁居右。<div id='poem_sentence_3_84628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_84628_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在桐庐鸬鹚源。年底，有诗唱和方允迪、江子我。作品：再用韵呈允迪秘监江子我郎中二首。<div id='poem_529213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再用韵呈允迪秘监江子我郎中二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　居桐庐期间，拆字为戏，有诗寄江子我。作品：山居作拆字诗一首寄江子我郎中比尝以拆字语为戏然未有以为诗者请自今始。<div id='poem_529159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529159' class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529159")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529159'>日月明朝昏，山风岚自起。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529159'>石皮破仍坚<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作拈壁）</span>，古木枯不死。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529159'>可人何当来，意若重千里。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529159'>永言咏黄鹄，志士心未已。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529159_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　居桐庐期间，刘一止有诗呈方允迪道踪昆仲。作品：借居鸬鹚山中一首呈方允迪道踪昆仲。<div id='poem_529158' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529158' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529158?labeling=true' target='_blank'>借居鸬鹚山中一首呈方允迪道踪昆仲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529158")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529158'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529158'>长松舞高寒，落涧泻清泚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529158'>笙簧响天上，金石鸣地底。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529158'>云容何润泽，下有隐君子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529158'>乐此山水音，清若变流徵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529158'>怪我从何来，尘土两目眯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529158'>寇戎在江浒，荐食心未已。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529158'>赤囊走边报，朝暮异忧喜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529158'>安知隐人乐，胜绝有如此。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529158'>古来成败事，不入山中耳。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529158'>愿言晚相收，置我岩壑里。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529158'>酌泉得醒心，茹朮可不死。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529158'>况有载酒人，半道同栗里<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　居桐庐期间，刘一止有诗次韵江子我。作品：次韵江子我郎中社饮一首。<div id='poem_529273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵江子我郎中社饮一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529273")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_529273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529273'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529273'>社醵遗风在，田家礼数饶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529273'>玉人疑解意，孺子故来邀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529273'>御寇惊先馈，庚桑惧见杓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529273'>习乡俱尚齿，惇族悟疏苗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529273'>未见雕戈静，方欣玉烛调。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529273'>山寒时作暝，火老不成歊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529273'>酾酒无留榼，蒸豚发堕樵。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529273'>蛮讴声带苦，村舞拍频招。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529273'>野性疏钟鼎，官身脱市朝。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529273'>形随石骨瘦，心与涧花彫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529273'>朔漠音尘断，膻胡意气骄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529273'>谁为今定远，空作老边韶。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529273'>枉矢知天变，双桃验服妖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529273'>献书惭痛哭，避地独无聊。<div id='poem_sentence_13_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_529273'>复古周宣治，中兴太白谣。<div id='poem_sentence_14_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_529273'>明年及春社，愁鬓雪应消。<div id='poem_sentence_15_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_529273'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_529273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_529273'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_529273_0'>⑴ 自注：宣和宫女头作冠，双桃相并，谓文并桃冠，人以桃音逃，为今日之谶。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_529273_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

余姚

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　兵乱中，刘一止携家避乱至余姚胡宗汲家，有诗赠之。作品：和胡浚明村中好客稀五字并作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年（1131）改越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_529132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和胡浚明村中好客稀五字并作一首</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_529132'>青山为郭云当门，疏烟细雨梅花村。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529132'>门前落涧泻寒溜，衮衮似是通河源。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529132'>隐居二士清而通，谈道不愧将无同。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529132'>何人载酒问奇字，糟床夜注时一中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529132'>天骥权奇嗟欲老，家有龙驹头尺好。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529132'>孙郎并舍真可人，散乱书签共探讨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529132'>只今干戈迷所适，我亦间关暂投迹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529132'>君家鸟雀不惊人，应怪苍黄如此客。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529132'>谋身已拙知遁肥，邂逅得此良亦稀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529132'>化云所愿四方逐，念绝侧翅随人飞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529132'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_529132_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月</a>　避地姚江，力劝傅崧卿起义师。<br /></div>

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fd81158b9a654bdfa8bc38eb59ba1d15_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fd81158b9a654bdfa8bc38eb59ba1d15");'><span id='fd81158b9a654bdfa8bc38eb59ba1d15_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1132')">1130-1132年</a>，53-55岁</div><div id='fd81158b9a654bdfa8bc38eb59ba1d15' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在临安，为李邴所荐，刘一止除详定一司敕令所删定官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年5月10日</a>　在临安，召试馆职，因对策，极言当世之务。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年6月25日</a>　在临安。除秘书省校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月</a>　在临安。因程俱申请，有旨令修篡日历，刘一止上书力辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月28日</a>　在临安。除监察御史，上疏论用君子小人之说。作品：上殿论用君子小人之说。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上殿论用君子小人之说劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年9月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220219")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220219'>臣闻天下之治，众君子成之而不足，一小人败之而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220219_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220219_comment'></div>君子虽众，其道则孤，小人虽寡，其势易蔓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220219_comment'></div>君子之忧在于天下国家，小人之忧在于一身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220219_comment'></div>君子之于法度纪纲，必欲正之，故为之也难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220219_comment'></div>小人之于法度纪纲，必欲乱之，故为之也易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220219_comment'></div>自古圣贤之君，未尝不欲近君子而远小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220219_comment'></div>小不加察，而小人已至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220219_comment'></div>故《立政》之书曰：「继自今立政，其勿以憸人，其惟吉士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220219_comment'></div>又曰：「时则勿有间之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220219_comment'></div>所谓间之者，非君子小人并进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220219_comment'></div>众君子而一小人，亦足以为间而败政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220219_comment'></div>臣请以《易》之说明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220219_comment'></div>《夬》之为卦，以五阳决一阴，阳为君子，阴为小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220219_comment'></div>故《系辞》曰：「继，决也，刚决柔也，君子道长，小人道忧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220219_comment'></div>夫以五君子决一小人，不曰小人道消而曰道忧，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220219_comment'></div>盖上下交而志同，如《泰》之时，然后小人之道不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220219_comment'></div>若乃以五君子临一小人，徒能使之忧而已矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220219_comment'></div>惟其有忧，则将图之，无不至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220219_comment'></div>恭惟陛下躬天纵之圣，懋日新之举，通达古今，洞照治体，日者好恶既明，黜陟既允矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220219_comment'></div>臣犹以是为言者，诚以事之几微，小不加察，则小人者乘间伺隙而入，其害至于败政，不可不惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220219_comment'></div>臣以一介之贱，骤对清光，谓天下事尤急于君子小人之说，故首用为献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220219_comment'></div>伏惟留神幸察，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1220219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月29日</a>　在临安。上疏请刊法令，从之。作品：论尚书六曹及百司法令之弊。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论尚书六曹及百司法令之弊劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220222")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220222'>臣愚不自揣，蒙恩擢寘台察之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220222_comment'></div>伏见尚书六曹下逮百司，比所用法令，初无画一之论，类以人吏省记便为与夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220222_comment'></div>盖法令具在，奸吏犹得侮之，今乃一切听其省记，顾欺弊何所不有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220222_comment'></div>欲与则陈与例，欲夺则陈夺例，或与或夺，在其牙颊，其患可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220222_comment'></div>陛下圣明，灼见此弊，尝降处分，令左右司郎官以其省记之文刊定颁行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220222_comment'></div>然左右司职事号为最烦，窃恐于此不能专一，无由速得成书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220222_comment'></div>臣愚伏望圣慈持降睿旨，改送详定一司敕令所，立限刊定，镂板颁降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220222_comment'></div>内吏部条法最为急务，乞责近限，先次施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220222_comment'></div>庶几杜绝奸吏弄法受贿之弊，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220222_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1220222_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在临安。有文祭父母。作品：焚黄祭文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>焚黄祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220398")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220398'>某不肖，承先人绪业，游学觅举垂三十载，名八上于春官，再宾兴于乡里，年踰强仕，始窃一第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220398_comment'></div>三釜之禄，不逮亲存，心自悼念，罪通于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220398_comment'></div>又十一年，通籍于朝，得官御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220398_comment'></div>会天子明堂礼成，眷及幽显，赠先人之官从八品，实为初典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220398_comment'></div>先妣曰太安人，超初赠二等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220398_comment'></div>某属有官守，不获躬展墓下，谨遣长孙峦奉纶綍以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220398_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220398_comment'></div>漏泉之泽，虽曰有光，陟岵之思，惟知罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220398_comment'></div>仰祈不昧，服此上恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1220398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在临安。有文祭刘焘。作品：祭族兄无言修撰文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭族兄无言修撰文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220401")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220401'>呜呼，天之生才，岂曰无意，既授之以能为之质，必处之以可为之地，苟异于是者，其必有谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220401_comment'></div>夫天地之秀，在人为贤才，在物为山岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220401_comment'></div>彼山岳者亦贵夫为群物之利，是故丹砂金玉之宝，楩楠栝柏之材，取之而不穷，用之而不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220401_comment'></div>至于奇峰峭壁，无所依而独峙，不借土以发生，则世不求其用，而以为瑰伟绝特之观，盖造物者之戏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220401_comment'></div>呜呼，公之生也，自其少时，有不可抑之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220401_comment'></div>既沉涵乎六籍，又均贯夫百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220401_comment'></div>其雄辞妙思，裂金石而感鬼神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220401_comment'></div>《风》、《雅》、《离骚》，配圣经而发鼓吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220401_comment'></div>当其抵掌而剧谈，操笔而论著，老师宿儒，引避太息，而后辈初学，袖手屏息而侧睨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220401_comment'></div>使其从容夜半，奉宣室之问，曾何有夫贾生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220401_comment'></div>代言内相，参戡难之功，而使武夫悍卒，感泣思奋，亦何取夫陆贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220401_comment'></div>顾四纪之回翔，尝践更乎中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220401_comment'></div>虽复踞蓬山之上游，赞明堂之坐治，与夫为使者牧守，所至有绝人之称，而用违所长，故识者以为公之才未试也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220401_comment'></div>呜呼，今则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220401_comment'></div>岂非造物者用公为戏剧，且自誇其神丽耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220401_comment'></div>仆又悲夫人谁不达，而公独弗遇其如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220401_comment'></div>仆等于公有昆弟宗族之亲，而兼师友之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220401_comment'></div>曾阅历之几何，乃暌违而隔世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220401_comment'></div>感知遇于畴昔，心怅焉而增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220401_comment'></div>念后夜之莫追，溯西风而陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220401_comment'></div>独缄词以寓哀，尚平生之不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220401_comment'></div>呜呼，词有穷矣，而哀未既也，公其闻知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220401_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1220401_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　在临安。举荐张九成取进士第一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月27日</a>　在临安。诏置修政局，上札子言省费裕国、强兵息民之策。作品：论侥幸之门不塞。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span>论财用。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span>应诏条具利害状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论侥倖之门不塞劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220287")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220287'>某尝闻朝廷之患在侥倖之门不塞，侥倖之门不塞由至公之路未开，好恶以是屡移，纲纪为之浸弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220287_comment'></div>数十年来，奸憸显行，蠹弊百出，职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220287_comment'></div>所赖以救世者，在大贤君子居上而力持之，如其持之不力，则至公之路必不开，侥倖之门必不塞，抑恐有以召之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220287_comment'></div>某请言一二事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220287_comment'></div>祖宗以来，人材进用，非功德盛大，才能超异，未有遽至显要者，大抵由外以及内，更历既熟，且须以岁月之久，始见选除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220287_comment'></div>今也内为省郎，外为监司，有未历二数考者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220287_comment'></div>侥倖之徒，殚竭日力，奔走求合，不复知分守之可安，不曰有以召之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220287_comment'></div>入仕之初，必由铨选，其来久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220287_comment'></div>今也后进少年仅得一官，即以参部为辱，夤缘请托，求为王官，次则辟举，往往得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220287_comment'></div>求而不得，其路自塞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220287_comment'></div>求而得之，何病而不求，不曰有以召之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220287_comment'></div>中外百职，初无异才，今朝廷之士入而不出，服职在外者虽有异能显效，不见召用，间有召者，则群起而诋之，恐其妨己进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220287_comment'></div>两途既分，向之乐事劝功者且化为苟简矣，不曰有以召之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220287_comment'></div>亲丧而夺情从仕者，盖士之所不忍，而朝廷非军兴抢攘，且其人才实足以当重寄者，不轻为此举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220287_comment'></div>异时虽迪功郎之微亦起复为州县官，甚者有亲丧未绝而先期求起复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220287_comment'></div>今此风未尽革也，特假从军之名，以为出仕之地耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220287_comment'></div>故士之无耻者，不复安于执丧，不曰有以召之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220287_comment'></div>事之可言，非特此数者而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220287_comment'></div>某窃谓救时之弊，莫先于至公，行此一言，疑若不难，且其事若迂缓，非所当急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220287_comment'></div>然而理有必至者，公道行则好恶明，好恶明则赏罚当，赏罚当则吏各尽其能，而贤者乐出为用，贤者乐出为用，则内治举而外侮销矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220287_comment'></div>在今之日，恢至公之道而力持之，岂无望于大贤君子也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220287_comment'></div>然以此属相公者，非特某也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220287_comment'></div>干冒钧严，无任恐惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1220287_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论财用劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220290")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220290'>某尝观唐史称，刘晏敛不及民而用度足，初未之信，及考其所以致之之术，大抵笼商贾之利而归之公上，以供赀用，故科敛不及于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220290_comment'></div>且山泽之利在商贾久矣，当天下太平无事时，固未尝较。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220290_comment'></div>官取之薄，商贾得之厚，以其利厚，故奔走之而不以为劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220290_comment'></div>不幸有军兴之后，用度日滋，将取之于民，则民力有时而弊，且仁君之所不忍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220290_comment'></div>不然，又不知计之所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220290_comment'></div>当是时也，岂可坐视商贾获甚厚之息而不自为计耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220290_comment'></div>晏之领漕事也，常募善走者，置遽相望，探报四方物价低昂，虽远方不数日皆达使司，食货轻重之权，悉在掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220290_comment'></div>又于诸道置知院官，每旬月具白州县雨雪丰歉之状，丰则贵籴，歉则贱粜，咸以谷易杂货供官用，及于丰处卖之，应民之急，公务交裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220290_comment'></div>其用榷盐法，不但转鬻商人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220290_comment'></div>又官自运载于乏盐州县鬻之，官获其利而民不乏，谓之常平盐事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220290_comment'></div>类此者不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220290_comment'></div>是以贞元之间，虽遭变故，而国用不匮，户口蕃息，由朝廷能尽晏之才，使得专制，故其效如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220290_comment'></div>某以为今日之事，莫若选择近臣之通晓财利者，于濒江要便处置司，听其自辟官属，专制国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220290_comment'></div>仿晏之意，远近移易，贸迁有无，悉从便宜，勿拘之法，得尽其智能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220290_comment'></div>庶几利入之源浸广，有以佐军需而宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220290_comment'></div>伏望朝廷详酌施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1220290_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1220245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应诏条具利害状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220245")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220245'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220245'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220245_comment'></div>臣伏睹今月二十七日手诏，令中外侍从、省台寺监执事官、监司、守令等名实已见的确利害，凡可以省费裕国、强兵息民者，条具以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220245_comment'></div>仍已诏大臣置司修政，有言闻达，悉付讲求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220245_comment'></div>有以见陛下焦劳图治，宵旰靡遑，仰师周宣所以内修政事、外攘夷狄之意，以惠天下，甚盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220245_comment'></div>然臣谓修政之举，置司而讲求之宜也，何宜闻而久未闻耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220245_comment'></div>昔梅福以南昌尉上书乞假轺传至行在所条对急政，四方之士，固愿效其所闻，以为所不当缓，如福者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220245_comment'></div>及今始求之，岂亦所谓急政者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220245_comment'></div>方今中原版荡，九庙播迁，外忧猾夏之远夷，内有弄兵之群寇，而又僭伪窃国之人，反侧自疑，日夜谋我，言政之急，未有如今日者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220245_comment'></div>陛下诏臣等以省费裕国、强兵息民之事，固议者所当急久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220245_comment'></div>然事不素讲而求之于一朝夕之间，所谓足国裕民者，诚不知其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220245_comment'></div>欲足国则民不裕，欲裕民则国不足，一旦用度有阙，郡县吏不过阴取于民，以应公上之须，陛下亦莫得而知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220245_comment'></div>所谓省费强兵之事亦然，欲省费则兵不益，欲益兵则费不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220245_comment'></div>加又有乌合招来之寇，存之则縻费廪食，不足恃以为强，汰之则无所归日覆出为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220245_comment'></div>议者处此，诚知其难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220245_comment'></div>今日欲为陛下论之，而不知所当先，则为不知言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220245_comment'></div>陛下问修政于群臣，而不先期所自为，则为不知政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220245_comment'></div>今日之事，在陛下躬行者，顾莫先于省费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220245_comment'></div>非谓天下之费必待陛下而省也，以为不如是，则不足以感人心而示好恶，政之本不立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220245_comment'></div>臣愚不肖，待罪台属，于兹有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220245_comment'></div>窃闻陛下小心如成康，俭德如文景，笃好书传，踰于声色，尚方服用，简朴无华，与士庶之家等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220245_comment'></div>搢绅交叹，以为圣虑宏达，不以一日奢靡快意为乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220245_comment'></div>然迩来议者颇谓岁取左藏库金帛之数不减全盛时，有司告病，缙绅惑焉，岂陛下俭于一躬，而赐予或未节耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220245_comment'></div>且左右亲近之人至无厌也，不以礼法抑之，将何时而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220245_comment'></div>仁宗皇帝尝语侍臣曰：「左藏库月供钱千二百缗，此周王所谓供王之好用，朕宫中无所费，其令罢之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220245_comment'></div>当是时，左右亲近之人非不多也，然而无所觊觎者，知不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220245_comment'></div>又况其间畏义知耻，与上同休戚者，虽予之，将辞焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220245_comment'></div>其不然者，皆贪得无厌，不与上同休戚者也，又何恤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220245_comment'></div>且陛下厚于及人，而以身当天下之谤，其无乃自为谋者疏邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220245_comment'></div>臣愿少抑赐予之费，与所谓杂色供奉冗食无用之人，稍镌减之，示好恶于天下，则修政之本已立，其事为之末乃可议耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220245_comment'></div>夫修政之日，无微而不当举，议将次第而行之，莫若诏监司郡守县令各至所部，询问父老，讲求一方之利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220245_comment'></div>若曰孰利未兴，孰害未除，孰民田有遗垦，孰为知兵，孰材武可用，孰土豪可任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220245_comment'></div>使其当山川控扼沿河濒海之地，则曰某地可守，某地可战，某地可为寨栅庐舍，其处可以积粟漕运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220245_comment'></div>各以方略来上，然后以其说深考而熟计之，度其可者行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220245_comment'></div>间遣近臣巡按某地而核其实，以为之赏罚黜陟，则事无有不得其要领者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220245_comment'></div>今未尝目见耳闻，而独使之汎然论天下之利害，其有益于施行者无几耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220245_comment'></div>赵充国号为通知四夷事者，且曰：「百闻不如一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220245_comment'></div>臣愿驰至金城，图上方略」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220245_comment'></div>况馀人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220245_comment'></div>乃若裕国省费、强兵息民见于事为者，则臣谓莫若求之民兵，盖四者一事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220245_comment'></div>古者兵民为一，故兵不可胜用，而国不知费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220245_comment'></div>赵一国耳，长平之战，四十万人死，其后亦不闻无兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220245_comment'></div>秦男子十五以上悉驱之从军，则是民即兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220245_comment'></div>比年以来，为民兵之说献于上者多矣，卒莫之行，巡社之法既行而旋罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220245_comment'></div>岂朝廷难之以为扰民耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220245_comment'></div>是计之未熟而行之不得其要者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220245_comment'></div>若臣之说则异于是，陛下即行之，不过下半纸檄以颁郡县，郡县承天子诏旨而告之民，民则乐从之矣，初无有甚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220245_comment'></div>盖其说曰：不募不籍不教，不易其名，不夺其业，不系縻于官，不程督以吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220245_comment'></div>如是，故民不扰而乐从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220245_comment'></div>凡县镇乡社之民，通使为之，不欲者勿强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220245_comment'></div>并习兵器，若弓弩戈矛枪挺刀牌等，随其所习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220245_comment'></div>以今所谓保正长者总之，晓以利害，使各保其田桑庐舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220245_comment'></div>境内有寇，悉听捕逐，其获寇之赏，则有常格，见于著令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220245_comment'></div>若遇大盗，并力杀获，则闻于朝，称其事而旌赏之，如效用之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220245_comment'></div>其平居讲习，精于武艺者，听保正长推举，不以多少闻于州郡，州郡按试之，如所举者，为之旌别，蠲其身丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220245_comment'></div>及三犯杖，听赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220245_comment'></div>彼固知保田桑庐舍之利，而又有意外旌赏之宠，无所系縻，无所程督，亦谁惮而不为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220245_comment'></div>今夫群天下之士而试之有司，次第荐送而官使之，彼诚利于得官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220245_comment'></div>挟策觅举，虽终老而不悔，曷尝募之使为科举，籍之使不得脱耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220245_comment'></div>使民习兵无以异此，为农为商，不易其名，不夺其业，且将因询暇时，啸其朋俦，自相讲习，梃者击，戈矛者刺，弓弩者驰射，彼归而求之有馀师，又何必驱而教之为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220245_comment'></div>且山谷强悍之民，初未尝教也，而艺绝官军者，所至多有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220245_comment'></div>如曰必驱而教之，使知坐作进退，是犹博士先生缓带徐步、升堂巍坐而谈经，坐诸生堂上，击鼓而进退之，以为文物表仪，化民成俗可也，所谓学者，岂真有待于是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220245_comment'></div>孔子曰：「不教民战，是谓弃之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220245_comment'></div>而臣乃以乡社之兵为不必教者，非兵无事于教也，以其势与官军不同，非仰食公上者之所系至众，一或扰之，将不乐从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220245_comment'></div>藉令习业不精，假之岁月，所得十一，不已多乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220245_comment'></div>呜呼，兵之弊甚矣，其患有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220245_comment'></div>在祖宗之时，平居无事，则竭天下之力以养兵，在今日国势阽危，则竭天下之力以养乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220245_comment'></div>今臣之说虽未能销患于赫赫之际，而能为陛下销患于冥冥之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220245_comment'></div>虽未能足国裕民于一朝夕之间，而能为陛下足国裕民于三岁之后，且为久远无穷之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220245_comment'></div>若以三岁之后无救目前，用置不讲，则是其弊终不可救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220245_comment'></div>愿陛下下臣章杂议，若以为可，则立为赏功劝劳之典，参酌旧所著令，损益而施行之，此臣所不能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220245_comment'></div>或曰，臣之说朝廷非不闻也，不果行者，惧民之知兵且为乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220245_comment'></div>臣曰不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220245_comment'></div>强悍之民崛起山谷，十百为群，轻犯县镇，居民无远近多寡，望风奔走，与异时敌人所至，率以一步卒联十百人而驱之，拱手屈膝，以受箠击，莫敢与抗者，非不顾其生也，诚未尝闻斗战击刺之事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1220245_comment'></div>仅有一能者，则荷戈持挺出当之矣，此臣所耳闻而目见者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1220245_comment'></div>借令一乡社之民自起为盗，则有他乡之兵制之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1220245_comment'></div>一县镇之民为盗，则有他县镇之兵制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1220245_comment'></div>矧未必皆然，即臣之念至熟悉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1220245_comment'></div>虽然，臣窃观陛下诏大臣说宫属，置司讲论，以修政为名，诚美矣，顾所以称是名者宜何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1220245_comment'></div>使一国之政如一家之政，小大快心，上下告语，毕精穷思，推忠尽诚，罔有嫌隙，不顾望陛下风旨，不迎合大臣论议，惓惓焉，闵闵焉，惟恐一事之有遗策，一物之有遁情，则庶几焉臻于有成，可日月冀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1220245_comment'></div>如其好是美名而不克充其实，且聚讼交訾，若筑室于道谋，则非独不可以日月冀，抑论议有不出于至公者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1220245_comment'></div>元丰条例之举，崇宁讲议之名，事出权臣，弊政充塞，贻天下患害，至今未艾也，愿陛下察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1220245_comment'></div>臣愚无知识，姑陈其槩，以塞圣问，伏惟留神幸察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1220245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月16日</a>　在临安。迁起居郎。上辞免状。作品：辞免除起居郎状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220232?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除起居郎状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220232")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220232'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220232'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220232_comment'></div>右，臣今月某日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣起居郎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220232_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220232_comment'></div>伏念臣才智庸下，自叨亲擢，未有丝发仰酬鸿造，而骤加六察，迁为二史，近世以来罕有此例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220232_comment'></div>况记注之任，言动是司，比因时巡，此典几废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220232_comment'></div>方陛下举修故事，遴简史官，宜得方正博洽之士，以称兹选，臣独何人，乃敢冒据？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220232_comment'></div>抑臣近缘多病，尝有丐闲之请，尚闻俞旨，更蒙超授，益非所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220232_comment'></div>伏望圣慈曲赐矜察，追寝成命，遂臣前恳，庶允公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220232_comment'></div>所有恩命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220232_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1220232_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在临安。夏秋间，有诗赋程瑀漫吾亭。作品：赋程伯禹给事漫吾亭一首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_529167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529167")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529167'>道州固伤时，晚岁吾山溪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529167'>彼物何曾争，我自分两畦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529167'>宣州绝代贤，雅志苏群黎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529167'>胸次包峥嵘，不肯去<span id='poem_sentence_4_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529167'>渺观身世空，万境俱一齐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529167'>浪云出处殊，不悟东自西。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529167'>向来功名辙，复入山水蹊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529167'>公今持左符，早晚朝金闺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529167'>生贤出世间，渠能绝攀跻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529167'>要须了此心，泛应忘高低。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529167'>昔我盖已漫，今我亦非迷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529167'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_529167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年8月25日</a>　在临安，因极陈堂吏宦官之蠹，罢职，主管台州崇道观。上谢表。作品：谢主管台州崇道观表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220247' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220247' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220247?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢主管台州崇道观表<span class='inlineComment2'>（罢起居郎责授）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220247")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220247_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220247'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220247'>祗奉训辞，伏思适咎，惟臣自取，跼地知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220247_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>伏念臣出自寒微，误膺简拔，以锄耰固陋之质，历台省清近之班，自始及终，不由他力，从顶至踵，皆出上恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220247_comment'></div>而臣所更既多，未有裨补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220247_comment'></div>欲效其议，则窃自薄陋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220247_comment'></div>以为可用，则无所短长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220247_comment'></div>仰惟圣德之方隆，内惧史书之有阙，臣之宜去，谁不谓然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220247_comment'></div>不图威命之行，尚得祠官之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220247_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下游心太古，侧席异闻，作成士类而明试以功，爱惜人材而阔略其过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220247_comment'></div>怜臣之罪以戆，察臣之志靡他，薄示谴呵，止投闲散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220247_comment'></div>省躬己辜，固将安分之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220247_comment'></div>没齿何言，惟有负恩之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220247_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220247_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='388a4466a2d24584b73403753399611c_label'><a
