ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1139')">1138-1139年</a>，61-62岁</div><div id='388a4466a2d24584b73403753399611c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年9月7日</a>　在临安。试秘书少监。上辞免状。作品：辞免秘书少监状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋建炎三年(1129)，高宗避金兵自扬州南渡至杭州，以州治为行宫，升杭州为临安府。）</span><div id='poem_1220238' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220238' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220238?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免秘书少监状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220238")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220238_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220238'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220238'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220238_comment'></div>右，今月十五日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，刘某除秘书少监者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220238_comment'></div>选抡误及，恐惧靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220238_comment'></div>伏念某人地凡下，学问空疏，去国七年，自意此身，终老岩穴，敢图误恩，复见收录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220238_comment'></div>矧中秘清华，号为妙选，宜得一时魁垒博洽之士，为之领袖，如某之陋，岂堪冒居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220238_comment'></div>伏望钧慈特赐敷奏，追寝成命，除某在外宫观差遣一次，庶于愚分，得以稍安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220238_comment'></div>伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220238_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年10月22日</a>　在临安。行李光除吏部尚书制。作品：知洪州李光除吏部尚书。<div id='poem_1219901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知洪州李光除吏部尚书制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年10月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219901")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219901'>朕忧勤在御，当馈兴嗟，思得耆艾骨鲠、谋国不贰之臣，献纳论思，以裨予治，以表庶工，俾四方万里之远，耸闻而跂慕，知朝廷之尊，不待告令而民自化焉，顾不伟哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219901_comment'></div>具官某师古圣贤，执义坚固，志节之厉，凛如秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219901_comment'></div>被遇累朝，始终惟一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219901_comment'></div>出入中外，险夷屡更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219901_comment'></div>朕熟察其所言，又详试之以事，盖有日矣，是用召从藩屏，还长天官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219901_comment'></div>激浊扬清，惟尔之旧，谋猷告后，益罄厥忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219901_comment'></div>使朕知人之明不愧于古，尔则与有无穷之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219901_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1219901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月21日</a>　在临安。试起居郎。上辞免状。作品：辞免再除起居郎状。<div id='poem_1220233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免再除起居郎状<span class='inlineComment2'>（自秘书少监再除此职。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220233")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220233'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220233'>右，臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>伏念臣赋性颛蒙，受才凡下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220233_comment'></div>曩膺误眷，擢寘近班，进直螭坳，退居鸾省，贪宠冒没，忘己空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220233_comment'></div>量既过而不知，悔且晚而何及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220233_comment'></div>间闻孤外，阅岁未多，拂拭使令，于臣已厚，傥复冒已试罔功之贵，犯求多不韪之愆，岂定命之当安，抑公朝之难幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220233_comment'></div>伏望大明委照，宏造曲成，察其所陈，出于非伪，追还成命，更选异能，庶使臣愚，获免官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220233_comment'></div>所有恩命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220233_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月21日</a>　在临安。行向子諲转一官致仕制。<div id='poem_1220136' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220136' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220136?labeling=true' target='_blank'>向子諲转一官致仕制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220136")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220136_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220136'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220136'>敕：乐于进为，则以逢时是幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220136_comment'></div>安于静退，则以得去为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220136_comment'></div>钟鼎山林，各存志慕，朕又乌能必以官职之事累之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220136_comment'></div>具官某修洁博习，甚敏而文，励行砥名，自殊肺腑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220136_comment'></div>阅历多故，勤劳百为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220136_comment'></div>顷辞法从之班，出领辅藩之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220136_comment'></div>浩然请老，去不待年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220136_comment'></div>结社香山，岂特栖心于澹泊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220136_comment'></div>角巾东路，殆将卒岁以优游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220136_comment'></div>贤哉大夫，自此远矣，进官一等，用宠其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220136_comment'></div>服我训辞，益绥寿祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220136_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220136_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月22日</a>　在临安。行王庶充资政殿学士知潭州制。作品：枢密副使左通议大夫王庶除资政殿学士知潭州。<div id='poem_1219898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密副使左通议大夫王庶除资政殿学士知潭州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219898")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219898'>朕缉熙庶政，允资左右之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219898_comment'></div>体貌大臣，务极始终之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219898_comment'></div>虽进退之间或异，而内外之势惟均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219898_comment'></div>具官王某气禀直方，学兼文武，夙负敢为之略，独高应变之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219898_comment'></div>草木知其威名，夷狄问其年状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219898_comment'></div>朕念兵民之大计，求缙绅之实能，召自远方，俾还近列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219898_comment'></div>旋授枢机之柄，方须帷幄之筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219898_comment'></div>何引疾之甚坚，屡抗章而莫止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1219898_comment'></div>眷湖湘襟带之地，连东南形势之区，疲氓未苏，邻盗仅息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1219898_comment'></div>是用开元戎之巨屏，锡秘殿之隆名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1219898_comment'></div>勉为朕行，徒得君重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1219898_comment'></div>勿谓长沙之地狭，不足回旋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1219898_comment'></div>当思陇右之风流，尚在忼慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1219898_comment'></div>服我明命，伫观壮猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1219898_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1219898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月22日</a>　在临安。勾龙如渊除御史中丞制。作品：中书舍人勾龙如渊除御史中丞。<div id='poem_1219899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书舍人勾龙如渊除御史中丞制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219899")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219899'>御史列职，皆朕耳目之官，而中执法实为之长，其任重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219899_comment'></div>苟非其人，朕不虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219899_comment'></div>具官某蕴经济之术，负绝特之才，授自时髦，荐更器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219899_comment'></div>学通以博，若贾谊之明治安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219899_comment'></div>论政而坚，若陆贽之本仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219899_comment'></div>每献可而替否，不吐刚而茹柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219899_comment'></div>逮其立言，足以华国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219899_comment'></div>考稽公议，益简朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1219899_comment'></div>是用命尔总持宪纲，以肃在位，俾中外士夫知朝廷之尊，有简书之畏，则予汝嘉，是曰称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1219899_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1219899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月25日</a>　在临安。行汪藻修史成书升显谟阁学士制。<div id='poem_1219928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汪藻修史成书升显谟阁学士制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219928")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219928'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219928'>敕：朕任贤能而责实，惟恐或遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219928_comment'></div>懋爵赏以劝功，不敢有爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219928_comment'></div>矧禁林之旧德，著艺苑之殊劳，可无涣恩，以昭至意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219928_comment'></div>具官某学贯九渊之邃，才绝千人之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219928_comment'></div>昔膺使令，服在近密，崇论宏议，有补于时，大册高文，悉出其手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219928_comment'></div>悼念两朝之故实，曾无一字之遗馀，出自尔心，不烦朕训，缉文辞于断简，问黜陟于故家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219928_comment'></div>远近异同，靡差岁月，品汇条贯，灿若日星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219928_comment'></div>搜罗旁逮于测幽，诵意不忘于寤寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1219928_comment'></div>左思作赋，既殚十稔之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1219928_comment'></div>马迁成书，自立一家之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1219928_comment'></div>此其来上，深用叹嘉，就升延阁之华，申锡赞书之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1219928_comment'></div>岂惟今日见国体之增光，抑使异时并尔名而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1219928_comment'></div>服我休命，益励厥修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1219928_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1219928_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月6日</a>　在临安。行颜师与补右迪功郎制，词甚伟。高宗叹赏不已，手书之。作品：颜鲁公远孙师与补右迪功郎。<div id='poem_1219953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颜鲁公远孙师与补右迪功郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219953")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219953'>敕具官某：朕遭世中否，思古兴怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219953_comment'></div>眷唐室之多贤，壮平原之大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219953_comment'></div>英风可想，恨不与之同时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219953_comment'></div>遗像俨然，至今犹有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219953_comment'></div>访求远裔，仅齿齐民，肆加异恩，宠以命秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219953_comment'></div>录功臣之世，朕无诮于周诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219953_comment'></div>对前人之光，尔尚存于家范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219953_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1219953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月11日</a>　在临安。行刘大中落职制。作品：刘大中落职依旧宫祠。<div id='poem_1219954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘大中落职依旧宫祠制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219954")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219954'>敕：含齿之类，共知笃于爱亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219954_comment'></div>垂髫之童，亦复羞称不孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219954_comment'></div>岂有居仪刑之重任，为名教之罪人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219954_comment'></div>民罔具瞻，朕有逸罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219954_comment'></div>具官某顷由过听，擢在要津，猥以小才，遂当大用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219954_comment'></div>忘所生之天属，视厥父如路人，炊烟不同，寝疾弗问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219954_comment'></div>事皆有状，闻者寒心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219954_comment'></div>人谁无亲，诚所切齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1219954_comment'></div>览弹章之沓至，知公议之靡容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1219954_comment'></div>其镌秘殿之崇，尚即真祠之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1219954_comment'></div>噫，始终之遇，朕犹屈于彝章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1219954_comment'></div>喜惧之年，尔盍图于改事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1219954_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1219954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月14日</a>　在临安。行王庶落职制。作品：王庶落职宫祠。<div id='poem_1219957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1219957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1219957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王庶落职宫祠制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1219957")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1219957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1219957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1219957'>敕：朕履兹艰虞，靡敢宁处，惟是二三执政，任之不疑，庶几左右宅师，用底于治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1219957_comment'></div>脱或怀徇私之志，无忧国之风，论日以乖，朕将安赖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1219957_comment'></div>具官某曩更中外，粗阅岁时，召自藩维，服在近密，授以枢机之柄，俾参帷幄之筹，所冀同寅，以克有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1219957_comment'></div>而乃大言惑众，小智饰奸，既陈立异之辞，旋有坏成之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1219957_comment'></div>倘谓和戎之非策，则虽执义以何惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1219957_comment'></div>乃因知己之莫留，始欲脱身而要誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1219957_comment'></div>第务死党，宁知有君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1219957_comment'></div>顾已照其肺肝，尚曲全于体貌，假之异数，出殿大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1219957_comment'></div>属公议之既喧，匪私心之敢贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1219957_comment'></div>其镌秘殿，往即真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1219957_comment'></div>噫，才各有长，尔岂无用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1219957_comment'></div>任过其量，朕则使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1219957_comment'></div>服此训言，毋忘循省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1219957_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1219957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月25日</a>　在临安。试中书舍人，上辞免状。作品：辞免中书舍人状。<div id='poem_1220234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免中书舍人状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220234")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220234'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220234'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220234_comment'></div>右，臣今月某日三省同奉圣旨，除臣中书舍人，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220234_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220234_comment'></div>窃以中书出号令之地，舍人掌文宗之官，非徒取于词章，抑预闻于政事，职任甚重，付委实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220234_comment'></div>自非博极群书，通达国体，言足以敷德意志虑之美，文足以穷讨论润色之工，则何以增焕皇猷，式孚民听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220234_comment'></div>伏念臣素出贫贱，初无艺能，遭遇圣明，猥叨识拔，曾知恩而未报，顾忍耻以自怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220234_comment'></div>及此衰颓，迄无裨补，敢期过听，俾躐近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220234_comment'></div>念么么之勿胜，惧癫隮之将及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220234_comment'></div>矧七年于外，已绝望于修门，而期月之间，乃再膺于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220234_comment'></div>与其悔罪于烦言啧至之后，孰若投诚于成命未行之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220234_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下隆天地育物之仁，廓日月容光之照，察臣愚悃，匪出伪为，追还涣汗之私，曲遂循墙之请，庶无进越，以速愆尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220234_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220234_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1220234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月25日</a>　在临安。试中书舍人，上谢表。作品：谢除中书舍人表。<div id='poem_1220250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除中书舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220250")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220250'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220250'>载笔殿坳，初远旧物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220250_comment'></div>演论词掖，递锡赞书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220250_comment'></div>恍莫知其所从，凛以荣而为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220250_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以自昔圣主建立非常之功，必有能臣发挥难论之旨，殆天所备，不谋而同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220250_comment'></div>故焕乎谟训誓命之文，于斯为盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220250_comment'></div>而粹然德意志虑之实，罔不自孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220250_comment'></div>矧今纲纪万微，鼓舞庶类，尧言广大，商语丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220250_comment'></div>是非得仲舒之古风，熟崔琳之今事，顾于述作，曷副选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220250_comment'></div>伏念臣器窘而用微，才疏而术陋，自守朴学，甘为臞儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220250_comment'></div>精丧耗于幽忧，艺业荒于不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220250_comment'></div>敢图迟暮之景，猥受圣神之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220250_comment'></div>顶踵皆出于睿恩，践历每从于亲擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220250_comment'></div>至于升华法从，接武近臣，岂其平生，有此过觊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220250_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下聪明稽古，慈恕及人，惟广览兼听之是图，曾小善寸长之不弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220250_comment'></div>况乎盛大德业，比隆于乾坤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220250_comment'></div>昭回文章，第辉于奎璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220250_comment'></div>而臣搜研末技，缀缉谀闻，以腐草之明而裨赫日之光，以秋蝉之翼而增九鼎之重，何能有补，祇益自劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220250_comment'></div>敢不勉竭孤忠，誓坚晚节，虽有惭于润色，庶无奭于告猷。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1220250'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220250_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月2日</a>　在临安。任中书舍人日，上状举陈之渊自代。作品：举陈之渊自代状。<div id='poem_1220243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举陈之渊自代状<span class='inlineComment2'>（任中书舍人日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年1月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220243")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220243'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220243_comment'></div>蒙恩授前件职，准令节文，侍从官授讫三日内举官一员自代者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220243_comment'></div>右，臣伏睹左从事郎、充临安府府学教授陈之渊学问淹通，文辞赡蔚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220243_comment'></div>顷居太学，试选屡优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220243_comment'></div>效官以来，志节弥励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220243_comment'></div>傥见录用，必有可观，举以代臣，实允公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220243_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月</a>　在临安。任便上奏，乞与莫将并罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年2月9日</a>　在临安。行周葵试太常少卿制。作品：周葵太常少卿制。<div id='poem_1220015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周葵太常少卿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年2月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220015")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220015'>敕具官某：朕念边境肃清，民物绥靖，宜公朝典礼之事，增重于观瞻，顾曲台论议之臣，不轻于付畀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220015_comment'></div>尔文备体要，学通天人，顿被简知，荐居华要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220015_comment'></div>召从外服，命典奉常，益观博物之能，垂训责成之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220015_comment'></div>制度多缺，冀贾谊之有陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220015_comment'></div>仪注复尊，赖叔孙之知变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220015_comment'></div>尚思称职，无愧前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220015_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220015_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。行李谊试中书舍人兼直学士院兼侍讲制。<div id='poem_1220025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李谊中书舍人兼直学士院兼侍讲制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220025")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220025'>敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220025_comment'></div>唐虞之制，莫尚于坦明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220025_comment'></div>商周之书，独称于灏噩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220025_comment'></div>盖斯文之兴替，关治道之污隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220025_comment'></div>惟兹播告之修，不匿厥指，则若卜筮之事，罔不是孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220025_comment'></div>代言之难，于斯为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220025_comment'></div>具官某学探圣域，文有古风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220025_comment'></div>顷以时髦，荐更亲擢，肃宪纲于台察，尽规益于棘垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220025_comment'></div>拳拳致主之忠，表表济时之略，载稽公议，益简朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220025_comment'></div>用锡赞书，就升辞掖，兼禁林之典册，侍经帏之深严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220025_comment'></div>非尔之能，其谁有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220025_comment'></div>尚思称塞，以对宠休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220025_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1220025_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。张浚复资政殿大学士充福建路安抚大使兼知福州制。<div id='poem_1220027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张浚复资政殿大学士充福建路安抚大使兼知福州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220027")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220027'>敕：朕当馈思贤，剧安危之注意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220027_comment'></div>殿邦作牧，赖文武之兼资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220027_comment'></div>乃眷迩臣，实惟旧德，肆颁名命，庸示宠私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220027_comment'></div>具官某笃实思和，刚明卓伟，忠可贯于金石，信自通于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220027_comment'></div>许国以来，视身何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220027_comment'></div>相朕艰难之际，备殚夙夜之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220027_comment'></div>功在王家，事藏盟府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220027_comment'></div>慨念投闲之久，属当谋帅之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220027_comment'></div>惟长乐之奥区，盖七闽之重镇，耕桑阜盛，民俗安恬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220027_comment'></div>欲并协于师虞，宜莫如于宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220027_comment'></div>通籍秘殿，增光元戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220027_comment'></div>风物不殊，曾是经行之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220027_comment'></div>旌麾所指，共知条教之新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220027_comment'></div>勉为朕行，徒得君重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220027_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220027_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。行勾龙如渊罢御史中丞提举宫观制。<div id='poem_1220028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>勾龙如渊罢御史中丞提举宫观制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220028")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220028'>敕：朕于废置予夺之命，若天地之化，春生秋杀，未尝有心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220028_comment'></div>至于子大夫自有罪，朕亦不得而私焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220028_comment'></div>具官某顷以时才，仪于要路，粤自词掖，执宪中司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220028_comment'></div>庶几肃将纪纲，以警有位，而狂言之发，乃在尔僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220028_comment'></div>事既稽于上闻，忿实由于交恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220028_comment'></div>颇失近臣之体，难逃不敏之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220028_comment'></div>免所居官，奉祠真馆，其思循省，毋重悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220028_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1220028_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。除兼侍讲。上辞免状。作品：辞免兼侍讲状。<div id='poem_1220236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼侍讲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220236")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220236'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220236'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220236_comment'></div>右，臣今月某日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣兼侍讲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220236_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220236_comment'></div>伏念臣受质庸愚，植学荒浅，不图么么，遭遇圣明，擢自稠人，寘之词掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220236_comment'></div>过越分量，愧心腼颜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220236_comment'></div>俾侍经帏，岂其素望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220236_comment'></div>仰惟陛下禀聪明睿智之性，有缉熙光明之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220236_comment'></div>其臣莫及，疏观五帝之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220236_comment'></div>厥修乃来，超视三王之懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220236_comment'></div>而臣乃以固陋，承乏露门，自视歉然，将焉称此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220236_comment'></div>矧臣年龄颓暮，志意凋零，记忆疏阔，得首遗尾，如令冒处，宁免讥嘲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220236_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣悃愊，追还成命，改授能臣，庶穆公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220236_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220236_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1220236_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。行楼炤兼侍读制。作品：楼炤除兼侍读。<div id='poem_1220048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楼炤除兼侍读制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220048")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220048'>敕：朕长育英才，寘之华近，将使左右前后，罔匪正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220048_comment'></div>从容帷幄之间，䌷绎圣贤之蕴，谓天下之乐，无以加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220048_comment'></div>具官某该贯六经，沈涵百氏，渊源所自，不愧古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220048_comment'></div>仰惟祖宗，垂裕后嗣，具存谟训，奉以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220048_comment'></div>爰资诵说之明，以发见闻之蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220048_comment'></div>益者三友，非汝而谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220048_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220048_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月21日</a>　在临安。行楼炤除端明殿学士签书枢密院事制。<div id='poem_1220063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楼炤除端明殿学士签书枢密院事制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年3月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220063")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220063'>敕：天武地文，所以妙生成之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220063_comment'></div>左仁右义，所以行威德之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220063_comment'></div>深惟拨乱之原，实在本兵之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220063_comment'></div>体隆参伍，位亚疑丞，敷求得人，兹朕有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220063_comment'></div>具官某惇大笃实，疏通敏明，学博古而通今，气绝群而迈往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220063_comment'></div>蹈履圣贤之域，从容礼义之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220063_comment'></div>大册高文，悉出其手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220063_comment'></div>崇论宏议，有补于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220063_comment'></div>力佐中兴，功居大半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220063_comment'></div>蔽自朕志，申锡赉书，爰升秘殿之华，进贰枢廷之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220063_comment'></div>并加徽数，庸示宠私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220063_comment'></div>噫，留公在朝，已觉强藩之悔过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220063_comment'></div>干木为政，岂止诸侯之息兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220063_comment'></div>尚殚不贰之谋，以永无穷之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220063_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月21日</a>　在临安。行楼炤除端明殿学士签书枢密院事封赠三代并妻制。作品：签书枢密院事楼炤封赠三代并妻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年4月10日</a>　在临安。行李纲知潭州制。作品：李纲知潭州兼安抚大使制。<div id='poem_1220037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李纲知潭州兼安抚大使制<span class='inlineComment2'>（改除宫祠）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220037")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220037'>敕：入总百揆，作股肱耳目之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220037_comment'></div>出殿大邦，号礼乐诗书之帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220037_comment'></div>任是安危之责，孰踰耆旧之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220037_comment'></div>具官某识洞几微，气全英特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220037_comment'></div>修身自昔，非孔孟之言不师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220037_comment'></div>许国以来，惟伊吕之心是志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220037_comment'></div>屡展经纶之学，寔兼文武之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220037_comment'></div>忼慨百为，夷险一意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220037_comment'></div>方且辞功名而不有，占薮泽以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220037_comment'></div>未忘忧国之风，忍袖济时之手？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220037_comment'></div>眷长沙之巨屏，居南纪之上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220037_comment'></div>地控荆湘，势临吴楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220037_comment'></div>惟威声之先暨，奸慝自消；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220037_comment'></div>矧条教之旧孚，歌谣犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220037_comment'></div>淮扬之徒得君重，其勿留行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220037_comment'></div>方叔之克壮其猷，岂能无望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220037_comment'></div>祗服朕训，有光前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220037_comment'></div>可。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1220037'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年4月19日</a>　在临安。行俞俟知扬州制。<div id='poem_1220102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>俞俟知扬州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220102")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220102'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220102'>敕具官某：广陵斗牛之枢，地控淮海，为一都会，自昔守臣，有连率之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220102_comment'></div>以尔屡试烦剧，才具有馀，吏畏其明，民怀其惠，肆以命汝，盖不惟其官惟其人之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220102_comment'></div>尔其布宣德泽，拊其凋瘵，使一方安尔之政，则为称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220102_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1220102_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年4月</a>　在临安。吕颐浩卒，有代祭文。作品：代祭吕丞相文。<div id='poem_1220410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代祭吕丞相文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220410")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220410'>维师尚父，太岳之裔，相彼武王，于燮伐事，光昭后人，克绍厥懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220410_comment'></div>惟公之生，英特伟异，心雄万夫，身兼数器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220410_comment'></div>拳拳爱君，曾靡敢易，天固异之，其必有意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220410_comment'></div>公实自以，遭遇不世，义所当为，九殉勿避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220410_comment'></div>帝嘉乃绩，社稷是利，谓督不忘，俾践厥位，再持魁柄，埏埴品汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220410_comment'></div>慨时艰难，志等外内，出入将相，文武兼备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220410_comment'></div>命圭崇崇，赤舄几几，秉旄仗钺，富贵始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220410_comment'></div>天子有命，公实至止，分陕之重，将公自倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220410_comment'></div>俄以病告，勿克入侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220410_comment'></div>我时视公，尚能强起，顾瞻精爽，何患不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220410_comment'></div>讵公之归，阅日未几，遽闻讣音，失声叹喟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220410_comment'></div>乔岳峰摧，壑舟夜逝，我不意公，而乃至是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220410_comment'></div>溯风永怀，泪溢两眦，奠此一觞，尚公不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220410_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1220410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年5月1日</a>　在临安。上书请诸县置仓窖入粟。后于嘉泰四年五月诸县置仓。作品：转对奏状。<div id='poem_1220246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>转对奏状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴乙未）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220246")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220246'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220246'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220246_comment'></div>准御史台牒，五月一日视朝，轮当转对，今具己见，须知奏闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220246_comment'></div>右，臣窃惟义仓之法，论始于隋，增广于唐，而国朝因焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220246_comment'></div>其意若曰，古者三年耕必有一年之蓄，九年耕必有三年之蓄，国无三年之蓄，则国非其国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220246_comment'></div>当其丰登，粒米狼戾，俾输其馀，以备凶荒，未为过举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220246_comment'></div>不幸有金穰水毁木饥火旱之变，则用其私蓄，固足以赈之，社仓是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220246_comment'></div>隋开皇间长孙平请令诸州百姓劝课，因社共立义仓，收穫之日，各出粟麦藏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220246_comment'></div>社司职长检校多少，岁或不登，则发以赈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220246_comment'></div>然立法犹未备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220246_comment'></div>至唐贞观间，戴胄请自王公以下爰及众庶，计所垦田稼穑亩顷，每至秋熟，以理劝课，尽令出粟，各于所在为立义仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220246_comment'></div>国朝乾德间，天子哀岁之不登，而仓吏不以时出与民，于是著发粟之制，使不待诏令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220246_comment'></div>其后病吏之烦扰，而民罹转输之困，又罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220246_comment'></div>至仁宗皇帝始复旧制，民到于今赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220246_comment'></div>然而推行之意有未尽合于古者，岂得不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220246_comment'></div>且所谓义仓者，取粟于民，还以赈之，固不可以不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220246_comment'></div>今也置仓入粟，正在州郡，岁饥散给，而山泽僻远之民，往往不沾其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220246_comment'></div>其力能赴州就食者盖亦鲜少，而况所得不足偿劳，流离颠沛，有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220246_comment'></div>此岂社仓之本意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220246_comment'></div>恭惟陛下天慈广覆，一视同仁，凡政事系赤子之利害者，见于诏令，丁宁熟复，靡有不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220246_comment'></div>而奉法之吏，因习故常，惮于改为，使上之德泽不克下究，臣窃惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220246_comment'></div>臣愚以谓义仓之粟，当于本县乡村多置仓窖，自始入粟，以及散给，悉在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220246_comment'></div>大县七八处，小县三四处，远近分布，俾适厥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220246_comment'></div>若未有仓窖，则寄寺观或大姓之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220246_comment'></div>县令总其凡，以时检校，遇饥馑时丞簿尉等分行乡村，计口给历，次第支散，旬一周之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220246_comment'></div>庶几僻处之民，均受其赐，不复弃家流转道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220246_comment'></div>此利害之较然者也，伏望圣慈下臣议，更赐详酌，傥以为可，断而行之，不胜厚幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220246_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1220246_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年5月1日</a>　在临安。行张浚辞免知福州制。作品：赐张浚辞免知福州不允诏制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年5月1日</a>　在临安。行张浚再辞免知福州制。作品：赐张浚再辞免知福州不允诏。<div id='poem_1220211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐张浚再辞免知福州不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220211")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220211'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220211'>敕张浚<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>：具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220211_comment'></div>朕惟长乐，为今名区，分阃之严，盖畴宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220211_comment'></div>卿以出将入相之器，席经文纬武之才，分朕顾忧，佥言惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220211_comment'></div>矧山川胜丽，未减昔游，饰版舆以奉亲，凭熊轼以问俗，为卿择地，无以加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220211_comment'></div>兹荐览于来章，似未孚于至意，往其祗服，勿复有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220211_comment'></div>所请宜不允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1220211_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年5月5日</a>　在临安。行周葵殿中侍御史制。<div id='poem_1220123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周葵殿中侍御史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220123")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220123'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220123'>敕具官某：治疾以苦口之药，疾已而药可捐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220123_comment'></div>治身以苦口之言，身修而言有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220123_comment'></div>君子以是知言之不可忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220123_comment'></div>尔顷以文行为朕识擢，既居御史，知无不言，言皆有益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220123_comment'></div>比其去也，朕心思焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220123_comment'></div>兹用诏除，复畀言路，上有仳政，朕所乐闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220123_comment'></div>吏之多奸，惟尔勿贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220123_comment'></div>但朕以治己之道治人，君子进为，小人退听，天下蒙福，其庶几乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220123_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1220123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年6月14日</a>　在临安。谏罢汪伯彦给俸。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年8月13日</a>　在临安。行周葵试起居郎制。作品：周葵起居郎制。<div id='poem_1220194' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220194' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220194?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周葵起居郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年8月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220194")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220194_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220194'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220194'>敕：左史载笔，职在记动，进直螭陛，退居鸾台，是惟儒者一时之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220194_comment'></div>以尔葵执德清夷，秉心端亮，两居御史，风节凛然，有藜藿不采之风，见松柏后凋之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220194_comment'></div>引以自近，益观厥猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220194_comment'></div>我乃正心，尔无曲笔，庶几终誉，不愧前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220194_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1220194_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。连入疏论程瑀忠信可以备献纳，正直可以司风宪，应在朝列，不宜去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年9月7日</a>　在临安。迁给事中，仍兼侍讲。上辞免状。作品：辞免给事中状。<div id='poem_1220237' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220237' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220237?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免给事中状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220237")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220237'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220237'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220237_comment'></div>右，臣今月某日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣给事中，依旧兼侍讲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220237_comment'></div>闻命震惧，不知所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220237_comment'></div>伏念臣出自寒乡，本无学术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220237_comment'></div>遭遇上圣，起于閒废之中，曾未淹时，遂参法从代言之选，从古所难，臣不自量，谬当其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220237_comment'></div>文辞骫骳，不足以追深厚之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220237_comment'></div>智识疏阔，不足以效讨论之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220237_comment'></div>理应汰斥，复玷序迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220237_comment'></div>矧东台号出纳之司，而给事以封驳为职，处之失当，有害政体，则名器之重，自臣而轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220237_comment'></div>冒昧居之，何施颜腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220237_comment'></div>伏望天地之德，猥赐曲成，察臣忱辞，追还误宠，则臣有知难之义，朝无虚授之讥，两义俱安，师言惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220237_comment'></div>所有告命，未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220237_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1220237_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年9月7日</a>　在临安。迁给事中，仍兼侍讲。上谢表。作品：谢除给事中表。<div id='poem_1220251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除给事中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220251")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220251'>宠锡自天，恳辞无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220251_comment'></div>祗拜莫回之命，俯惭未报之恩，惊惧交营，周张失次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220251_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣少非特立，老不自强，谓当静退之年，无复进为之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220251_comment'></div>不图晚遇，乃玷误知，持橐近班，代言西掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220251_comment'></div>正上圣作兴之日，躬万几总揽之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220251_comment'></div>与禁省之腹心，而臣乏谟猷之益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220251_comment'></div>窃训辞之手笔，而臣无润色之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220251_comment'></div>思轧轧其如抽，心摇摇而若失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220251_comment'></div>宜在黜幽之域，更叨躐等之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220251_comment'></div>矧是东台，最为要地，号人才进退之关键，为王命出纳之咽喉，岂容迂疏，膺此责任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220251_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下皇明广被，英断独成，宏开复古之规，克尽官人之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220251_comment'></div>长材成厦，未忘朴遫之兼收；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220251_comment'></div>众骏在闲，尚意疲驽之可勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220251_comment'></div>敢不激昂末路，殚竭谀闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220251_comment'></div>躯命几何，顾无益丘山之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220251_comment'></div>飞鸣自誓，庶少偿乌鸟之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1220251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年9月7日</a>　在临安。荐吕广问、徐康。作品：举吕广问徐康状。<div id='poem_1220244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举吕广问徐康状<span class='inlineComment2'>（任给事中日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220244")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220244'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220244'>具位臣刘某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220244_comment'></div>准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，令行在侍从官各举所知二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220244_comment'></div>臣恭依圣旨选举到官，具列于左，须至奏闻者：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1220244'>一、左宣教郎吕广问文行粹美，论议高明，胸有所存，实有治具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220244_comment'></div>流寓岁久，守道安贫，鲜见其比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220244_comment'></div>尝蒙朝廷召试馆职，不报，寻出补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220244_comment'></div>前后历任，职业甚修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220244_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1220244'>一、右奉议郎、提举两浙西路茶盐公事徐康性行冲粹，学识淹通，论辨古今，悉有依据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220244_comment'></div>虽以蒙朝廷擢为使者，用建所长，未究施设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220244_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1220244'>右件二人，实臣所知，兼采舆议，傥蒙录用，必有可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220244_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌，付外施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220244_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年11月16日</a>　在临安。刘一止奏潘正夫、孟忠厚、徐伟达事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。任给事中百许日，缴奏未己。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年12月29日</a>　在临安。被忌落职，提举江州太平观。上谢表。作品：谢授提举江州太平观表。<div id='poem_1220252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授提举江州太平观表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220252")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220252'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220252'>罪大责轻，感深涕殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220252_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣浅闻单见，极陋至愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220252_comment'></div>受知殆阅于十年，冒宠浸更于两禁，不量弱植，滥据要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220252_comment'></div>属上圣之思贤，戒迩臣而举类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220252_comment'></div>而臣栖幽居之日久，识中原之士希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220252_comment'></div>智实昧于是非，迹遂成于乖缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220252_comment'></div>揆其重负，合寘严辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220252_comment'></div>止削从班，俾安散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220252_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下励精致化，加惠臣工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220252_comment'></div>若天地之含生，心不私于与夺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220252_comment'></div>犹父母之怒子，教终厚于谴呵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220252_comment'></div>遂以庸材，蒙此善贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220252_comment'></div>再念臣赋命蹇薄，如出仇谋，偶世阔疏，率与祸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220252_comment'></div>知非晚节，既踰蘧氏之年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220252_comment'></div>受罚閒身，尚窃侏儒之饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220252_comment'></div>念报恩之无所，嗟视荫其几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220252_comment'></div>惟有腼颜，至于没齿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1220252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。叔父刘拱卒，刘一止有挽诗。作品：叔父朝请挽诗二首。<div id='poem_529356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叔父朝请挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529356")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529356'>厉节冰霜似，摛辞锦绣如。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529356'>诚心惟济物，老眼更便书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529356'>备养今谁及，辞荣计未疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529356'>郎君官已重，门户合关渠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529356'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529356_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529357?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529357'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529357'>四纪儒林誉，谈经我一门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529357'>那知诗礼学，晚失父师尊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529357'>阡陌南阳旧，松杉厚夜温。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529357'>心摧寒日落，泪尽晚云昏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529357'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。叔父刘拱卒，刘一止有墓志铭。作品：叔父朝请墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叔父朝请墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220381")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220381'>刘氏出自祁姓，陶唐氏之子孙曰刘累者，以扰龙事夏孔甲为御龙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220381_comment'></div>自商历周为豕韦，为唐杜，在晋为士，在秦为刘，后徙魏徙丰，曰丰公者名仁，汉高帝祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220381_comment'></div>汉子孙多受封，曰彭城、曰中山、曰京兆、曰丹阳，与高平、东海、长沙、平原、广陵、南康、范阳、宣城等郡皆所封之地，子孙家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220381_comment'></div>惟彭城由高祖六世孙、宣帝之子曰楚孝王嚣者实始受封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220381_comment'></div>后汉司空恺，嚣之四世孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220381_comment'></div>晋司隶校尉讷，恺之六世孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220381_comment'></div>其裔孙德威为唐刑部尚书，生审礼，封彭城公，子孙以文学政事名于时，如知章、知几辈，不可槩举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220381_comment'></div>公之先实自彭城，五代时避乱徙吴兴，迹晦不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220381_comment'></div>其名称有闻与坟墓存焉者，讳权、讳润、讳泰、讳昈、讳逢，至公为六世云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220381_comment'></div>公讳拱，字持道，实为郡之归安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220381_comment'></div>祖以伯父杂端讳述累赠至尚书刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220381_comment'></div>祖妣吴氏，濮阳郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220381_comment'></div>父任，太子中允，以兄朝议讳损及公前后累赠至光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220381_comment'></div>母吴氏，新安郡夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220381_comment'></div>前母吴氏，信安郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220381_comment'></div>公生五岁而孤，杂端公为择师教焉，嗜学自立，不类儿童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220381_comment'></div>弱冠，荐名乡书，乡先生秘丞朱公临见而异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220381_comment'></div>谏大夫陈公瓘幼为郡从事教授诸生，时郡学肄业数百人，一小较艺，以公为第一，且相器重，俾领袖学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220381_comment'></div>凡与计偕者三，试于礼部者六，卒不得一第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220381_comment'></div>崇宁五年春，以特奏名授汀州文学，时年五十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220381_comment'></div>大观二年冬，调汉阳军汉阳县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220381_comment'></div>任满，以捕寇赏改承务郎，转承事郎，授密州高密县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220381_comment'></div>未几，就除通判饶州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220381_comment'></div>终更造朝，除监明州船场，未赴，改授通判严州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220381_comment'></div>阅岁乞闲，除主管亳州明道宫、江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220381_comment'></div>绍兴五年，公第三子宁止任权尚书户部侍郎，公自以再世服官，率不过刺史郡守，今子为侍从，分当知足，遂告老于朝，自承事郎以年老致仕，及遇渊圣皇帝、今皇帝即位，霈泽序迁，明堂礼成，宁止初除徽猷阁直学士恩封，凡八转至右朝请郎、赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220381_comment'></div>在汉阳时，太守游公酢雅闻公名，礼遇甚厚，且荐之于朝，不果召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220381_comment'></div>高密令黩货紊法，公数与争，民赖以不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220381_comment'></div>其后令以贪败，辞连僚佐，公独无所与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220381_comment'></div>鄱阳岁潦，谷贵流亡相望，公摄郡事，营屋庐、发廪粟居养之，全活以万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220381_comment'></div>朝廷得民谣，下使者问状，公数以职事忤使者，匿勿以闻，公未尝有愠色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220381_comment'></div>时兴崇老氏教，其徒颇肆，郡僧有得废观为寺者，缮葺殆数十年，至是夺之，既又欲并得后所薤产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220381_comment'></div>使者以朝命属公，有顾望意，公曰：「我不敢私」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220381_comment'></div>卒沮止之，后人更定，无能易公议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220381_comment'></div>其守道不回类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220381_comment'></div>绍兴九年二月某甲子终于嘉禾郡舍，寿八十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220381_comment'></div>以其年九月丙午葬于乌程县澄静乡郎村某山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220381_comment'></div>配真氏，赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220381_comment'></div>男四人：恭止，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220381_comment'></div>勤止，右从政郎、江淮荆浙闽广路经制发运司主管文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220381_comment'></div>宁止，徽猷阁直学士、左奉议郎、提举江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220381_comment'></div>爰止，右迪功郎、监潭州南岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220381_comment'></div>女一人，适右迪功郎、监通州支盐仓江寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220381_comment'></div>孙男九人，岩、嵫、嶷、峣、嵎、峻、峋、岧、。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220381_comment'></div>孙女八人，长适右迪功郎、临安府临安县主簿范寿卿，次适进士陈如雪，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220381_comment'></div>公惟质直，不为表暴，乐道人之善若己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220381_comment'></div>于书无所不读，自始学至老且病，未尝一日废卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220381_comment'></div>所论著多，尤工于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220381_comment'></div>后进经公指教者，无虑数十辈，皆能有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220381_comment'></div>政和间，公三子宾于太学，悉以文称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220381_comment'></div>宁止射策廷中，极论时政阙失，无所讳避，天子嘉之，擢居甲科，名闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220381_comment'></div>由天禄阁、尚书郎为监司郡守，入居法从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220381_comment'></div>率迎公之官，安舆往来，左右就养，颐指无阙，远近歆艳，以为教忠之报宜有此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220381_comment'></div>晚岁康宁，视听言动如中年时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220381_comment'></div>一日语家人曰：「吾大数垂尽，自此不过两旬浃耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220381_comment'></div>宁止方守嘉禾，怪其语无从，亟上疏乞奉祠以归，比得请，则公疾革矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220381_comment'></div>真氏楚之山阳人，赠金紫光禄大夫锴之曾孙，赠通议大夫晃之孙，故进士元矩之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220381_comment'></div>以贤行闻于乡闾，奉祭祀、教子孙率有规则、相其夫以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220381_comment'></div>先公十四年卒，盖靖康改元三月某甲子也，享年六十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220381_comment'></div>公葬，乃从安人之兆，至是合祔云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220381_comment'></div>公于某为叔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220381_comment'></div>某从叔父学，粤自少时，负笈游京师，与居里间，自念其孤，侍叔父之日为最多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220381_comment'></div>岁时举酒寿叔父，喜溢于色，已而感焉，则仰视怅怅，惟恐泣之缘睫而堕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220381_comment'></div>今叔父复弃诸孤，某老矣，苟生奚为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220381_comment'></div>勤止等见属以铭，所不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220381_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1220381'>呜呼公乎，学无愧于古之人，自视曰不足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220381_comment'></div>任弗克偿其志，自分为有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220381_comment'></div>至于享报之丰，虽当世所谓富贵利达者，曾莫及其髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220381_comment'></div>则夫身之遇，与有子之祸，孰少孰多，吾不知为何如也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1220381'></div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1220381_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。为莫国华作墓志铭。作品：莫国华墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莫国华墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220377")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220377'>君讳廷芬，字国华，湖州乌程人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220377_comment'></div>曾祖敌，祖抑，皆晦德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220377_comment'></div>父侗，右迪功郎、封州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220377_comment'></div>君自幼颖悟，种学积文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220377_comment'></div>未冠，入太学，与一时俊彦争名场屋间，籍籍有称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220377_comment'></div>政和六年，赐上舍出身，调单州成武主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220377_comment'></div>君初仕，属时承平久，宪纲稍疏，奸贪肆行，上下相冒籍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220377_comment'></div>会拱辅宗室子受贿觉，寻窜匿，部使者委君治，既而有所观望，欲中辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220377_comment'></div>君督捕益峻，竟狱乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220377_comment'></div>金郎令不法，为民所讼，邑人以君能竟拱狱，乞委君问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220377_comment'></div>辞连部使者，且见祷，君笑曰：「吾岂可私挠哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220377_comment'></div>卒以实闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220377_comment'></div>任满，升从政郎，授黄州黄冈县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220377_comment'></div>以父忧去官，哀毁尽礼，乡里称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220377_comment'></div>既免丧，十年不赴调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220377_comment'></div>或勉之，则曰：「仕本为亲，吾忍死至是，尚何求」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220377_comment'></div>族父大卿公哀其志，以泽逮泉壤感之，君勉出，调平江府录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220377_comment'></div>因自喜曰：「此吾尽心之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220377_comment'></div>夫狱，人命所系，死者不可复生，事至重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220377_comment'></div>而典狱之官，贪者顾金钱，巧者弄文法，至其谨厚廉洁者，又常患不通事情，混然无章，听以一律，甚者权移吏胥，揽成案书名而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220377_comment'></div>向我摄治某事，颇自谓无愧，今真为狱官矣，其不敢不尽心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220377_comment'></div>每夜分录囚，事无巨细，躬自讯鞫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220377_comment'></div>有葛十者盗葛亮告身，至三迁其官，犯法下吏，更二狱不承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220377_comment'></div>廷尉檄君治，一见得情，叩头伏罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220377_comment'></div>君明敏绝人，而济之以恕，视食饮之节，不加楚毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220377_comment'></div>强盗因死，二人将即刑，谓狱吏曰：「令我谢录事而死」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220377_comment'></div>其不冤可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220377_comment'></div>朝廷遣使宣谕江浙，使者以事属君，君条画尽公，不当其意，怒见于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220377_comment'></div>既乃省文书，得君廉谨状，叹曰：「吾几失此人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220377_comment'></div>车驾巡幸，以应办肃给迁文林郎，终更用荐改宣教郎，授常州宜兴县丞，待次里间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220377_comment'></div>绍兴九年某月甲子以疾终于正寝，享年四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220377_comment'></div>君初得疾，遽乞致仕，愿以恩追贲其父，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220377_comment'></div>诸孤以某年十一月甲子葬于归安县至孝乡施渚方山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220377_comment'></div>娶吴氏，先君七年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220377_comment'></div>男四人，澈、测、浚、潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220377_comment'></div>澈早亡，浚中八年进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220377_comment'></div>女一人，适右迪功郎沈正邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220377_comment'></div>孙男二人，杞、棣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220377_comment'></div>孙女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220377_comment'></div>君之在母，司理梦异人授梵僧像，既寤而君生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220377_comment'></div>生性冲淡，于物无所甚好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220377_comment'></div>自居父丧，多读浮屠氏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220377_comment'></div>一日，得色空之说于梦寐间，有契于心，作为诗颂，辞旨超诣，不类畴昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220377_comment'></div>屏嗜欲，薄声利，官舍萧条，惟一仆自随，人知其宿值有异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220377_comment'></div>然于世故所当为者，未尝不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220377_comment'></div>遇宗族以恩，与人交以信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220377_comment'></div>平居慈祥，尝恐一语伤人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220377_comment'></div>至临事毅然守正，不随俗俯仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220377_comment'></div>军兴以来，衣冠流离，有急叩门，无爱吝意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220377_comment'></div>资遣幼妹，为择良婿，踰于己女，闻者义之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220377_comment'></div>晚教子甚笃，所与习业，必时之名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220377_comment'></div>亲戚子弟有来学者，亦谆谆焉诲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220377_comment'></div>浚遂以弱冠登科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220377_comment'></div>君虽不遇，实有以慰其心者，为善之报，岂偶然也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220377_comment'></div>君于余为姻家，而余与君游始自乡拔，时余壮而君尚少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220377_comment'></div>或谓余：「莫子循循寡笑，子言□则有当，其重厚如老成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220377_comment'></div>吾不忧其失德，而惧其不克年也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220377_comment'></div>今不幸而信，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220377_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1220377'>君自弱龄，实富于艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220377_comment'></div>于彼西廱，得隽屡试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220377_comment'></div>仕不苟全，志行砥砺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220377_comment'></div>奸贪病民，横肆齧噬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220377_comment'></div>堕于宪网，百不一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220377_comment'></div>我岂忘怒，覆出可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220377_comment'></div>惟法之公，何惮大吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220377_comment'></div>惨彼犴狱，人命所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220377_comment'></div>鞫讯弗躬，枉直倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220377_comment'></div>我心泓澄，如水在器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220377_comment'></div>辞见情得，曾莫骫骳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220377_comment'></div>惟君之生，在母有异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220377_comment'></div>见色明空，悉感梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220377_comment'></div>眇现世间，福不盈地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220377_comment'></div>谓生若浮，何有声利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1220377_comment'></div>君虽位卑，其得超诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1220377_comment'></div>我作铭诗，以诏来裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1220377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在临安。为杨存中祖母作墓志铭。作品：宋故恩平郡夫人刘氏墓碑。<div id='poem_1220374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故恩平郡夫人刘氏墓碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220374")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220374'>绍兴八年冬，某待罪史官，执笔螭陛，而殿帅杨公每相遇于东庑下，意色款款，不相配夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220374_comment'></div>明年春，见语曰：「存中逮事祖母恩平郡夫人，蒙教育之恩甚厚，葬十年矣，而碑铭未立，私心恧焉，敢以累子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220374_comment'></div>某曰：「公家世忠孝，闻于三晋，而公复以勋绩被宠遇，致位通显，益大厥家，其继述先懿宜有人，顾安取此」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220374_comment'></div>然不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220374_comment'></div>既而观夫人行实，而感《周南》之诗，妇人能勉其君子以正，字应书法，谨叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220374_comment'></div>夫人姓刘氏，其先居相台，后徙开封，遂为封人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220374_comment'></div>祖斌事真宗朝，久宿卫五边功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220374_comment'></div>一日，以偏裨从大将北征，会天晦冥失道，至北海，有老人持舟渡之，且授以乳香，云：「服此可不食」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220374_comment'></div>皇祐中，从狄武襄公征侬智高有功，迁澶州总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220374_comment'></div>卒，赠太保，敕葬开封之沙台，号「吃香刘太保」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220374_comment'></div>父居易守忻州，终供备库副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220374_comment'></div>母王氏封寿安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220374_comment'></div>夫人，供备之长女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220374_comment'></div>自幼淑惠，供备钟爱，难其配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220374_comment'></div>永兴路步军副总管杨公宗闵初任为三班借职，供备一见与语，奇之，曰：「将帅才也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220374_comment'></div>以夫人归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220374_comment'></div>夫人之归杨氏，事姑檀夫人甚谨，侍疾不解带，不顷刻去左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220374_comment'></div>辑睦宗族，遇其下有恩，喜愠不见于色，而家事井井，皆有条理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220374_comment'></div>总管公以忠义自将，躬冒矢石，闻命引道，或不介而驱，视骨肉如路人，不少牵制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220374_comment'></div>居无事时，夫人率勉之赴公，不以私事一毫累其心，故坚决若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220374_comment'></div>夫人早遍通群书及内典，得其大旨，敏识绝人，义所当为，断然不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220374_comment'></div>朝廷之复燕山也，总管以河东第三将驻军静寨城，且沿檄武州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220374_comment'></div>时常胜军五百人实散从留静寨，官吏失职，廪无见粮，至贸衣以食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220374_comment'></div>夫人语其子霆曰：「燕人陷夷踰二百年，今始归朝，而郡县无以给其食，至冻饿，岂人情也哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220374_comment'></div>命捐私藏数百解济之，悉赖以全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220374_comment'></div>自是夫人之誉，溢于边境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220374_comment'></div>初，总管为永兴副师，金人长驱，河东郡以城降者，过予永兵河虏，俾夫人携家之属，夫人执义不从，总管曰：「吾效死于此，然不可以无后，以百口累夫人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220374_comment'></div>夫人泣涕，诀曰：「百口责在我，君无顾家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220374_comment'></div>受国深恩，无临难苟免」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220374_comment'></div>永兴陷，总管以死节闻，夫人号恸不自胜，既而曰：「我夫得其死矣，未亡人复何憾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220374_comment'></div>时道梗，多剽敚，行次成州奥亭，县尉郭先将夫人所赍厚，与盗刘敢战以兵圜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220374_comment'></div>敢战骑卒有尝隶总管麾下者，语其徒，曰：「此长安杨总管家属，无辄犯也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220374_comment'></div>众皆竦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220374_comment'></div>夫人抗声呼敢战曰：「刘侯，尔名将家子，今举义当为上帅，无久在草路，隤其家声」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220374_comment'></div>敢战盖太尉刘发之辟从也，感夫人之言，流涕再拜，请姑事夫人，且愿因夫人求受节制于成州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220374_comment'></div>夫人遣建以其情告成守，曰：「必许之，外可无寇，内益胜兵，一举而两得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220374_comment'></div>成守以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220374_comment'></div>既而僚属属曰：「杨夫人果免于难，虽古智谋之士何以加」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220374_comment'></div>至兴元，闻孙存中扈驾南巡，屡立战名，喜曰：「我孙幼不凡，固宜有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220374_comment'></div>我当犯锋镝趋行在，所冀一见而死，愿毕矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220374_comment'></div>明年冬，发二蜀，阅半岁，会存中于建康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220374_comment'></div>是秋，遽以疾终，实建炎三年八月二日也，享年六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220374_comment'></div>累封至宜人，以存中追赠恩平郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220374_comment'></div>存中以其年九月十日葬夫人于建康蒋山西草堂之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220374_comment'></div>男四人，曰震，敦武郎，靖康初知麟州建宁寨，夏人与契丹将小鞠䩮寇河东，死于贼，追赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220374_comment'></div>次曰霖，乡贡进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220374_comment'></div>次曰云，承信郎，皆早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220374_comment'></div>次曰霆，承节郎，后夫人一月卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220374_comment'></div>女三人，适乡贡进士王仲举、靳亮、何充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220374_comment'></div>孙男七人，长曰存中，殿前副虞候、保成军节度使、主管殿前司公事、武功郡开国侯、食邑一千户、实封二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1220374_comment'></div>次曰居中、执中，皆从其父死难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1220374_comment'></div>曰师中，秉义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1220374_comment'></div>曰彦中、安中、守中，皆承信郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1220374_comment'></div>孙女三人，长适乡贡进士王公宏，次未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1220374_comment'></div>曾孙三人，曰契，成忠郎、閤门祗候，曰倓、曰㒜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1220374_comment'></div>曾孙女四人在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1220374_comment'></div>呜呼，恩义相胜，平时士夫处之，称以为难，而夫人判之于仓猝扰攘之间，不失其正，名到于今，伉俪俱荣，斯亦奇矣，论者以是深数之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1220374_comment'></div>至孙鼎贵，间关东来，仅如其志，不克久受钟鼎之养，事为可矜，岂为善之报不于其身于其后人，兹可信耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1220374_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1220374'>夫人之德，式是嫔则，恭顺且直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1220374_comment'></div>以严其身，有彝有伦，壸政以振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1220374_comment'></div>允毅杨公，秉心恪志，国尔忘躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1220374_comment'></div>闻命引途，不介以驱，何有厥挐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1220374_comment'></div>夫人刘氏，克相君子，惟义所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1220374_comment'></div>生死之决，虽古猛烈，志义或蹶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1220374_comment'></div>曾是闺门，谓此断恩，慷慨以论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1220374_comment'></div>声实播闻，缙绅云云，有苾其芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1220374_comment'></div>夫人来东，孝孙之从，受养则丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1220374_comment'></div>惟时孝孙，日侍帝阍，帝顾为温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1220374_comment'></div>车服炜炜，归奉燕喜，惟其有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1220374_comment'></div>曾未更时，壑舟已移，孝孙孔悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1220374_comment'></div>惟积也厚，厥报未究，以溢我后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1220374_comment'></div>迤迤新冈，川流泱泱，庆如许长<span class='inlineComment2'>（《苕溪集》卷四八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1220374_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1220374'>「初」上，清抄本补「建炎」二字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1220374_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

德清
