class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭族兄希范资政文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220402")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220402'>惟公孕川岳之神姿，怀金玉之英华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220402_comment'></div>问学纷以钩贯，辞采蔚其纬经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220402_comment'></div>行神茂以笃实，论感激而深明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220402_comment'></div>唾掌以取富贵，俛首而拾功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220402_comment'></div>御王良而足骅骝，既决骤而长鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220402_comment'></div>方安辔以徐驱，寄万里于修龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220402_comment'></div>曷岁月之不淹，卒忧患其与并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220402_comment'></div>自他人视之，公则遇矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220402_comment'></div>若自公视，如龙泉、太阿，手持而不试，曾未足以快其生平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220402_comment'></div>斯民之望也，庶几乎为霖雨以终惠，何遽骑箕尾而自比乎列星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220402_comment'></div>惟贱子之蠢愚，席累世之宗盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220402_comment'></div>接步武于左廱，事终岁之笔耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220402_comment'></div>虽通塞之殊途，宁喜戚之异情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220402_comment'></div>望五岭之还辕，居刺促而靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220402_comment'></div>奉哀讣于不虞，泪迸散而沾缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220402_comment'></div>惊云寄之晚弦，怅覆水之不返，孰知此世之均梦，何得丧之足评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220402_comment'></div>姑酌酒以叫公，尚髣髴其音声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220402_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1220402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居德清。春，刘一止有诗次韵郑几如。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居德清。有诗悼沈与求夫人范氏。作品：沈夫人二首。<div id='poem_529375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沈夫人挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529375")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529375'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529375'>婉娩闺门秀，安贫六十春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529375'>相夫惟礼义，玩意独清真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529375'>蜀道灵归远，吴山兆卜新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529375'>哀声传北里，悽感路傍人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529375_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529375'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529375_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_529376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529376?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_529376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529376'>盛德高门阀，荣光动里间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529376'>如何<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作符）</span>偕老愿，端向此时悭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529376'>幼妇辞新刻，仙游梦莫攀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529376'>吁嗟袆翟贵，不立内朝班。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529376'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_529376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居德清。作吴公择墓志铭。<div id='poem_1220380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴公择墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220380")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220380'>绍兴二年正月甲子，吴君公择以疾终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220380_comment'></div>明年四月壬子葬于吴兴之安吉曰铜山乡俞坞之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220380_comment'></div>君之子罕过余门，累然深墨，拜且泣曰：「先子既克葬矣，隧未有铭，托子文为不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220380_comment'></div>且先子之未属纩也，驰书命罕卜归葬之地，曰必得艮山，初不言有疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220380_comment'></div>罕时摄官旁近，私心骇异，将请急以归问所以然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220380_comment'></div>未行而讣至，距遗书才十日云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220380_comment'></div>罕不敢即死者，以窀穸之故，屡卜而后得之，则如先志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220380_comment'></div>独潜德不白于后世是惧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220380_comment'></div>余于吴氏为弥甥，从游君父子间有年矣，知君宜详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220380_comment'></div>抑闻罕之葬其亲，蒙荆棘，沐风雨，躬窀穸庐舍之役，其事良苦，又闵闵焉惧其亲之名不传，察其志为可哀，余何敢以荒陋为解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220380_comment'></div>按吴氏之先事吴越钱氏，家安吉之梅溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220380_comment'></div>君大父徙乌程，实始为乌程人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220380_comment'></div>君讳某，公择其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220380_comment'></div>曾大父琰，以其子通议大夫知几累封尚书都官郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220380_comment'></div>大父惟几，父景元，德行见推，乡里称贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220380_comment'></div>母夫人周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220380_comment'></div>居士亡薄声利，乐燕闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220380_comment'></div>与贤士大夫游，治觞豆速客，几无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220380_comment'></div>年踰七十，以乐终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220380_comment'></div>君与昆弟奉承惟谨，自始及终，无纤介可恨，宗族称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220380_comment'></div>君性警敏，少嗜书，善属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220380_comment'></div>及冠，走京师，与吴俊并游场屋，虽不偶，人以为能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220380_comment'></div>丁内外艰，终丧如礼，自是绝意科举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220380_comment'></div>或勉之，则曰：「禄不逮亲矣，尚何道」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220380_comment'></div>教其子甚严，朝暮课试，不惮寒暑，故罕自初及壮无他师，艺业绝人，有称太学，再以荐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220380_comment'></div>馀子以属罕，曰：「吾惟汝之责」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220380_comment'></div>其后次子冠，亦肄业，尝与计偕，士友歆艳，以君为有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220380_comment'></div>君素不喜植产，当居士、夫人无恙时，谓不应有私财，他日昆弟析异，君不视券，不问多寡，独以所应得应易先世藏书，且将以贻后人、继前业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220380_comment'></div>既久，生理稍艰，家人辈以子孙为言，君诵疏广益过之语告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220380_comment'></div>颇好客不倦，以诗酒相娱乐，晚岁益笃，人谓有居士之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220380_comment'></div>享年六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220380_comment'></div>平居未尝有疾，一日昧爽调护，家人方进药，君曰：「少须之，吾就寝焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1220380_comment'></div>语毕已瞑目矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1220380_comment'></div>娶曹氏，生四子：宗，以倍属出疆授从事郎，调临川金溪县尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1220380_comment'></div>次宜、冠、宪，后君二十日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1220380_comment'></div>女五人，适奉议郎、无为军司录事关春、进士袁安中、莫才彦，馀二人在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1220380_comment'></div>适关莫者前亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1220380_comment'></div>孙男三人，曰述、曰大同、曰逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1220380_comment'></div>孙女五人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1220380_comment'></div>君姿貌魁伟，慷慨有气节，言识少所降屈，往往忤物，久自知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1220380_comment'></div>宣和间官吏访求花石，君所居有名木，黄封其上，且责守护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1220380_comment'></div>君曰：「主上神圣，宁复有此，盖倖臣所为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1220380_comment'></div>遂伐去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1220380_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1220380'>灵之归，铜山隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1220380_comment'></div>曰艮岑，郁不孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1220380_comment'></div>视培塿，皆仆奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1220380_comment'></div>前左泽，下统庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1220380_comment'></div>灵所欣，复当腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1220380_comment'></div>福而门，大厥初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1220380_comment'></div>谁云者，古青乌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1220380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居德清。结识临邑闻人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　居德清。年初，江端友卒，刘一止有文祭之。作品：祭江子我郎中文。<div id='poem_1220399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭江子我郎中文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220399")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220399'>呜呼子我，行如古人，而不有合于今；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220399_comment'></div>志如古人，而不克行于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220399_comment'></div>疾邪佞其如雠，欲捽辱而鞭笞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220399_comment'></div>怀胸中之不平，用申吐于其诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220399_comment'></div>自仕言之，以处士起为望郎，固非终否；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220399_comment'></div>自公言之，或以为不遇，且仕且隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220399_comment'></div>盖次山之聱牙漫浪，而太白之磊落嵚㟢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220399_comment'></div>仆始识公严滩之湄，接诗酒于逡巡，陪杖屦以遨嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220399_comment'></div>曾一别之几何，乃生死之乖暌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220399_comment'></div>虽无斗酒只鸡之约，车过而不下，则何以写吾心之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220399_comment'></div>一觞之微，匪以为重，亦庶几浇公之磥磈也，公其尚闻之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220399_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1220399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年3月24日</a>　在德清，召为尚书祠部员外郎，奉神主于温州，未行，改权发于袁州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月9日</a>　居德清期间。有诗次韵方允迪。作品：次韵方允迪秘监九日登高一首。<div id='poem_529125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵方允迪袐监九日登高一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529125")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529125'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529125'>九日意萧条，病卧如漳滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529125'>红萸起自插，黄菊兹及辰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529125'>身落芹藻间，心与鸿雁亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529125'>想见龙山游，嘲谑落帽人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529125'>眷焉<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作春坞）</span>瀛洲客，共此溪港邻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529125'>白发俱许长，清愁浩无垠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529125'>四年京华别，前事宁忍询。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529125'>国耻久未雪，愤切此逐臣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529125'>革路何时还，今谁叫穹旻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529125'>驾言写心忧，一涴<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作洗）</span>衣上尘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_529125'>扁舟羡鸱夷，举酒忆季真。<div id='poem_sentence_10_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_529125'>目极樵径风，便拟从采薪。<div id='poem_sentence_11_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_529125'>但恐嵌岩中，不著功名身。<div id='poem_sentence_12_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_529125'>报国君尚强，我拙甘长贫。<div id='poem_sentence_13_529125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_529125'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_529125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月21日</a>　在德清，为两浙东路提点刑狱公事。上谢启。作品：提点浙东刑狱谢启。<div id='poem_1220305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>提点浙东刑狱谢启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220305")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220305'>卧疾漳滨，久忘岁月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220305_comment'></div>拜恩粤部，遽见吏民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220305_comment'></div>荷宸扆之矜怜，试庙堂之记录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220305_comment'></div>事非意出，愧与惧并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220305_comment'></div>伏念某鼯技易穷，蠹书何益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220305_comment'></div>一罹罪籍，四易岁星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220305_comment'></div>惯从樵牧之游，不作轩裳之梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220305_comment'></div>孰云枯槁，更被光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220305_comment'></div>念一道之平反，系几人之休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220305_comment'></div>矧复图□荒政于不任，责未可以见塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220305_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官德全忠厚，明烛幽遐，哀庶狱之无辜，悯一夫之失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220305_comment'></div>故兹固陋，亦与使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220305_comment'></div>某敢不益广所闻，自鞭其惰，勉副责成之意，庶为报德之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220305_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1220305_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月12日</a>　居德清，加直显谟阁。有谢表。作品：谢除直显谟阁表。<div id='poem_1220248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除直显谟阁表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年闰2月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220248")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220248'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220248'>念咎洗心，三移岁律；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220248_comment'></div>典州奉使，再锡命书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220248_comment'></div>敢图延阁之华，又玷直庐之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220248_comment'></div>逡巡拜赐，跼蹐自疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220248_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣曩昔无从，遭逢特异，遽由台属，进直殿坳，独恃上圣之知，不借游谈之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220248_comment'></div>恩已隆而未报，量既过而不辞，固弱植之难安，岂疾颠之敢悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220248_comment'></div>夫何庸陋，犹在记怜，假之内阁之名，以重外台之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220248_comment'></div>宠光并及，枯槁再春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220248_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下懋成汤之宽仁，躬尧帝之神圣，兼物众智，猥及臣愚，而臣怅末路之难图，誓初心之不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220248_comment'></div>天高地厚，若为称塞之阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220248_comment'></div>人微命轻，会有縻捐之所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1220248_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰3月12日</a>　居德清，加直显谟阁。有谢宰执启。作品：除直显谟阁谢宰执启。<div id='poem_1220304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除直显谟阁谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年闰3月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220304")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220304_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220304'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220304'>阁连中禁，藏列圣之宝章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220304_comment'></div>职逮外官，盖本朝之秘选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220304_comment'></div>不图枯槁，忽被光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220304_comment'></div>闻命自疑，循躬知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220304_comment'></div>伏念某以锄耰固陋之质，躐台省清近之班，宠既厚而不辞，量已踰而莫觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220304_comment'></div>粤从废黜，自卜隐沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220304_comment'></div>更时阽危，身独安于丘壑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220304_comment'></div>在己进退，义敢怠于君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220304_comment'></div>而况阅岁者三，拜恩已再，复簉名于内阁，俾增重于外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220304_comment'></div>有何劳能，得此殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220304_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官恢垂绝仅存之直道，建久安不拔之宏规，力何啻于回天，心但知于许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220304_comment'></div>若就深于沧海，虽不择流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220304_comment'></div>顾快意于屠门，岂必得肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220304_comment'></div>仰愧生成之施，孰为称塞之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220304_comment'></div>苟未死亡，尚收寸尺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1220304_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年3月</a>　居德清。有跋题李光诗。作品：跋李尚书赠政上人三诗。<div id='poem_1220343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李尚书赠政上人三诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220343")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220343'>政上人携尚书陇西公送行三诗见示，将刻之石，俾余跋其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220343_comment'></div>陇西公胸中如水鉴，所见外物，不能以情遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220343_comment'></div>师既经题品矣，黄龙三关不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220343_comment'></div>绍兴五年三月日吴兴刘某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1220343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月1日</a>　居德清。与沈次仲、沈长卿、陈袒安同游德清纵云台，有文纪行。作品：纵云台记。<div id='poem_1220358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>纵云台记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220358")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220358'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220358'>德清盖吴兴支邑，而山水明丽清远，为他邑冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220358_comment'></div>南朝以来，曰沈氏者世有韪人，或以文雄一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220358_comment'></div>士虽少，必秀于其额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220358_comment'></div>民贫而安，力于农桑种艺渔樵之业，斗讼简少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220358_comment'></div>岩居川观，吏或似隐，故仕于此者乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220358_comment'></div>县治枕山，山岿然特高，为百里之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220358_comment'></div>问其名于长老，则无所根据，缙绅者不道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1220358_comment'></div>旧有台，下直令舍，相距仅百尺，规制甚美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1220358_comment'></div>松竹清閟之音，桃杏妖冶之容，与他名木秀蘤，分列左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1220358_comment'></div>天欲雨，云气习习生于步武襟衱之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1220358_comment'></div>今大夫沈次仲与二客燕其上，客咏韩吏部「释峤孤云纵」，以为台名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1220358_comment'></div>次仲喜，以告余，见属为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1220358_comment'></div>次仲之临是邑也，阅五晦朔矣，旦朝坐堂上受诉谍，群吏立两庑，屏息侧睨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1220358_comment'></div>次仲独即民听其事，究所以然，反复问诘，其情毕得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1220358_comment'></div>文书虽多，必尽读乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1220358_comment'></div>律身严，无毫发私，亦不受私吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1220358_comment'></div>退与寮佐休于台上，危坐剧谈，或随时觞豆，举酒相乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1220358_comment'></div>抑尝语人：「仕吾非所爱也，有不得志则弃去如传舍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1220358_comment'></div>人以其志笃而事勤，谓若将窘，而中实纵适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1220358_comment'></div>然则客之名是台有当于主人之心者，岂以云之逸为可羡，固将仰之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1220358_comment'></div>余邑寓而山栖者也，朝见云之出，暮见云之归，进退容与于太虚寥廓之中，千态万状，不自知其然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1220358_comment'></div>其于出处，亦何心哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1220358_comment'></div>余观云于此山四年矣，余年有尽，而云之朝出暮返、变化容与之状，如余所见，不知何时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1220358_comment'></div>以其无心，故能久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1220358_comment'></div>虽然次仲方仕，余方隐，迹若不同，而从容于事物之境，愈久而愈安，则或仕或隐，未始有异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1220358_comment'></div>余燕坐内观，欲忘其心，如此云之出处，未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1220358_comment'></div>次仲勉乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1220358_comment'></div>余既告焉，因为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1220358_comment'></div>次仲名造，处之缙云人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1220358_comment'></div>二客，归安沈文伯名长卿，福唐陈仲久名袒安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1220358_comment'></div>名台者文伯，题其榜者仲久，皆奇士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1220358_comment'></div>绍兴五年七月壬申，郡人刘某行简记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1220358_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月1日</a>　居德清。与沈次仲、沈长卿、陈袒安同游德清纵云台，有词纪行。作品：水调歌头（缥缈青溪畔）<div id='poem_84595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_84595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/84595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_84595")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_84595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_84595'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_84595'>缥缈青溪畔，山翠欲粘天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_84595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_84595'>纵云台上，揽风招月自何年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_84595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_84595'>新旧今逢二妙，人地一时清绝，高并两峰寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_84595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_84595'>歌发烟霏外，人在去留间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_84595_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_84595'>著方床，容老子，醉时眠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_84595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_84595'>一尊相属，高会何意此时圆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_84595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_84595'>况是古今难遇，人月竹花俱妙，曾见句中传。<div id='poem_sentence_6_84595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_84595'>不向今宵醉，忍负四婵娟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_84595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年12月10日</a>　居德清。为褚邦直印施金光明经题跋。作品：题褚氏印施金光明经后。<div id='poem_1220342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1220342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1220342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题褚氏印施金光明经后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年12月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_1220342")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1220342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1220342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1220342'>会稽褚邦直印施《大乘金光明经》，荐严二亲，用报罔极，属余题其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1220342_comment'></div>每得书，问无恙外，未尝不以为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1220342_comment'></div>余谓孝子之于亲，无所不用其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1220342_comment'></div>以为亲之德不可报者，终于不报而已，若曰必报，在一念顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1220342_comment'></div>盖以周遍十方，于光明会，王菩萨诸佛如一一亲至其前，承事供养，无空过者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1220342_comment'></div>而况此经一句一偈，一字一义，了然在目，其为庄严亦岂有量乎哉，余之言无能加损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1220342_comment'></div>绍兴五年十二月戊申，吴兴刘某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1220342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　居德清。有诗谢李光致酒。作品：谢吴兴守李端明致酒一首时寓德清。<div id='poem_529162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_529162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/529162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢吴兴守李端明致酒一首时寓德清</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24997, "宋", "刘一止", "poem_title_529162")'>刘一止</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_529162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_529162'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_529162'>孔愉庙边溪水长，石壁岩下飞泉香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_529162'>居士住此几寒暑，只见四山青又黄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_529162'>今年春雨摧麦芒，六月稻穗乾欲僵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_529162'>烦公焦劳坐黄堂，何不趣公归赞襄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_529162'>为时开阁阴与阳，不令此忧遗君王。<div id='poem_sentence_4_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_529162'>我君有如坐甑内，口顾怫郁不得骧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_529162'>公欲令我苏肺肠，白衣致酒甚沛滂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_529162'>瓶粟未空陶氏仓，得酒且到王生乡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_529162'>更招山前老漫郎<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：谓沈次律。）</span>，渠家曲柄荷可觞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_529162'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_529162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_529162'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_529162_0'>⑴ 自注：大梅山法常禅师隐居馀姚南梅子真故栖，有僧寻拄杖迷路至庵前，问师住此多少时？师云：只见四山青又黄。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_529162_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
